可得 \( {c}^{2} - {ca} - {a}^{2} = 0 \) . 于是 \( \frac{c}{a} = \frac{\sqrt{5} + 1}{2} \) .

于是 \( {b}^{2} = \frac{\sqrt{5} + 1}{2}{a}^{2},{c}^{2} = \frac{3 + \sqrt{5}}{2}{a}^{2} \) .

解得 \( \cos B = \frac{{a}^{2} + {c}^{2} - {b}^{2}}{2ac} = \frac{\sqrt{5} - 1}{2} \) .

10. 在平面直角坐标系 \( {xOy} \) 中,圆 \( \Omega \) 与抛物线 \( \Gamma  : {y}^{2} = {4x} \) 恰有一个公共点,且圆 \( \Omega \) 与 \( x \) 轴相切于 \( \Gamma \) 的焦点 \( F \) . 求圆 \( \Gamma \) 的半径.

解析 \( \frac{4\sqrt{3}}{9} \) .

设抛物线上的点为 \( A\left( {{x}_{0},{y}_{0}}\right) \) ,则该点处的切线为 \( {y}_{0}y = 2\left( {x + {x}_{0}}\right) \) ,

其法向量 \( \overrightarrow{n} = \left( {2, - {y}_{0}}\right) \)

则线段 \( {AF} \) 的中垂线为 \( \left( {{x}_{0} - 1}\right) \left( {x - \frac{{x}_{0} + 1}{2}}\right)  + {y}_{0}\left( {y - \frac{{y}_{0}}{2}}\right)  = 0 \) .

其与 \( x = 1 \) 的交点为 \( \Omega \left( {1,\frac{{\left( {x}_{0} + 1\right) }^{2}}{2{y}_{0}}}\right) \) .

向量 \( \overrightarrow{A\Omega } = \left( {1 - {x}_{0},\frac{{\left( {x}_{0} + 1\right) }^{2}}{2{y}_{0}} - {y}_{0}}\right) \) ,

由 \( \overrightarrow{A\Omega } \) 与 \( \overrightarrow{n} \) 共线解得 \( {x}_{0} = \frac{1}{3},{y}_{0} =  \pm  \frac{2}{\sqrt{3}} \) .

故 \( r = \frac{{\left( {x}_{0} + 1\right) }^{2}}{2\left| {y}_{0}\right| } = \frac{4\sqrt{3}}{9} \) .

11. 称一个复数列 \( \left\{  {z}_{n}\right\} \) 是” 有趣的”,若 \( \left| {z}_{1}\right|  = 1 \) ,且对任意正整数 \( n \) ,均有 \( 4{z}_{n + 1}^{2} + \) \( 2{z}_{n}{z}_{n + 1} + {z}_{n}^{2} = 0 \) . 求最大的常数 \( C \) ,使得对一切有趣的数列 \( \left\{  {z}_{n}\right\} \) 及任意正整数 \( m \) ,均有 \( \left| {{z}_{1} + {z}_{2} + \cdots  + {z}_{m}}\right|  \geq  C \) .

解析 \( \frac{\sqrt{3}}{3} \) .

根据题意, 有

\[{z}_{n + 1} = \frac{-1 \pm  \sqrt{3}\mathrm{i}}{4}{z}_{n} \Leftrightarrow  {z}_{n + 1} = \left( {\pm \frac{2\pi }{3} : \frac{1}{2}}\right)  \cdot  {z}_{n}.\]

记 \( {q}_{1} = \left( {\frac{2\pi }{3} : \frac{1}{2}}\right) ,{q}_{2} = \left( {-\frac{2\pi }{3} : \frac{1}{2}}\right) \) . 取 \( {z}_{1} = 1 \) ,且

\[{z}_{n + 1} = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} {q}_{1} \cdot  {z}_{n}, & 2 \nmid  n, \\  {q}_{2} \cdot  {z}_{n}, & 2 \mid  n, \end{array}\right. \]


则

\[\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{m \rightarrow   + \infty }}\left( {{z}_{1} + {z}_{2} + \cdots  + {z}_{m}}\right)  = \left( {0 : 1}\right)  + \left( {\frac{2\pi }{3} : \frac{1}{2} + \frac{1}{8} + \cdots }\right)  + \left( {-\frac{2\pi }{3} : \frac{1}{4} + \frac{1}{16} + \cdots }\right) \]

\[ = \left( {0 : 1}\right)  + \left( {\frac{2\pi }{3} : \frac{2}{3}}\right)  + \left( {-\frac{2\pi }{3} : \frac{1}{3}}\right) \]

\[ = \frac{1}{2} + \frac{\sqrt{3}}{6}\mathrm{i}\]

因此

\[\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{m \rightarrow   + \infty }}\left| {{z}_{1} + {z}_{2} + \cdots  + {z}_{m}}\right|  = \frac{\sqrt{3}}{3}.\]

接下来证明 \( C = \frac{\sqrt{3}}{3} \) 符合题意. 考虑

\[\left| {{z}_{n} + {z}_{n + 1}}\right|  = \left| {z}_{n}\right|  \cdot  \left| {1 + \frac{{z}_{n + 1}}{{z}_{n}}}\right|  = \frac{1}{{2}^{n - 1}} \cdot  \left| {1 + \left( {\pm \frac{2\pi }{3} : \frac{1}{2}}\right) }\right|  = \frac{\sqrt{3}}{{2}^{n}},\]

于是当 \( m = 1 \) 时,有 \( \left| {z}_{1}\right|  = 1 > \frac{\sqrt{3}}{3} \) ; 当 \( m \) 为偶数时,有

\[\left| {{z}_{1} + {z}_{2} + \cdots  + {z}_{m}}\right|  \geq  \left| {{z}_{1} + {z}_{2}}\right|  - \left| {{z}_{3} + {z}_{4}}\right|  - \cdots  - \left| {{z}_{m - 1} + {z}_{m}}\right| \]

\[ > \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} - \left( {\frac{\sqrt{3}}{8} + \frac{\sqrt{3}}{32} + \cdots }\right) \]

\[ = \frac{\sqrt{3}}{3},\]

当 \( m \) 为不小于 3 的奇数时,有

\[\left| {{z}_{1} + {z}_{2} + \cdots  + {z}_{m}}\right|  \geq  \left| {{z}_{1} + {z}_{2}}\right|  - \left| {{z}_{3} + {z}_{4}}\right|  - \cdots  - \left| {{z}_{m - 2} + {z}_{m - 1}}\right|  - \left| {z}_{m}\right| \]

\[ > \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} - \left( {\frac{\sqrt{3}}{8} + \frac{\sqrt{3}}{32} + \cdots  + \frac{\sqrt{3}}{{2}^{m - 2}}}\right)  - \frac{1}{{2}^{m}}\]

\[ > \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} - \left( {\frac{\sqrt{3}}{8} + \frac{\sqrt{3}}{32} + \cdots  + \frac{\sqrt{3}}{{2}^{m - 2}} + \frac{\sqrt{3}}{{2}^{m}}}\right) \]

\[ > \frac{\sqrt{3}}{3}\]

综上所述,符合题意的最大常数为 \( \frac{\sqrt{3}}{3} \) .


## 2019 年全国高中数学联赛二试答案 (A 卷)

一、如图,在锐角 \( \bigtriangleup  {ABC} \) 中, \( M \) 是 \( {BC} \) 边的中点,点 \( P \) 在 \( \bigtriangleup  {ABCC} \) 内,使得 \( {AP} \) 平分 \( \angle {BAC} \) . 直线 \( {MP} \) 与 \( \bigtriangleup {ABP},\bigtriangleup {ACP} \) 的外接圆分别相交于不同于点 \( P \) 的两点 \( D,E \) . 证明: 若 \( {DE} = {MP} \) ,则 \( {BC} = {2BP} \) .

解析

<!-- Media -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_99.jpg?x=667&y=737&w=391&h=272&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

由于 \( M \) 是中点,对 \( \bigtriangleup {PBC} \) 有 \( \frac{BP}{CP} = \frac{\sin \angle {BPM}}{\sin \angle {CPM}} \) .

而对 \( \bigtriangleup {BDP} \) 由正弦定理有 \( \frac{BP}{\sin \angle {BDP}} = \frac{BD}{\sin \angle {BPD}} \) .

同理也有 \( \frac{CE}{\sin \angle {CPE}} = \frac{CP}{\sin \angle {CEP}} \) .

故由 \( \angle {BDP} = \angle {BAP} = \angle {CAP} = \angle {CEP} \) 有 \( {BD} = {BP} \cdot  \frac{\sin \angle {BPD}}{\sin \angle {BDP}} = {CP} \) . \( \frac{\sin \angle {CPM}}{\sin \angle {BPM}} \cdot  \frac{\sin \angle {BPD}}{\sin \angle {BDP}} = {CP} \cdot  \frac{\sin \angle {CPE}}{\sin \angle {CEP}} = {CE} \)

于是由 \( \angle {BDP} = \angle {CEM} \) 且有条件可知 \( {DE} = {MP} \) ,我们有 \( \bigtriangleup {BDP} \cong  \bigtriangleup {CEM} \) ,即 \( {BP} = {CM} \) . 故 \( {BC} = {2BP} \) .

二、 设整数 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},\cdots ,{a}_{2019} \) 满足 \( 1 = {a}_{1} \leq  {a}_{2} \leq  \cdots  \leq  {a}_{2019} = {99} \) .

记 \( f = \left( {{a}_{1}^{2} + {a}_{2}^{2} + \cdots  + {a}_{2019}^{2}}\right)  - \left( {{a}_{1}{a}_{3} + {a}_{2}{a}_{4} + {a}_{3}{a}_{5} + \cdots  + {a}_{2017}{a}_{2019}}\right) \) .

求 \( f \) 的最小值 \( {f}_{0} \) . 并确定使 \( f = {f}_{0} \) 成立的数组 \( \left( {{a}_{1},{a}_{2},\cdots ,{a}_{2019}}\right) \) 的个数.

解析


\[f = \frac{1}{2}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{{2017}}{\left( {a}_{i} - {a}_{i + 2}\right) }^{2} + \frac{{a}_{1}^{2}}{2} + \frac{{a}_{2}^{2}}{2} + \frac{{a}_{2018}^{2}}{2} + \frac{{a}_{2019}^{2}}{2}\]

\[ \geq  \frac{1}{2}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{{2015}}{\left( {a}_{i} - {a}_{i + 2}\right) }^{2} + \frac{{\left( {a}_{2016} - {a}_{2017}\right) }^{2}}{2} + \frac{{\left( {a}_{2017} - {a}_{2019}\right) }^{2}}{2} + \frac{{a}_{2}^{2}}{2} + \frac{{a}_{2017}^{2}}{2} + {4901}\]

\[\text{(因为}{a}_{2017} \leq  {a}_{2018}\text{)}\]

\[ \geq  \frac{1}{2}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{{2015}}\left( {{a}_{i + 2} - {a}_{i}}\right)  + \frac{\left( {a}_{2017} - {a}_{2016}\right) }{2} + \frac{{\left( {a}_{2017} - {a}_{2019}\right) }^{2}}{2} + \frac{{a}_{2}^{2}}{2} + \frac{{a}_{2017}^{2}}{2} + {4901}\]

(因为整数平方大于等于自己)

\[ = {a}_{2017} - \frac{{a}_{2}}{2} - \frac{1}{2} + \frac{{\left( {a}_{2017} - {99}\right) }^{2}}{2} + \frac{{a}_{2}^{2}}{2} + \frac{{a}_{2017}^{2}}{2} + {4901}\]

\[ \geq  {a}_{2017}^{2} - {98}{a}_{2017} + {9801}\]

\[ \geq  {7400}\]

第一个不等号取等在于 \( {\left( {a}_{2016} - {a}_{2018}\right) }^{2} + {a}_{2018}^{2} = {\left( {a}_{2016} - {a}_{2017}\right) }^{2} + {a}_{2017}^{2} \) ,即我们有 \( {a}_{2018} = {a}_{2017}. \)

第二个不等号取等在于 \( {a}_{i} - {a}_{i + 2} = 0 \) 或 \( - 1\left( {1 \leq  i \leq  {2015}}\right) \) 和 \( {a}_{2016} - {a}_{2017} = 0 \) 或-1. 第三个不等号取等在于 \( {a}_{2}^{2} = {a}_{2} \) ,也是 \( {a}_{2} = 1 \) .

第四个不等号取等条件在于 \( {a}_{2017} = \frac{98}{2} = {49} \) .

所以综上, \( f \geq  {7400} \) 的取等条件是 \( {a}_{2} = 1,{a}_{2017} = {a}_{2018} = {49} \) ,而 \( {a}_{2} \) 到 \( {a}_{2017} \) 之间每两个相邻的数的差为 0 或 -1 .

所以取等的组数等于 \( {a}_{i} - {a}_{i - 2}\left( {4 \leq  i \leq  {2017}}\right) \) 和 \( {a}_{2017} - {a}_{2016} \) 中的 1 的个数.

由于这些数可以分两组:

\( 2,4,6,\ldots ,{2016},{2018} \)

\( 1,3,5,\ldots ,{2015},{2017} \)

并由于 \( {a}_{1} = {a}_{2} = 1,{a}_{2017} = {a}_{2018} = {49} \) ,所以显然对每一个 \( i \) 而言, \( {a}_{i - 1} \) 和 \( {a}_{i + 1} \) 总有一个与 \( {a}_{i} \) 相等.

故我们设 \( {a}_{i} = j\left( {1 \leq  j \leq  {49}}\right) \) 的解数为 \( {b}_{j} + 1 \) .

则 \( {b}_{j} \geq  1 \) ,且 \( {b}_{1} + \ldots  + {b}_{49} = {2018} - {49} = {1969} \) .

所以 \( \left( {{b}_{1},\ldots ,{b}_{49}}\right) \) 的解数为 \( {C}_{1968}^{48} \) ,即 \( \left( {{a}_{3},\ldots ,{a}_{2016}}\right) \) 的取法有 \( {C}_{1968}^{48} \) 种.

三、设 \( m \) 为整数, \( \left| m\right|  > 2 \) . 整数数列 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},\ldots \) 满足: \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2} \) 不全为零,且对任意正整数 \( n \) , 均有 \( {a}_{n + 2} = {a}_{n + 1} - m{a}_{n} \) .

证明: 若存在整数 \( r,s\left( {r > s \geq  2}\right) \) 使得 \( {a}_{r} = {a}_{s} = {a}_{1} \) ,则 \( r - s \geq  \left| m\right| \) .

解析

首先我们不妨设 \( \left( {{a}_{1},{a}_{2}}\right)  = 1 \) ,不然整个数列每一项都除以一个 \( \left( {{a}_{1},{a}_{2}}\right) \) 可以得到同样的结果和结论.


我们先证一个非常显然的引理.

引理: 对任意 \( {a}_{n},n \geq  3 \) ,我们都可以将 \( {a}_{n} \) 写成 \( {a}_{n} = {k}_{n}{a}_{2} + {l}_{n}{a}_{1} \) ,其中 \( m \mid  {k}_{n} - 1 \) , \( m \mid  {l}_{n} \) .

引理的证明: \( {a}_{3} = {a}_{2} - m{a}_{1},{a}_{4} = {a}_{3} - m{a}_{2} = \left( {1 - m}\right) {a}_{2} - m{a}_{1} \) . 所以 \( n = 3,4 \) 时显然. 若 \( n - 2 \) 和 \( n - 1 \) 时都成立的话,则

\( {a}_{n} = {a}_{n - 1} - m{a}_{n - 2} = \left( {{k}_{n - 1} - m{k}_{n - 2}}\right) {a}_{2} + \left( {{l}_{n - 1} - m{l}_{n - 2}}\right) {a}_{1} \) 所以还是显然.

所以在模 \( m \) 的时候我们总有 \( {a}_{n} \equiv  {a}_{2}\left( {\;\operatorname{mod}\;m}\right) \) ,故 \( {a}_{r} = {a}_{s} = {a}_{1} \) 就表明了 \( {a}_{2} \equiv  {a}_{1} \) \( \left( {\;\operatorname{mod}\;m}\right) \) ,由 \( \left( {{a}_{1},{a}_{2}}\right)  = 1 \) 可得 \( \left( {{a}_{1},m}\right)  = 1 \) .

那么 \( \frac{{a}_{r} - {a}_{s}}{m} = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = s + 1}}^{r}\frac{{a}_{i} - {a}_{i - 1}}{m} = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = s + 1}}^{r}{a}_{i - 2} \equiv  \left( {r - s}\right) {a}_{1}\left( {\;\operatorname{mod}\;m}\right) \)

故 \( m \mid  \left( {r - s}\right) {a}_{1} \) ,所以 \( m \mid  r - s \) . 于是 \( r - s \geq  \left| m\right| \) .

四、设 \( V \) 是空间中 2019 个点构成的集合,其中任意四点不共面. 某些点之间连有线段,记 \( E \) 为这些线段构成的集合. 试求最小的正整数 \( n \) ,满足条件: 若 \( E \) 至少有 \( n \) 个元素,则 \( E \) 一定含有 908 个二元子集,其中每个二元子集中的两条线段有公共端点,且任意两个二元子集的交为空集.

## 解析

为了叙述方便, 称一个图中的两条相邻的边构成一个 “角”.

先证明一个引理: 设 \( G = \left( {V,E}\right) \) 是一个简单图,且 \( G \) 是连通的,则 \( G \) 含有 \( \left\lbrack  \frac{\left| E\right| }{2}\right\rbrack \) 个两两无公共边的角 (这里 \( \left\lbrack  \alpha \right\rbrack \) 表示实数 \( \alpha \) 的整数部分).

引理的证明: 对 \( E \) 的元素个数 \( \left| E\right| \) 归纳证明. 当 \( \left| E\right|  = 0,1,2,3 \) 时,结论显然成立. 下面假设 \( \left| E\right|  \geq  4 \) ,并且结论在 \( \left| E\right| \) 较小时均成立.

只需证明,在 \( G \) 中可以选取两条边 \( a,b \) 构成一个角,在 \( G \) 中删去 \( a,b \) 这两条边后,剩下的图含有一个连通分支包含 \( \left| E\right|  - 2 \) 条边. 对这个连通分支应用归纳假设即得结论成立.

考虑 \( G \) 中的最长路 \( P : {v}_{1}{v}_{2}\ldots {v}_{k} \) ,其中 \( {v}_{1},{v}_{2},\ldots ,{v}_{k} \) 是互不相同的顶点. 因为 \( G \) 连通,故 \( k \geq  3 \) .

情形 1: \( \deg \left( {v}_{1}\right)  \geq  2 \) . 由于 \( P \) 是最长路, \( {v}_{1} \) 的邻点均在 \( {v}_{2},\ldots ,{v}_{k} \) 中,设 \( {v}_{1}{v}_{i} \in  E \) ,其中 \( 3 \leq  i \leq  k \) . 则 \( \left\{  {{v}_{1}{v}_{2},{v}_{1}{v}_{i}}\right\} \) 是一个角,在 \( E \) 中删去这两条边. 若 \( {v}_{1} \) 处还有第三条边, 则剩下的图是连通的: 若 \( {v}_{1} \) 处仅有被删去的两条边,则 \( {v}_{1} \) 成为孤立点,其余顶点仍互相连通. 总之在剩下的图中有一个连通分支含有 \( \left| E\right|  - 2 \) 条边.

情形 2: \( \deg \left( {v}_{1}\right)  = 1,\deg \left( {v}_{2}\right)  = 2 \) . 则 \( \left\{  {{v}_{1}{v}_{2},{v}_{2}{v}_{3}}\right\} \) 是一个角,在 \( G \) 中删去这两条边后, \( {v}_{1},{v}_{2} \) 都成为孤立点,其余的点互相连通,因此有一个连通分支含有 \( \left| E\right|  - 2 \) 条边.

情形 3: \( \deg \left( {v}_{1}\right)  = 1,\deg \left( {v}_{2}\right)  \geq  3 \) ,且 \( {v}_{2} \) 与 \( {v}_{4},\ldots ,{v}_{k} \) 中某个点相邻. 则 \( \left\{  {{v}_{1}{v}_{2},{v}_{2}{v}_{3}}\right\} \) 是一个角,在 \( G \) 中删去这两条边后, \( {v}_{1} \) 成为孤立点,其余点互相连通,因此有一个连通分支含有 \( \left| E\right|  - 2 \) 条边.

情形 4: \( \deg \left( {v}_{1}\right)  = 1,\deg \left( {v}_{2}\right)  \geq  3 \) ,且 \( {v}_{2} \) 与某个 \( u \notin  \left\{  {{v}_{1},{v}_{3},\ldots ,{v}_{k}}\right\} \) 相邻. 由于 \( P \) 是最长路,故 \( u \) 的邻点均在 \( {v}_{2},\ldots ,{v}_{k} \) 之中. 因 \( \left\{  {{v}_{1}{v}_{2},{v}_{2}u}\right\} \) 是一个角,在 \( G \) 中删去这两条边,则 \( {v}_{1} \) 是孤立点,若 \( u \) 处仅有边 \( u{v}_{2} \) ,则删去所述边后 \( u \) 也是孤立点,而其余点互相连通. 若 \( u \) 处还有其他边 \( u{v}_{i},3 \leq  i \leq  k \) ,则删去所述边后,除 \( {v}_{1} \) 外其余点互相连通,总之,剩下的图中有一个连通分支含有 \( \left| E\right|  - 2 \) 条边. 引理获证.


回到原题,题中的 \( V \) 和 \( E \) 可看作一个图 \( G = \left( {V,E}\right) \) .

首先证明 \( n \geq  {2795} \) .

设 \( V = \left\{  {{v}_{1},{v}_{2},\ldots ,{v}_{2019}}\right\} \) . 在 \( {v}_{1},{v}_{2},\ldots ,{v}_{61} \) 中,首先两两连边,再删去其中 15 条边 (例如 \( {v}_{1}{v}_{2},{v}_{1}{v}_{3},\ldots ,{v}_{1}{v}_{16} \) ),共连了 \( {C}_{61}^{2} - {15} = {1815} \) 条边,则这 61 个点构成的图是连通图. 再将剩余的 2019-61 = 1958 个点配成 979 对,每对两点之间连一条边,则图 \( G \) 中一共连了 \( {1815} + {979} = {2794} \) 条线段.

由上述构造可见, \( G \) 中的任何一个角必须使用 \( {v}_{1},{v}_{2},\ldots ,{v}_{61} \) 相连的边,因此至多有 \( \left\lbrack  \frac{1815}{2}\right\rbrack   = {907} \) 个两两无公共边的角. 故满足要求的 \( n \) 不小于 2795 . 另一方面,若 \( \left| E\right|  \geq \) 2795,可任意删去若干条边,只考虑 \( \left| E\right|  = {2795} \) 的情形. 设 \( G \) 有 \( k \) 个连通分支,分别有 \( {m}_{1},\ldots ,{m}_{k} \) 个点,及 \( {e}_{1},\ldots ,{e}_{k} \) 条边. 下面证明 \( {e}_{1},\ldots ,{e}_{k} \) 中至多有 979 个奇数.

反证法,假设 \( {e}_{1},\ldots ,{e}_{k} \) 中有至少 980 个奇数,由于 \( {e}_{1} + \ldots  + {e}_{k} = {2795} \) 是奇数,故 \( {e}_{1},\ldots ,{e}_{k} \) 中至少有 981 个奇数,故 \( k \geq  {981} \) . 不妨设 \( {e}_{1},{e}_{2},\ldots ,{e}_{981} \) 都是奇数,显然 \( {m}_{1},{m}_{2},\ldots ,{m}_{981} \geq  2 \) . 令 \( m = {m}_{981} + \ldots  + {m}_{k} \geq  2 \) . 则有 \( {C}_{{m}_{i}}^{2} \geq  {e}_{i}\left( {1 \leq  i \leq  {980}}\right) \) , \( {C}_{m}^{2} \geq  {e}_{981} + \ldots  + {e}_{k} \) ,故

\[{2795} = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{k}{e}_{i} \leq  {C}_{m}^{2} + \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{{980}}{C}_{{m}_{i}}^{2}\]

利用组合数的凸性,即对 \( x \geq  y \geq  3 \) ,有 \( {C}_{x}^{2} + {C}_{y}^{2} \leq  {C}_{x + 1}^{2} + {C}_{y - 1}^{2} \) ,可知当 \( {m}_{1},\ldots ,{m}_{980},m \) 由 980 个 2 以及一个 59 构成时, \( {C}_{m}^{2} + \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{{980}}{C}_{{m}_{i}}^{2} \) 取得最大值. 于是

\[{C}_{{m}_{i}}^{2} + \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{{980}}{C}_{{m}_{i}}^{2} \leq  {C}_{59}^{2} + {980}{C}_{2}^{2} = {2691} < {2795}\]

这与前式矛盾.

从而 \( {e}_{1},\ldots ,{e}_{k} \) 中至多有 979 个奇数. 对每个连通分支应用引理,可知 \( G \) 中含有 \( N \) 个两两无公共边的角, 其中

\[N = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{k}\left\lbrack  \frac{{e}_{i}}{2}\right\rbrack   \geq  \frac{1}{2}\left( {\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{k}{e}_{i} - {979}}\right)  = \frac{1}{2}\left( {{2795} - {979}}\right)  = {908}\]

综上,所求最小的 \( n \) 是 2795.


## 2019 年全国高中数学联赛一试答案 (B 卷)

## 一、 填空题: 本大题共 8 小题, 每小题 8 分, 满分 64 分.

1. 已知实数集合 \( \{ 1,2,3,x\} \) 的最大元素等于该集合的所有元素之和,则 \( x \) 的值为_____. 解析 -3.

条件等价于 \( 1,2,3,x \) 中除最大数以外的另三个数之和为 0 . 显然 \( x < 0 \) ,从而 \( 1 + 2 + x = 0 \) , 得 \( x =  - 3 \) .

2. 若平面向量 \( \bar{a} = \left( {{2}^{m}, - 1}\right) \) 与 \( \bar{b} = \left( {{2}^{m} - 1,{2}^{m + 1}}\right) \) 垂直,其中 \( m \) 为实数,则 \( \bar{a} \) 的模为_____.

解析 \( \sqrt{10} \) .

令 \( {2}^{m} = t \) ,则 \( t > 0 \) . 条件等价于 \( t \cdot  \left( {t - 1}\right)  + \left( {-1}\right)  \cdot  {2t} = 0 \) ,解得 \( t = 3 \) . 因此 \( \bar{a} \) 的模为 \( \sqrt{{3}^{2} + {\left( -1\right) }^{2}} = \sqrt{10}. \)

3. 设 \( \alpha ,\beta  \in  \left( {0,\pi }\right) ,\cos \alpha ,\cos \beta \) 是方程 \( 5{x}^{2} - {3x} - 1 = 0 \) 的两根,则 \( \sin \alpha \sin \beta \) 的值为_____.

解析 \( \frac{\sqrt{7}}{5} \) .

由条件知 \( \cos \alpha  + \cos \beta  = \frac{3}{5},\cos \alpha \cos \beta  =  - \frac{1}{5} \) ,从而 \( {\left( \sin \alpha \sin \beta \right) }^{2} = \left( {1 - {\cos }^{2}\alpha }\right) (1 - \) \( \left. {{\cos }^{2}\beta }\right)  = 1 - {\cos }^{2}\alpha  - {\cos }^{2}\beta  + {\cos }^{2}\alpha {\cos }^{2}\beta \) \( = {\left( 1 + \cos \alpha \cos \beta \right) }^{2} - {\left( \cos \alpha  + \cos \beta \right) }^{2} = {\left( \frac{4}{5}\right) }^{2} - {\left( \frac{3}{5}\right) }^{2} = \frac{7}{25}. \)

又由 \( \alpha ,\beta  \in  \left( {0,\pi }\right) \) 知 \( \sin \alpha \sin \beta  > 0 \) ,从而 \( \sin \alpha \sin \beta  = \frac{\sqrt{7}}{5} \) .

4. 设三棱锥 \( P - {ABC} \) 满足 \( {PA} = {PB} = 3,{AB} = {BC} = {CA} = 2 \) ,则该三棱锥的体积的最大值为_____.

解析 \( \frac{2\sqrt{6}}{3} \) .

设三棱锥 \( P - {ABC} \) 的高为 \( h \) . 取 \( M \) 为棱 \( {AB} \) 的中点,则 \( h \leq  {PM} = \sqrt{{3}^{2} - {1}^{2}} = 2\sqrt{2} \) . 当平面 \( {PAB} \) 垂直于平面 \( {ABC} \) 时, \( h \) 取到最大值 \( 2\sqrt{2} \) . 此时三棱锥 \( P - {ABC} \) 的体积取到最大值 \( \frac{1}{3}{S}_{\bigtriangleup {ABC}} \cdot  2\sqrt{2} = \frac{1}{3} \cdot  \sqrt{3} \cdot  2\sqrt{2} = \frac{2\sqrt{6}}{3} \) .

5. 将 5 个数2,0,1,9,2019按任意次序排成一行,拼成一个 8 位数 (首位不为 0 ),则产生的不同的 8 位数的个数为_____.

解析 95.

易知2,0,1,9,2019的所有不以 0 为开头的排列共有 \( 4 \times  4! = {96} \) 个,其中,除了


(2,0,1,9,2019)和(2019,2,0,1,9)这两种排列对应同一个数 20192019,其余的数互不相等,因此满足条件的 8 位数的个数为 \( {96} - 1 = {95} \) .

6. 设整数 \( n > 4,{\left( x + 2\sqrt{y} - 1\right) }^{n} \) 的展开式中 \( {x}^{n - 4} \) 与 \( {xy} \) 两项的系数相等,则 \( n \) 的值为_____.

解析 51.

注意到 \( {\left( x + 2\sqrt{y} - 1\right) }^{n} = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{r = 0}}^{n}{C}_{n}^{r}{x}^{n - r}{\left( 2\sqrt{y} - 1\right) }^{r} \) .

其中 \( {x}^{n - 4} \) 项仅出现在求和指标 \( r = 4 \) 时的展开式 \( {C}_{n}^{4}{x}^{n - 4}{\left( 2\sqrt{y} - 1\right) }^{4} \) 中,其 \( {x}^{n - 4} \) 项系数为 \( {\left( -1\right) }^{4}{C}_{n}^{4} = \frac{n\left( {n - 1}\right) \left( {n - 2}\right) \left( {n - 3}\right) }{24} \) . 而 \( {xy} \) 项仅出现在求和指标 \( r = n - 1 \) 时的展开式 \( {C}_{n}^{n - 1}x{\left( 2\sqrt{y} - 1\right) }^{n - 1} \) 中,其 \( {xy} \) 项系数为 \( {C}_{n}^{n - 1}{C}_{n - 2}^{2}4 \cdot  {\left( -1\right) }^{n - 3} = {\left( -1\right) }^{n - 3}{2n}\left( {n - 1}\right) \left( {n - 2}\right) \) .

因此有 \( \frac{n\left( {n - 1}\right) \left( {n - 2}\right) \left( {n - 3}\right) }{24} = {\left( -1\right) }^{n - 3}{2n}\left( {n - 1}\right) \left( {n - 2}\right) \) . 注意到 \( n > 4 \) ,化简得 \( n - 3 = {\left( -1\right) }^{n - 3}{48} \) ,故只能是 \( n \) 为奇数且 \( n - 3 = {48} \) . 解得 \( n = {51} \) .

7. 在平面直角坐标系中,若以 \( \left( {r + 1,0}\right) \) 为圆心, \( r \) 为半径的圆上存在一点(a,b)满足 \( {b}^{2} \geq  {4a} \) ,则 \( r \) 的最小值为_____.

解析 4.

由条件知 \( {\left( a - r - 1\right) }^{2} + {b}^{2} = {r}^{2} \) ,故 \( {4a} \leq  {b}^{2} = {r}^{2} - {\left( a - r - 1\right) }^{2} = {2r}\left( {a - 1}\right)  - {\left( a - 1\right) }^{2} \) . 即 \( {a}^{2} - 2\left( {r - 1}\right) a + {2r} + 1 \leq  0 \) .

上述关于 \( a \) 的一元二次不等式有解,故判别式 \( {\left( 2\left( r - 1\right) \right) }^{2} - 4\left( {{2r} + 1}\right)  = {4r}\left( {r - 4}\right)  \geq  0 \) , 解得 \( r \geq  4 \) .

经检验,当 \( r = 4 \) 时, \( \left( {a,b}\right)  = \left( {3,2\sqrt{3}}\right) \) 满足条件. 因此 \( r \) 的最小值为 4 .

8. 设等差数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 的各项均为整数,首项 \( {a}_{1} = {2019} \) ,且对任意正整数 \( n \) ,总存在正整数 \( m \) ,使得 \( {a}_{1} + {a}_{2} + \cdots  + {a}_{n} = {a}_{m} \) . 这样的数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 的个数为_____.

解析 5.

设 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 的公差为 \( d \) . 由条件知 \( {a}_{1} + {a}_{2} = {a}_{k} \) ( \( k \) 是某个正整数),则 \( 2{a}_{1} + d = {a}_{1} + \left( {k - 1}\right) d \) , 即 \( \left( {k - 2}\right) d = {a}_{1} \) ,因此必有 \( k \neq  2 \) ,且 \( d = \frac{{a}_{1}}{k - 2} \) ,这样就有 \( {a}_{n} = {a}_{1} + \left( {n - 1}\right) d = \) \( {a}_{1} + \frac{n - 1}{k - 2}{a}_{1} \) ,而此时对任意正整数 \( n \) ,

\( {a}_{1} + {a}_{2} + \cdots  + {a}_{n} = {a}_{1}n + \frac{n\left( {n - 1}\right) }{2}d = {a}_{1} + \left( {n - 1}\right) {a}_{1} + \frac{n\left( {n - 1}\right) }{2}d = {a}_{1} + \left( {\left( {n - 1}\right) \left( {k - 2}\right)  + \frac{n\left( {n - 1}\right) }{2}}\right) d \)

确实为 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 中的一项.

因此,仅需考虑使 \( k - 2 \mid  {a}_{1} \) 成立的正整数 \( k \) 的个数. 注意到 2019 为两个素数 3 与 673

之积,易知 \( k - 2 \) 可取-1,1,3,673,2019这 5 个值,对应得到 5 个满足条件的等差数列.

## 二、 解答题：本大题共 3 小题,满分 56 分. 解答应写出文字说明、证明过程或演算步骤. 其

中第 9 题满分 16 分, 第 10、11 题满分 20 分.


9. 在椭圆 \( \Gamma \) 中, \( F \) 为一个焦点, \( A,B \) 为两个顶点. 若 \( \left| {FA}\right|  = 3,\left| {FB}\right|  = 2 \) ,求 \( \left| {AB}\right| \) 的所有可能值.

## 解析

不妨设平面直角坐标系中椭圆 \( \Gamma \) 的标准方程为 \( \frac{{x}^{2}}{{a}^{2}} + \frac{{y}^{2}}{{b}^{2}} = 1\left( {a > b > 0}\right) \) ,并记 \( c = \) \( \sqrt{{a}^{2} - {b}^{2}} \) . 由对称性,可设 \( F \) 为 \( \Gamma \) 的右焦点.

易知 \( F \) 到 \( \Gamma \) 的左顶点的距离为 \( a + c \) ,到右顶点的距离为 \( a - c \) ,到上,下顶点的距离均为 \( a \) . 分以下情况讨论:

(1) \( A,B \) 分别为左右顶点,,此时 \( a + c = 3,a - c = 2 \) ,故 \( \left| {AB}\right|  = {2a} = 5 \) (相应地, \( {b}^{2} = \left( {a + c}\right) \left( {a - c}\right)  = 6,\Gamma \) 的方程为 \( \frac{4{x}^{2}}{25} + \frac{{y}^{2}}{6} = 1 \) )

(2) \( A \) 为左顶点, \( B \) 为上顶点或下顶点,此时 \( a + c = 3,a = 2 \) ,故 \( c = 1 \) ,进而 \( {b}^{2} = {a}^{2} - {c}^{2} = 3 \) ,所以 \( \left| {AB}\right|  = \sqrt{{a}^{2} + {b}^{2}} = \sqrt{7} \) (相应的 \( \Gamma \) 的方程为 \( \frac{{x}^{2}}{4} + \frac{{y}^{2}}{3} = 1 \) )

(3) \( A \) 为上顶点或下顶点, \( B \) 为右顶点,此时 \( a = 3,a - c = 2 \) 故 \( c = 1 \) ,进而 \( {b}^{2} = \) \( {a}^{2} - {c}^{2} = 8 \) ,所以 \( \left| {AB}\right|  = \sqrt{{a}^{2} + {b}^{2}} = \sqrt{17} \) (相应的 \( \Gamma \) 的方程为 \( \frac{{x}^{2}}{9} + \frac{{y}^{2}}{8} = 1 \) ) 综上可知, \( \left| {AB}\right| \) 的所有可能值为 \( 5,\sqrt{7},\sqrt{17} \) .

10. 设 \( a,b,c \) 均大于 1,满足 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} \log a + {\log }_{b}c = 3 \\  \log b + {\log }_{a}c = 4 \end{array}\right. \) 求 \( \log a \cdot  \log c \) 的最大值.

解析

设 \( {\log }_{a} = x,{\log }_{b} = y,{\log }_{c} = z \) ,由 \( a,b,c > 1 \) 可知 \( x,y,z > 0 \) .

由条件及换底公式知 \( x + \frac{z}{y} = 3,y + \frac{z}{x} = 4 \) ,即 \( {xy} + z = {3y} = {4x} \) .

由此,令 \( x = {3t},y = {4t}\left( {t > 0}\right) \) ,则 \( z = {4x} - {xy} = {12t} - {12}{t}^{2} \) . 其中由 \( z > 0 \) 可知 \( t \in  \left( {0,1}\right) \) .

因此, 结合三元平均不等式得

\( {\log }_{a}{\log }_{c} = {xz} = {3t} \cdot  {12t}\left( {1 - t}\right)  = {18} \cdot  {t}^{2}\left( {2 - {2t}}\right)  \leq  {18} \cdot  {\left( \frac{t + t + \left( {2 - {2t}}\right) }{3}\right) }^{3} = {18} \cdot  {\left( \frac{2}{3}\right) }^{3} = \)

\( \frac{16}{3} \)

当 \( t = 2 - {2t} \) ,即 \( t = \frac{2}{3} \) (相应的 \( a,b,c \) 分别为 \( {100},{10}^{\frac{8}{3}},{10}^{\frac{8}{3}} \) ) 时, \( {\log }_{a}{\log }_{c} \) 取到最大值 \( \frac{16}{3} \) .

11. 设复数数列 \( \left\{  {z}_{n}\right\} \) 满足: \( \left| {z}_{1}\right|  = 1 \) ,且对任意正整数 \( n \) ,均有 \( 4{z}_{n + 1}^{2} + 2{z}_{n}{z}_{n + 1} + {z}_{n}^{2} = 0 \) . 证明; 对任意正整数 \( m \) ,均有 \( \left| {{z}_{1} + {z}_{2} + \cdots  + {z}_{m}}\right|  < \frac{2\sqrt{3}}{3} \) .

解析

归纳地可知 \( {z}_{n} \neq  0\left( {n \in  {\mathbb{N}}^{ * }}\right) \) ,由条件得 \( 4{\left( \frac{{z}_{n + 1}}{{z}_{n}}\right) }^{2} + 2\left( \frac{{z}_{n + 1}}{{z}_{n}}\right)  + 1 = 0\left( {n \in  {\mathbb{N}}^{ * }}\right) \)

解得 \( \frac{{z}_{n + 1}}{{z}_{n}} = \frac{-1 \pm  \sqrt{3}i}{4}\left( {n \in  {\mathbb{N}}^{ * }}\right) \)


因此 \( \frac{\left| {z}_{n + 1}\right| }{\left| {z}_{n}\right| } = \left| \frac{{z}_{n + 1}}{{z}_{n}}\right|  = \left| \frac{-1 \pm  \sqrt{3}i}{4}\right|  = \frac{1}{2} \) ,故 \( \left| {z}_{n}\right|  = \left| {z}_{1}\right|  \cdot  \frac{1}{{2}^{n - 1}} = \frac{1}{{2}^{n - 1}}\left( {n \in  {\mathbb{N}}^{ * }}\right) \) ①

进而有 \( \left| {{z}_{n} + {z}_{n + 1}}\right|  = \left| {z}_{n}\right|  \cdot  \left| {1 + \frac{{z}_{n + 1}}{{z}_{n}}}\right|  = \frac{1}{{2}^{n - 1}} \cdot  \left| \frac{3 \pm  \sqrt{3}i}{4}\right|  = \frac{\sqrt{3}}{{2}^{n}}\left( {n \in  {\mathbb{N}}^{ * }}\right) \) ②

当 \( m \) 为偶数时,设 \( m = {2s}\left( {s \in  {\mathbb{N}}^{ * }}\right) \) . 利用 ② 可得

\( \left| {{z}_{1} + {z}_{2} + \cdots  + {z}_{m}}\right|  \leq  \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{k = 1}}^{s}\left| {{z}_{{2k} - 1} + {z}_{2k}}\right|  < \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{k = 1}}^{\infty }\left| {{z}_{{2k} - 1} + {z}_{2k}}\right|  = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{k = 1}}^{\infty }\frac{\sqrt{3}}{{2}^{{2k} - 1}} = \frac{2\sqrt{3}}{3}. \)

当 \( m \) 为奇数时,设 \( m = {2s} + 1\left( {s \in  \mathbb{N}}\right) \) . 由 ①,② 可知

\( \left| {z}_{{2s} + 1}\right|  = \frac{1}{{2}^{s}} < \frac{\sqrt{3}}{3 \cdot  {2}^{{2s} - 1}} = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{k = s + 1}}^{\infty }\frac{\sqrt{3}}{{2}^{{2s} - 1}} = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{k = s + 1}}^{\infty }\left| {{z}_{{2k} - 1} + {z}_{2k}}\right| \)

故 \( \left| {{z}_{1} + {z}_{2} + \cdots  + {z}_{m}}\right|  \leq  \left( {\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{k = 1}}^{s}\left| {{z}_{{2k} - 1} + {z}_{2k}}\right| }\right)  + \left| {z}_{{2k} + 1}\right|  < \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{k = 1}}^{\infty }\left| {{z}_{{2k} - 1} + {z}_{2k}}\right|  = \frac{2\sqrt{3}}{3} \) .

综上, 结论获证.


## 2019 年全国高中数学联赛二试答案 (B 卷)

一、设正实数 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},\cdots ,{a}_{100} \) 满足 \( {a}_{i} \geq  {a}_{{101} - i}\left( {i = 1,2,\cdots ,{50}}\right) \) . 记 \( {x}_{k} = \frac{k{a}_{k + 1}}{{a}_{1} + {a}_{2} + \cdots  + {a}_{k}}(k = \)

\( 1,2,\cdots ,{99}) \) . 证明: \( {x}_{1}{x}_{2}^{2}\cdots {x}_{99}^{99} \leq  1 \) .

解析

注意到 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},\cdots ,{a}_{100} > 0 \) . 对 \( k = 1,2,\cdots ,{99} \) ,由平均值不等式知 \( 0 < {\left( \frac{k}{{a}_{1} + {a}_{2} + \cdots  + {a}_{k}}\right) }^{k} \leq \)

\( \frac{1}{{a}_{1}{a}_{2}\cdots {a}_{k}} \)

从而有 \( {x}_{1}{x}_{2}^{2}\cdots {x}_{99}^{99} = \mathop{\prod }\limits_{{k = 1}}^{{99}}{a}_{k + 1}^{k}\left( \frac{k}{{a}_{1} + {a}_{2} + \cdots  + {a}_{k}}\right)  \leq  \mathop{\prod }\limits_{{k = 1}}^{{99}}\frac{{a}_{k + 1}^{k}}{{a}_{1}{a}_{2}\cdots {a}_{k}} \) ①

记 ① 的右端为 \( T \) ,则对任意 \( i = 1,2,\cdots ,{100},{a}_{i} \) 在 \( T \) 的分子中的次数为 \( i - 1 \) ,在 \( T \)

的分母中的次数为 \( {100} - i \) . 从而

\( T = \mathop{\prod }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{{100}}{a}_{i}^{{2i} - {101}} = \mathop{\prod }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{{50}}{a}_{i}^{{2i} - {101}}{a}_{{101} - i}^{2\left( {{101} - i}\right)  - {101}} = \mathop{\prod }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{{50}}{\left( \frac{{a}_{{101} - i}}{{a}_{i}}\right) }^{{101} - {2i}} \)

又 \( 0 \leq  {a}_{{101} - i} \leq  {a}_{i}\left( {i = 1,2,\cdots ,{50}}\right) \) ,故 \( T \leq  1 \) ,结合 ① 得 \( {x}_{1}{x}_{2}^{2}\cdots {x}_{99}^{99} \leq  T \leq  1 \) .

二、求满足以下条件的所有正整数 \( n \) :

(1) \( n \) 至少有 4 个正约数；

( 2 )若 \( {d}_{1} < {d}_{2} < \cdots  < {d}_{k} \) 是 \( n \) 的所有正约数,则 \( {d}_{2} - {d}_{1},{d}_{3} - {d}_{2},\cdots ,{d}_{k} - {d}_{k - 1} \) 构成

等比数列.

解析

由条件知 \( k \geq  4 \) ,且 \( \frac{{d}_{3} - {d}_{2}}{{d}_{2} - {d}_{1}} = \frac{{d}_{k} - {d}_{k - 1}}{{d}_{k - 1} - {d}_{k - 2}} \) .

易知 \( {d}_{1} = 1,{d}_{k} = n,{d}_{k - 1} = \frac{n}{{d}_{2}},{d}_{k - 2} = \frac{n}{{d}_{3}} \) ,代入上式得

\( \frac{{d}_{3} - {d}_{2}}{{d}_{2} - 1} = \frac{n - \frac{n}{{d}_{2}}}{\frac{n}{{d}_{2}} - \frac{n}{{d}_{3}}} \) ,化简得 \( {\left( {d}_{3} - {d}_{2}\right) }^{2} = {\left( {d}_{2} - 1\right) }^{2}{d}_{3} \) .

由此可知 \( {d}_{3} \) 是完全平方数. 由于 \( {d}_{2} = p \) 是 \( n \) 的最小素因子, \( {d}_{3} \) 是平方数,故只能 \( {d}_{3} = {p}^{2}. \)

从而序列 \( {d}_{2} - {d}_{1},{d}_{3} - {d}_{2},\cdots ,{d}_{k} - {d}_{k - 1} \) 为 \( p - 1,{p}^{2} - p,{p}^{3} - {p}^{2},\cdots ,{p}^{k - 1} - {p}^{k - 2} \) ,即 \( {d}_{1},{d}_{2},{d}_{3},\cdots ,{d}_{k} \) 为 \( 1,p,{p}^{2},\cdots ,{p}^{k - 1} \) ,而此时相应的 \( n \) 为 \( {p}^{k - 1} \) .

综上可知,满足条件的 \( n \) 为所有形如 \( {p}^{a} \) 的数,其中 \( p \) 是素数,整数 \( a \geq  3 \) .

三、如图,点 \( A,B,C,D,E \) 在一条直线上顺次排列,满足 \( {BC} = {CD} = \sqrt{{AB} \cdot  {DE}} \) ,点 \( P \) 在该直线外,满足 \( {PB} = {PD} \) . 点 \( K,L \) 分别在线段 \( {PB},{PD} \) 上,满足 \( {KC} \) 平分 \( \angle {BKE} \) ,


\( {LC} \) 平分 \( \angle {ALD} \) .

证明: \( A,K,L,E \) 四点共圆.

<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( A \) \( B \) \( C \) \( D \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_108.jpg?x=487&y=392&w=742&h=427&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

解析

令 \( {AB} = 1,{BC} = {CD} = t\left( { > 0}\right) \) ,由条件知 \( {DE} = {t}^{2} \) .

注意到 \( \angle {BKE} < \angle {ABK} = \angle {PDE} < {180}^{ \circ  } - \angle {DEK} \) ,可在 \( {CB} \) 延长线上取一点 \( {A}^{\prime } \) , 使得 \( \angle {A}^{\prime }{KE} = \angle {ABK} = \angle {A}^{\prime }{BK} \) .

<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( A\left( \overline{{A}^{\prime }}\right) \) \( B \) \( C \) \( D \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_108.jpg?x=489&y=1072&w=739&h=425&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

此时有 \( \bigtriangleup {A}^{\prime }{BK} \sim  \bigtriangleup {A}^{\prime }{KE} \) ,故 \( \frac{{A}^{\prime }B}{{A}^{\prime }K} = \frac{{A}^{\prime }K}{{A}^{\prime }E} = \frac{BK}{KE} \) .

又 \( {KC} \) 平分 \( \angle {BKE} \) ,故 \( \frac{BK}{KE} = \frac{BC}{CE} = \frac{1}{t + {t}^{2}} = \frac{1}{1 + t} \) . 于是有

\( \frac{{A}^{\prime }B}{{A}^{\prime }E} = \frac{{A}^{\prime }B}{{A}^{\prime }K} \cdot  \frac{{A}^{\prime }K}{{A}^{\prime }E} = {\left( \frac{BK}{KE}\right) }^{2} = \frac{1}{1 + {2t} + {t}^{2}} = \frac{AB}{AE}. \)

由上式两端减 1,得 \( \frac{BE}{{A}^{\prime }E} = \frac{BE}{AE} \) ,从而 \( {A}^{\prime } = A \) . 因此 \( \angle {AKE} = \angle {A}^{\prime }{KE} = \angle {ABK} \) .

同理可得 \( \angle {ALE} = \angle {EDL} \) .

而 \( \angle {ABK} = \angle {EDL} \) ,所以 \( \angle {AKE} = \angle {ALE} \) . 因此 \( A,K,L,E \) 四点共圆.


四、 将一个凸 2019 边形的每条边任意染为红, 黄, 蓝三种颜色之一, 每种颜色的边各 673 条. 证明: 可作这个凸 2019 边形的 2016 条在内部互不相交的对角线将其剖分成 2017 个三角形, 并将所作的每条对角线也染为红, 黄, 蓝三种颜色之一, 使得每个三角形的三条边或者颜色全部相同, 或者颜色互不相同.

## 解析

我们对 \( n \geq  5 \) 归纳证明加强的命题: 如果将凸 \( n \) 边形的边染为三种颜色 \( a,b,c \) ,并且三种颜色的边均至少有一条, 那么可作满足要求的三角形剖分.

当 \( n = 5 \) 时,若三种颜色的边数为1,1,3,由对称性,只需考虑如下两种情形,分别可作图中所示的三角形剖分.

<!-- Media -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_109.jpg?x=691&y=715&w=335&h=323&r=0"/>

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_109.jpg?x=691&y=1079&w=335&h=330&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

若三种颜色的边数为1,2,2,由对称性,只需考虑如下三种情形,分别可作图中所示的三角形剖分.

<!-- Media -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_109.jpg?x=691&y=1568&w=337&h=332&r=0"/>


<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_110.jpg?x=685&y=271&w=346&h=697&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

假设结论对 \( n\left( {n \geq  5}\right) \) 成立,考虑 \( n + 1 \) 的情形,将凸 \( n + 1 \) 边形记为 \( {A}_{1}{A}_{2}\cdots {A}_{n + 1} \) . 情形一：有两种颜色的边各只有一条. 不妨设 \( a,b \) 色边只有一条. 由于 \( n + 1 \geq  6 \) ,故存在连续两条边均为 \( c \) 色,不妨设是 \( {A}_{n}{A}_{n + 1},{A}_{n + 1}{A}_{1} \) . 作对角线 \( {A}_{1}{A}_{n} \) ,并将 \( {A}_{1}{A}_{n} \) 染为 \( c \) 色,则三角形 \( {A}_{n}{A}_{n + 1}{A}_{1} \) 的三边全部同色. 此时凸 \( n \) 边形 \( {A}_{1}{A}_{2}\cdots {A}_{n} \) 的三种颜色的边均至少有一条, 由归纳假设, 可对其作符合要求的三角形剖分.

情形二：某种颜色的边只有一条,其余颜色的边均至少两条. 不妨设 \( a \) 色边只有一条, 于是可以选择两条相邻边均不是 \( a \) 色,不妨设 \( {A}_{n}{A}_{n + 1},{A}_{n + 1}{A}_{1} \) 均不是 \( a \) 色,作对角线 \( {A}_{1}{A}_{n} \) ,则 \( {A}_{1}{A}_{n} \) 有唯一的染色方式,使得三角形 \( {A}_{n}{A}_{n + 1}{A}_{1} \) 的三边全部同色或互不同色. 此时凸 \( n \) 边形 \( {A}_{1}{A}_{2}\cdots {A}_{n} \) 的三种颜色的边均至少有一条,由归纳假设,可对其作符合要求的三角形剖分.

情形三: 每种颜色的边均至少两条. 作对角线 \( {A}_{1}{A}_{n} \) ,则 \( {A}_{1}{A}_{n} \) 有唯一的染色方式,使得三角形 \( {A}_{n}{A}_{n + 1}{A}_{1} \) 的三边全部同色或互不同色. 此时凸 \( n \) 边形 \( {A}_{1}{A}_{2}\cdots {A}_{n} \) 的三种颜色的边均至少有一条, 由归纳假设, 可对其作符合要求的三角形剖分.

综合以上 3 种情形,可知 \( n + 1 \) 的情形下结论也成立.

由数学归纳法, 结论获证.


## 2018 年全国高中数学联赛一试答案 (A 卷)

## 一、 填空题: 本大题共 8 小题, 每小题 8 分, 满分 64 分.

1. 设集合 \( A = \{ 1,2,3,\cdots ,{99}\} ,B = \{ {2x} \mid  x \in  A\} ,C = \{ x \mid  {2x} \in  A\} \) ,则 \( B \cap  C \) 的元素个数为_____.

解析 24.

由条件知, \( B \cap  C = \{ 2,4,6,\cdots ,{198}\}  \cap  \left\{  {\frac{1}{2},1,\frac{3}{2},2,\cdots ,\frac{99}{2}}\right\}   = \{ 2,4,6,\cdots ,{48}\} \) ,故 \( B \cap  C \) 的元素的个数为 24 .

2. 设点 \( P \) 到平面 \( \alpha \) 的距离为 \( \sqrt{3} \) ,点 \( Q \) 在平面 \( \alpha \) 上,使得直线 \( {PQ} \) 与 \( \alpha \) 所成角不小于 \( {30}^{ \circ  } \) 且不大于 \( {60}^{ \circ  } \) ,则这样的点 \( Q \) 所构成的区域的面积为_____.

解析 \( {8\pi } \) .

设点 \( P \) 在平面 \( \alpha \) 上的射影为 \( O \) . 由条件知, \( \frac{OP}{OQ} = \tan \angle {OQP} \in  \left\lbrack  {\frac{\sqrt{3}}{3},\sqrt{3}}\right\rbrack \) ,即 \( {OQ} \in  \left\lbrack  {1,3}\right\rbrack \) , 故所求的区域面积为 \( \pi  \cdot  {3}^{2} - \pi  \cdot  {1}^{2} = {8\pi } \) .

3. 将1,2,3,4,5,6随机排成一行,记为 \( a,b,c,d,e,f \) ,则 \( {abc} + {def} \) 是偶数的概率为_____. 解析 \( \frac{9}{10} \) .

先考虑 \( {abc} + {def} \) 为奇数的情况,此时 \( {abc},{def} \) 一奇一偶,若 \( {abc} \) 为奇数,则 \( a,b,c \) 为 1,3,5的排列,进而 \( d,e,f \) 为2,4,6的排列,这样有 \( 3! \times  3! = {36} \) 种情况,由对称性可知,使 \( {abc} + {def} \) 为奇数的情况数为 \( {36} \times  2 = {72} \) 种. 从而 \( {abc} + {def} \) 为偶数的概率为 \( 1 - \frac{72}{6!} = 1 - \frac{72}{720} = \frac{9}{10}. \)

4. 在平面直角坐标系 \( {xOy} \) 中,椭圆 \( C : \frac{{x}^{2}}{{a}^{2}} + \frac{{y}^{2}}{{b}^{2}} = 1\left( {a > b > 0}\right) \) 的左右焦点分别是 \( {F}_{1},{F}_{2} \) ,椭圆 \( C \) 的弦 \( {ST} \) 与 \( {UV} \) 分别平行于 \( x \) 轴与 \( y \) 轴,且相交于点 \( P \) . 已知线段 \( {PU},{PS},{PV},{PT} \) 的长分别为1,2,3,6,则 \( \bigtriangleup  P{F}_{1}{F}_{2} \) 的面积为_____.

解析 \( \sqrt{15} \) .

由对称性,不妨设 \( P\left( {{x}_{p},{y}_{p}}\right) \) 在第一象限,则由条件知 \( {x}_{p} = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\left| {PT}\right|  - \left| {PS}\right| }\right)  = 2,{y}_{P} = \) \( \frac{1}{2}\left( {\left| {PV}\right|  - \left| {PU}\right| }\right)  = 1 \) ,即 \( P\left( {2,1}\right) \) . 进而由 \( {x}_{P} = \left| {PU}\right|  = 1,\left| {PS}\right|  = 2 \) 得 \( U\left( {2,2}\right) ,S\left( {4,1}\right) \) , 代入椭圆 \( C \) 的方程知 \( 4 \cdot  \frac{1}{{a}^{2}} + 4 \cdot  \frac{1}{{b}^{2}} = {16}\cdots \frac{1}{{a}^{2}} + \frac{1}{{b}^{2}} = 1 \) ,解得 \( {a}^{2} = {20},{b}^{2} = 5 \) . 从而 \( {S}_{\bigtriangleup P{F}_{1}{F}_{2}} = \frac{1}{2} \cdot  \left| {{F}_{1}{F}_{2}}\right|  \cdot  \left| {y}_{P}\right|  = \sqrt{{a}^{2} - {b}^{2}} \cdot  {y}_{P} = \sqrt{15}. \)


5. 设 \( f\left( x\right) \) 是定义在 \( \mathrm{R} \) 上的以 2 为周期的偶函数,在区间 \( \left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack \) 上严格递减,且满足 \( f\left( \pi \right)  = \) \( 1,f\left( {2\pi }\right)  = 2 \) ,则不等式组 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{l} 1 \leq  x \leq  2 \\  1 \leq  f\left( x\right)  \leq  2 \end{array}\right. \) 的解集为_____.

解析 \( \left\lbrack  {\pi  - 2,8 - {2\pi }}\right\rbrack \) .

由 \( f\left( x\right) \) 为偶函数及在 \( \left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack \) 上严格递减知, \( f\left( x\right) \) 在 \( \left\lbrack  {-1,0}\right\rbrack \) 上严格递增,再结合 \( f\left( x\right) \) 以 2 为周期可知, \( \left\lbrack  {1,2}\right\rbrack \) 是 \( f\left( x\right) \) 的严格递增区间. 注意到 \( f\left( {\pi  - 2}\right)  = f\left( \pi \right)  = 1,f\left( {8 - {2\pi }}\right)  = \) \( f\left( {-{2\pi }}\right)  = f\left( {2\pi }\right)  = 2 \) ,所以 \( 1 \leq  f\left( x\right)  \leq  2 \Leftrightarrow  f\left( {\pi  - 2}\right)  \leq  f\left( x\right)  \leq  f\left( {8 - {2\pi }}\right) \) ,而 \( 1 < \pi  - 2 < 8 - {2\pi } < 2 \) ,故原不等式组成立当且仅当 \( x \in  \left\lbrack  {\pi  - 2,8 - {2\pi }}\right\rbrack \) .

6. 设复数 \( z \) 满足 \( \left| z\right|  = 1 \) ,使得关于 \( x \) 的方程 \( z{x}^{2} + 2\bar{z}x + 2 = 0 \) 有实根,则这样的复数 \( z \) 的和为_____.

解析 \( - \frac{3}{2} \) .

设 \( z = a + {bi}\left( {a,b \in  \mathrm{R},{a}^{2} + {b}^{2} = 1}\right) \) . 将原方程改为 \( \left( {a + {bi}}\right) {x}^{2} + 2\left( {a - {bi}}\right) x + 2 = 0 \) ,分离实部与虚部后等价于 \( a{x}^{2} + {2ax} + 2 = 0 \) ,①

\( b{x}^{2} - {2bx} = 0 \) . ②

若 \( b = 0 \) ,则 \( {a}^{2} = 1 \) ,但当 \( a = 1 \) 时,① 无实数解,从而 \( a =  - 1 \) ,此时存在实数 \( x =  - 1 \pm  \sqrt{3} \) 满足 ①,②,故 \( z =  - 1 \) 满足条件. 若 \( b \neq  0 \) ,则由 ② 知 \( x \in  \{ 0,2\} \) ,但显然 \( x = 0 \) 不满足 ①,故只能是 \( x = 2 \) ,代入 ① 解得 \( a =  - \frac{1}{4} \) ,进而 \( b =  \pm  \frac{\sqrt{15}}{4} \) ,相应有 \( z = \frac{-1 \pm  \sqrt{15}i}{4} \) .

综上,满足条件的所有复数 \( z \) 之和为 \( - 1 + \frac{-1 + \sqrt{15}i}{4} + \frac{-1 - \sqrt{15}i}{4} =  - \frac{3}{2} \) .

7. 设 \( O \) 为 \( \bigtriangleup {ABC} \) 的外心,若 \( \overrightarrow{AO} = \overrightarrow{AB} + 2\overrightarrow{AC} \) ,则 \( \sin \angle {BAC} \) 的值为_____.

解析 \( \frac{\sqrt{10}}{4} \) .

不失一般性,设 \( \bigtriangleup  {ABC} \) 的外接圆半径 \( R = 2 \) . 由条件知, \( 2\overrightarrow{AC} = \overrightarrow{AO} - \overrightarrow{AB} = \overrightarrow{BO} \) . ① 故 \( {AC} = \frac{1}{2}{BO} = 1 \) . 取 \( {AC} \) 的中点 \( M \) ,则 \( {OM}\bot {AC} \) ,结合 ① 知 \( {OM}\bot {BO} \) ,且 \( B \) 与 \( A \) 位于直线 \( {OM} \) 的同侧. 于是 \( \cos \angle {BOC} = \cos \left( {{90}^{ \circ  } + \angle {MOC}}\right)  =  - \sin \angle {MOC} =  - \frac{MC}{OC} = \) \( - \frac{1}{4} \) . 在 \( \bigtriangleup {BOC} \) 中,由余弦定理得 \( {BC} = \sqrt{O{B}^{2} + O{C}^{2} - {2OB} \cdot  {OC} \cdot  \cos \angle {BOC}} = \) \( \sqrt{10} \) ,进而在 \( \bigtriangleup {ABC} \) 中,由正弦定理得 \( \sin \angle {BAC} = \frac{BC}{2R} = \frac{\sqrt{10}}{4} \) .

8. 设整数数列 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},\cdots ,{a}_{10} \) 满足 \( {a}_{10} = 3{a}_{1},{a}_{2} + {a}_{8} = 2{a}_{5} \) ,且 \( {a}_{i + 1} \in  \left\{  {1 + {a}_{i},2 + {a}_{i}}\right\}  ,i = \) \( 1,2,\cdots ,9 \) ,则这样的数列的个数为_____.

解析 80.

设 \( {b}_{i} = {a}_{i + 1} - {a}_{i} \in  \{ 1,2\} \left( {i = 1,2,\cdots ,9}\right) \) ,则有 \( 2{a}_{1} = {a}_{10} - {a}_{1} = {b}_{1} + {b}_{2} + \cdots  + {b}_{9} \) ,① \( {b}_{2} + {b}_{3} + {b}_{4} = {a}_{5} - {a}_{2} = {a}_{8} - {a}_{5} = {b}_{5} + {b}_{6} + {b}_{7} \) . ② 用 \( t \) 表示 \( {b}_{2},{b}_{3},{b}_{4} \) 中值为 2 的项数. 由 ② 知, \( t \) 也是 \( {b}_{5},{b}_{6},{b}_{7} \) 中值为 2 的项数,其中 \( t \in  \{ 0,1,2,3\} \) . 因此 \( {b}_{2},{b}_{3},\cdots ,{b}_{7} \) 的取法数为 \( {\left( {\mathrm{C}}_{3}^{0}\right) }^{2} + {\left( {\mathrm{C}}_{3}^{1}\right) }^{2} + {\left( {\mathrm{C}}_{3}^{2}\right) }^{2} + {\left( {\mathrm{C}}_{3}^{3}\right) }^{2} = {20} \) .


取定 \( {b}_{2},{b}_{3},\cdots ,{b}_{7} \) 后,任意指定 \( {b}_{8},{b}_{9} \) 的值,有 \( {2}^{2} = 4 \) 种方式.

最后由 ① 知,应取 \( {b}_{1} \in  \{ 1,2\} \) 使得 \( {b}_{1} + {b}_{2} + \cdots  + {b}_{9} \) 为偶数,这样的 \( {b}_{1} \) 的取法是唯一的,并且确定了整数 \( {a}_{1} \) 的值,进而数列 \( {b}_{1},{b}_{2},\cdots ,{b}_{9} \) 唯一对应一个满足条件的数列 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},\cdots ,{a}_{10} \) .

综上可知,满足条件的数列的个数为 \( {20} \times  4 = {80} \) .

## 二、 解答题：本大题共 3 小题,满分 56 分. 解答应写出文字说明、证明过程或演算步骤. 其 中第 9 题满分 16 分, 第 10、11 题满分 20 分.

9. 已知定义在 \( {\mathrm{R}}^{ * } \) 上的函数 \( f\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{l} \left| {{\log }_{3}x - 1}\right| ,0 < x \leq  9 \\  4 - \sqrt{x},x > 9 \end{array}\right. \) 设 \( a,b,c \) 是三个互不相同的实数,满足 \( f\left( a\right)  = f\left( b\right)  = f\left( c\right) \) ,求 \( {abc} \) 的取值范围.

解析(81,144).

不妨假设 \( a < b < c \) ,由于 \( f\left( x\right) \) 在 \( (0,3\rbrack \) 上严格递减,在 \( \left\lbrack  {3,9}\right\rbrack \) 上严格递增,在 \( \lbrack 9, + \infty ) \) 上严格递减,且 \( f\left( 3\right)  = 0,f\left( 9\right)  = 1 \) ,故结合图像可知 \( a \in  \left( {0,3}\right) ,b \in  \left( {3,9}\right) ,c \in  \left( {9, + \infty }\right) \) , 并且 \( f\left( a\right)  = f\left( b\right)  = f\left( c\right)  \in  \left( {0,1}\right) \) . 由 \( f\left( a\right)  = f\left( b\right) \) 得 \( 1 - {\log }_{3}a = {\log }_{3}b - 1 \) ,取 \( {\log }_{3}a + {\log }_{3}b = 2 \) ,因此 \( {ab} = {3}^{2} = 9 \) . 于是 \( {abc} = {9c} \) . 又 \( 0 < f\left( c\right)  = 4 - \sqrt{c} < 1 \) ,故 \( c \in  \left( {9,{16}}\right) \) . 进而 \( {abc} = {9c} \in  \left( {{81},{144}}\right) \) .

10. 已知实数列 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},{a}_{3},\cdots \) 满足: 对任意正整数 \( n \) ,有 \( {a}_{n}\left( {2{S}_{n} - {a}_{n}}\right)  = 1 \) ,其中 \( {S}_{n} \) 表示数列的前 \( n \) 项和. 证明:

(1)对任意正整数 \( n \) ,有 \( {a}_{n} < 2\sqrt{n} \) ；

(2)对任意正整数 \( n \) ,有 \( {a}_{n}{a}_{n + 1} < 1 \) .

解析

(1) 根据题意, 有

\[{a}_{1}^{2} = 1\]

命题成立. 当 \( n \geq  2 \) 时,有

\[\left( {{S}_{n} - {S}_{n - 1}}\right) \left( {{S}_{n} + {S}_{n - 1}}\right)  = 1\]

于是

\[{S}_{n}^{2} = {S}_{n - 1}^{2} + 1\]

从而

\[{S}_{n}^{2} = n,n = 1,2,\cdots .\]


因此当 \( n \geq  2 \) 时,有

\[{a}_{n} = {S}_{n} - {S}_{n - 1} \leq  \sqrt{n} + \sqrt{n - 1} < 2\sqrt{n},\]

命题成立.

(2)只需要考虑 \( {a}_{n} \) 与 \( {a}_{n + 1} \) 同号的情形,不妨设 \( {a}_{n} \) , \( {a}_{n + 1} \) 均为正数,则

\[{S}_{n + 1} > {S}_{n} > {S}_{n - 1} >  - \sqrt{n},\]

于是

\[{S}_{n} = \sqrt{n},{S}_{n + 1} = \sqrt{n + 1},\]

于是

\[{a}_{n} = \sqrt{n} \pm  \sqrt{n - 1},{a}_{n + 1} = \sqrt{n + 1} - \sqrt{n},\]

从而

\[{a}_{n}{a}_{n + 1} \leq  \left( {\sqrt{n} + \sqrt{n - 1}}\right)  \cdot  \left( {\sqrt{n + 1} - \sqrt{n}}\right) \]

\[ < \left( {\sqrt{n + 1} + \sqrt{n}}\right)  \cdot  \left( {\sqrt{n + 1} - \sqrt{n}}\right) \]

\[ = 1\text{,}\]

命题得证.

11. 在平面直角坐标系 \( {xOy} \) 中,设 \( {AB} \) 是抛物线 \( {y}^{2} = {4x} \) 的过点 \( F\left( {1,0}\right) \) 的弦, \( \bigtriangleup {AOB} \) 的外接圆交抛物线于点 \( P \) (不同于点 \( O,A,B \) ). 若 \( {PF} \) 平分 \( \angle {APB} \) ,求 \( \left| {PF}\right| \) 的所有可能值.

解析 \( \sqrt{13} - 1 \) .

设 \( A\left( {\frac{{y}_{1}^{2}}{4},{y}_{1}}\right) ,B\left( {\frac{{y}_{2}^{2}}{4},{y}_{2}}\right) ,P\left( {\frac{{y}_{3}^{2}}{4},{y}_{3}}\right) \) ,由条件知 \( {y}_{1},{y}_{2},{y}_{3} \) 两两不等且非零. 设直线 \( {AB} \) 的方程为 \( x = {ty} + 1 \) ,与抛物线方程联立可得 \( {y}^{2} - {4ty} - 4 = 0 \) ,故 \( {y}_{1}{y}_{2} =  - 4 \) . ①

注意到 \( \bigtriangleup {AOB} \) 的外接圆过点 \( O \) ,可设该圆的方程为 \( {x}^{2} + {y}^{2} + {dx} + {ey} = 0 \) ,与 \( x = \frac{{y}^{2}}{4} \) 联立得, \( \frac{{y}^{4}}{16} + \left( {1 + \frac{d}{4}}\right) {y}^{2} + {ey} = 0 \) . 该四次方程有 \( y = {y}_{1}{y}_{2},{y}_{3},0 \) 这四个不同的实根,故由韦达定理得 \( {y}_{1} + {y}_{2} + {y}_{3} + 0 = 0 \) ,从而 \( {y}_{3} =  - \left( {{y}_{1} + {y}_{2}}\right) \) . ②

因 \( {PF} \) 平分 \( \angle {APB} \) ,由角平分线定理知, \( \frac{\left| PA\right| }{\left| PB\right| } = \frac{\left| FA\right| }{\left| FB\right| } = \frac{\left| {y}_{1}\right| }{\left| {y}_{2}\right| } \) ,结合①,②,有 \( \frac{{y}_{1}^{2}}{{y}_{2}^{2}} = \frac{{\left| PA\right| }^{2}}{{\left| PB\right| }^{2}} = \frac{{\left( \frac{{y}_{3}^{2}}{4} - \frac{{y}_{1}^{2}}{4}\right) }^{2} + {\left( {y}_{3} - {y}_{1}\right) }^{2}}{{\left( \frac{{y}_{3}^{2}}{4} - \frac{{y}_{2}^{2}}{4}\right) }^{2} + {\left( {y}_{3} - {y}_{2}\right) }^{2}} = \frac{{\left( {\left( {y}_{1} + {y}_{2}\right) }^{2} - {y}_{1}^{2}\right) }^{2} + {16}{\left( 2{y}_{1} + {y}_{2}\right) }^{2}}{{\left( {\left( {y}_{1} + {y}_{2}\right) }^{2} - {y}_{2}^{2}\right) }^{2} + {16}{\left( 2{y}_{2} + {y}_{1}\right) }^{2}} = \)

\[\frac{{\left( {y}_{2}^{2} - 8\right) }^{2} + {16}\left( {4{y}_{1}^{2} + {y}_{2}^{2} - {16}}\right) }{{\left( {y}_{1}^{2} - 8\right) }^{2} + {16}\left( {4{y}_{2}^{2} + {y}_{1}^{2} - {16}}\right) } = \frac{{y}_{2}^{4} + {64}{y}_{1}^{2} - {192}}{{y}_{1}^{4} + {64}{y}_{2}^{2} - {192}}\]

即 \( {y}_{1}^{6} + {64}{y}_{1}^{2}{y}_{2}^{2} - {192}{y}_{1}^{2} = {y}_{2}^{6} + {64}{y}_{2}^{2}{y}_{1}^{2} - {192}{y}_{2}^{2} \) ,故 \( \left( {{y}_{1}^{2} - {y}_{2}^{2}}\right) \left( {{y}_{1}^{4} + {y}_{1}^{2}{y}_{2}^{2} + {y}_{2}^{4} - {192}}\right)  = 0 \) .


当 \( {y}_{1}^{2} = {y}_{2}^{2} \) 时, \( {y}_{2} =  - {y}_{1} \) ,故 \( {y}_{3} = 0 \) ,此时 \( P \) 与 \( O \) 重合,与条件不符.

当 \( {y}_{1}^{4} + {y}_{1}^{2}{y}_{2}^{2} + {y}_{2}^{4} - {192} = 0 \) 时,注意到 ①,有 \( {\left( {y}_{1}^{2} + {y}_{2}^{2}\right) }^{2} = {192} + {\left( {y}_{1}{y}_{2}\right) }^{2} = {208} \) . 因 \( {y}_{1}^{2} + {y}_{2}^{2} = 4\sqrt{13} > 8 = \left| {2{y}_{1}{y}_{2}}\right| \) ,故满足 ① 以及 \( {y}_{1}^{2} + {y}_{2}^{2} = 4\sqrt{13} \) 的实数 \( {y}_{1},{y}_{2} \) 存在,对应可得满足条件的点 \( A,B \) . 此时,结合 ①,② 知 \( \left| {PF}\right|  = \frac{{y}_{3}^{2}}{4} + 1 = \frac{{\left( {y}_{1} + {y}_{2}\right) }^{2} + 4}{4} = \) \( \frac{{y}_{1}^{2} + {y}_{2}^{2} - 4}{4} = \frac{\sqrt{208} - 4}{4} = \sqrt{13} - 1. \)


## 2018 年全国高中数学联赛二试答案 (A 卷)

一、 设 \( n \) 是正整数, \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},\cdots ,{a}_{n},{b}_{1},{b}_{2},\cdots ,{b}_{n},A,B \) 均为正实数,满足 \( {a}_{i} \leq  {b}_{i},{a}_{i} \leq  A,i = \)

\( 1,2,\cdots ,n \) ,且 \( \frac{{b}_{1}{b}_{2}\cdots {b}_{n}}{{a}_{1}{a}_{2}\cdots {a}_{n}} \leq  \frac{B}{A} \) .

证明: \( \frac{\left( {{b}_{1} + 1}\right) \left( {{b}_{2} + 1}\right) \cdots \left( {{b}_{n} + 1}\right) }{\left( {{a}_{1} + 1}\right) \left( {{a}_{2} + 1}\right) \cdots \left( {{a}_{n} + 1}\right) } \leq  \frac{B + 1}{A + 1} \) .

解析

由条件知, \( {k}_{i} = \frac{{b}_{i}}{{a}_{i}} \geq  1,i = 1,2,\cdots ,n \) . 记 \( \frac{B}{A} = K \) ,则 \( \frac{{b}_{1}{b}_{2}\cdots {b}_{n}}{{a}_{1}{a}_{2}\cdots {a}_{n}} \leq  \frac{B}{A} \) 化为

\( {k}_{1}{k}_{2}\cdots {k}_{n} \leq  K \) . 要证明

\( \mathop{\prod }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}\frac{{k}_{i}{a}_{i} + 1}{{a}_{i} + 1} \leq  \frac{{KA} + 1}{A + 1} \) . ①

对 \( i = 1,2,\cdots ,n \) ,由于 \( {k}_{i} \geq  1 \) 及 \( 0 < {a}_{i} \leq  A \) 知, \( \frac{{k}_{i}{a}_{i} + 1}{{a}_{i} + 1} = {k}_{i} - \frac{{k}_{i} - 1}{{a}_{i} + 1} \leq  {k}_{i} - \frac{{k}_{i} - 1}{A + 1} = \)

\( \frac{{k}_{i}A + 1}{A + 1} \)

结合 \( K \geq  {k}_{1}{k}_{2}\cdots {k}_{n} \) 知,为证明 ①,仅需证明当 \( A > 0,{k}_{i} \geq  1\left( {i = 1,2,\cdots ,n}\right) \) 时,有

\( \mathop{\prod }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}\frac{{k}_{i}A + 1}{A + 1} \leq  \frac{{k}_{1}{k}_{2}\cdots {k}_{n}A + 1}{A + 1} \) . ②

对 \( n \) 进行归纳,当 \( n = 1 \) 时,结论显然成立.

当 \( n = 2 \) 时,由 \( A > 0,{k}_{1},{k}_{2} \geq  1 \) 可知 \( \frac{{k}_{1}A + 1}{A + 1} \cdot  \frac{{k}_{2}A + 1}{A + 1} - \frac{{k}_{1}{k}_{2}A + 1}{A + 1} =  - \frac{A\left( {{k}_{1} - 1}\right) \left( {{k}_{2} - 1}\right) }{{\left( A + 1\right) }^{2}} \leq \)

0 ③

因此 \( n = 2 \) 时结论成立.

设 \( n = m \) 时结论成立,则当 \( n = m + 1 \) 时,利用归纳假设知, \( \mathop{\prod }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{{m + 1}}\frac{{k}_{1}A + 1}{A + 1} = \left( {\mathop{\prod }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{m}\frac{{k}_{i}A + 1}{A + 1}}\right) \) .

\( \frac{{k}_{m + 1}A + 1}{A + 1} \leq  \frac{{k}_{1}{k}_{2}\cdots {k}_{m}A + 1}{A + 1} \cdot  \frac{{k}_{m + 1}A + 1}{A + 1} \leq  \frac{{k}_{1}{k}_{2}\cdots {k}_{m + 1}A + 1}{A + 1}, \)

最后一步是在 ③ 中用 \( {k}_{1}{k}_{2}\cdots {k}_{m},{k}_{m + 1} \) (注意 \( {k}_{1}{k}_{2}\cdots {k}_{m} \geq  1,{k}_{m + 1} \geq  1 \) ) 分别代替

\( {k}_{1},{k}_{2} \) . 从而 \( n = m + 1 \) 时结论成立.

由数学归纳法可知,② 对所有正整数 \( n \) 成立,故命题得证.

二、如图, \( \bigtriangleup {ABC} \) 为锐角三角形, \( {AB} < {AC},M \) 为 \( {BC} \) 边的中点,点 \( D \) 和 \( E \) 分别为

\( \bigtriangleup {ABC} \) 的外接圆弧 \( {BAC} \) 和弧 \( {BC} \) 的中点, \( F \) 为 \( \bigtriangleup {ABC} \) 的内切圆在 \( {AB} \) 边上的切点,

\( G \) 为 \( {AE} \) 与 \( {BC} \) 的交点, \( N \) 在线段 \( {EF} \) 上,满足 \( {NB}\bot {AB} \) .

证明: 若 \( {BN} = {EM} \) ,则 \( {DF}\bot {FG} \) . (答题时请将图画在答卷纸上)


<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( D \) \( B \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_117.jpg?x=614&y=280&w=492&h=502&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

## 解析

由条件知, \( {DE} \) 为 \( \bigtriangleup {ABC} \) 外接圆的直径, \( {DE}\bot {BC} \) 于 \( M,{AE}\bot {AD} \) . 记 \( I \) 为 \( \bigtriangleup {ABC} \) 的内心,则 \( I \) 在 \( {AE} \) 上, \( {IF}\bot {AB} \) . 由 \( {NB}\bot {AB} \) 可知 \( \angle {NBE} = \angle {ABE} - \angle {ABN} = \) \( \left( {{180}^{ \circ  } - \angle {ADE}}\right)  - {90}^{ \circ  } = {90}^{ \circ  } - \angle {ADE} = \angle {MEI} \) . ①

<!-- Media -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_117.jpg?x=802&y=1034&w=113&h=115&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

又根据内心的性质,有 \( \angle {EBI} = \angle {EBC} + \angle {CBI} = \angle {EAC} + \angle {ABI} = \angle {EAB} + \) \( \angle {ABI} = \angle {EIB} \) ,从而 \( {BE} = {EI} \) . 结合 \( {BN} = {EM} \) 及①知, \( \bigtriangleup {NBE} \cong  \bigtriangleup {MEI} \) . 于是 \( \angle {EMI} = \angle {BNE} = {90}^{ \circ  } + \angle {BFE} = {180}^{ \circ  } - \angle {EFI} \) ,故 \( E,F,I,M \) 四点共圆. 进而可知 \( \angle {AFM} = {90}^{ \circ  } + \angle {IFM} = {90}^{ \circ  } + \angle {IEM} = \angle {AGM} \) ,从而 \( A,F,G,M \) 四点共圆. 再由 \( \angle {DAG} = \angle {DMG} = {90}^{ \circ  } \) 知, \( A,G,M,D \) 四点共圆,所以 \( A,F,G,M,D \) 五点共圆. 从而 \( \angle {DFG} = \angle {DAG} = {90}^{ \circ  } \) ,即 \( {DF} \bot  {FG} \) .

三、 设 \( n,k,m \) 是正整数,满足 \( k \geq  2 \) ,且 \( n \leq  m < \frac{{2k} - 1}{k}n \) . 设 \( A \) 是 \( \{ 1,2,\cdots ,m\} \) 的 \( n \) 元子集.

证明: 区间 \( \left( {0,\frac{n}{k - 1}}\right) \) 中每个整数均可表示为 \( a - {a}^{\prime } \) ,其中 \( a,{a}^{\prime } \in  A \) .

解析

用反证法. 假设存在整数 \( x \in  \left( {0,\frac{n}{k - 1}}\right) \) 不可表示为 \( a - {a}^{\prime },a,{a}^{\prime } \in  A \) . 作带余除法 \( m = {xq} + r \) ,其中 \( 0 \leq  r < x \) . 将 \( 1,2,\cdots ,m \) 按模 \( x \) 的同余类划分成 \( x \) 个公差为 \( x \) 的等差数列,其中 \( r \) 个等差数列有 \( q + 1 \) 项, \( x - r \) 个等差数列有 \( q \) 项. 由于 \( A \) 中没有两数之差为 \( x \) ,故 \( A \) 不能包含以 \( x \) 为公差的等差数列的相邻两项. 从而 \( n = \left| A\right|  \leq \)


\( r\left\lbrack  \frac{q + 1}{2}\right\rbrack   + \left( {x - r}\right) \left\lbrack  \frac{q}{2}\right\rbrack   = \left\{  \begin{array}{l} x \cdot  \frac{q + 1}{2},2/q \\  x \cdot  \frac{q}{2} + r,2 \mid  q \end{array}\right. \)

这里 \( \lceil \alpha \rceil \) 表示不小于 \( \alpha \) 的最小整数. 由条件,我们有

\( n > \frac{k}{{2k} - 1}m = \frac{k}{{2k} - 1}\left( {{xq} + r}\right) \) . ②

又 \( x \in  \left( {0,\frac{n}{k - 1}}\right) \) ,故 \( n > \left( {k - 1}\right) x \) . ③

情形一

\( q \) 是奇数,则由 ① 知, \( n \leq  x \cdot  \frac{q + 1}{2} \) .

结合 ②,④ 可知, \( x \cdot  \frac{q + 1}{2} \geq  n > \frac{k}{{2k} - 1}\left( {{xq} + r}\right)  \geq  \frac{k}{{2k} - 1}{xq} \) ,从而 \( q < {2k} - 1 \) . 再由 \( q \) 是奇数可知, \( q \leq  {2k} - 3 \) ,于是 \( n \leq  x \cdot  \frac{q + 1}{2} \leq  \left( {k - 1}\right) x \) ,与 ③ 矛盾.

情形二

\( q \) 是偶数,则由 ① 知, \( n \leq  x \cdot  \frac{q}{2} + r \) . ⑤

结合 ②,⑤ 可知, \( x \cdot  \frac{q}{2} + r \geq  n > \frac{k}{{2k} - 1}\left( {{xq} + r}\right) \) ,从而 \( \frac{xq}{2\left( {{2k} - 1}\right) } < \frac{k - 1}{{2k} - 1}r < \frac{\left( {k - 1}\right) x}{{2k} - 1} \) , 故 \( q < 2\left( {k - 1}\right) \) . 再由 \( q \) 是偶数可知, \( q \leq  {2k} - 4 \) ,于是 \( n \leq  x \cdot  \frac{q}{2} + r \leq  \left( {k - 2}\right) x + r < \left( {k - 1}\right) x \) , 与 ③ 矛盾.

综上可知, 反证法假设不成立, 结论获证.

四、数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 定义如下: \( {a}_{1} \) 是任意正整数,对整数 \( n \geq  1,{a}_{n + 1} \) 是与 \( \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}{a}_{i} \) 互素,且不等于 \( {a}_{1},\cdots ,{a}_{n} \) 的最小整数.

证明: 每个正整数均在数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 中出现.

解析

显然 \( {a}_{1} = 1 \) 或 \( {a}_{2} = 1 \) . 下面考虑整数 \( m > 1 \) ,设 \( m \) 有 \( k \) 个不同素因子,我们对 \( k \) 归纳证明 \( m \) 在 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 中出现. 记 \( {S}_{n} = {a}_{1} + \cdots  + {a}_{n},n \geq  1 \) .

\( k = 1 \) 时, \( m \) 时素数方幂,设 \( m = {p}^{a} \) ,其中 \( a > 0,p \) 是素数. 假设 \( m \) 不在 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 中出现. 由于 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 各项互不相同,因此存在正整数 \( N \) ,当 \( n \geq  N \) 时,都有 \( {a}_{n} > {p}^{a} \) . 若对某个 \( n \geq  N,p//{S}_{n} \) ,那么 \( {p}^{a} \) 与 \( {S}_{n} \) 互素,又 \( {a}_{1},\cdots ,{a}_{n} \) 中无一项是 \( {p}^{a} \) ,故由数列定义知 \( {a}_{n + 1} \leq  {p}^{a} \) ,但是 \( {a}_{n + 1} > {p}^{a} \) ,矛盾!

因此对每个 \( n \geq  N \) ,都有 \( p \mid  {S}_{n} \) ,但由 \( p \mid  {S}_{n + 1} \) 及 \( p \mid  {S}_{n} \) 知 \( p \mid  {a}_{n + 1} \) ,从而 \( {a}_{n + 1} \) 与 \( {S}_{n} \) 不互素,这与 \( {a}_{n + 1} \) 的定义矛盾.

假设 \( k \geq  2 \) ,且结论对 \( k - 1 \) 成立. 设 \( m \) 的标准分解为 \( m = {p}_{1}^{{a}_{1}}{p}_{2}^{{a}_{2}}\cdots {p}_{k}^{{a}_{k}} \) ,假设 \( m \) 不在 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 中出现,于是存在正整数 \( {N}^{\prime } \) ,当 \( n \geq  {N}^{\prime } \) 时,都有 \( {a}_{n} > m \) . 取充分大的正整数 \( {\beta }_{1},\cdots ,{\beta }_{k - 1} \) ,使得 \( M = {p}_{1}^{{\beta }_{1}}\cdots {p}_{k - 1}^{{\beta }_{k - 1}} > \mathop{\max }\limits_{{1 \leq  n \leq  {N}^{\prime }}}{a}_{n} \) .

我们证明,对 \( n \geq  {N}^{\prime } \) ,有 \( {a}_{n + 1} \neq  M \) . 对任意 \( n \geq  {N}^{\prime } \) ,若 \( {S}_{n} \) 与 \( {p}_{1}{p}_{2}\cdots {p}_{k} \) 互素,则 \( m \) 与 \( {S}_{n} \) 互素,又 \( m \) 在 \( {a}_{1},\cdots ,{a}_{n} \) 中均未出现,而 \( {a}_{n + 1} > m \) ,这与数列的定义矛盾. 因


此我们推出: 对任意 \( n \geq  {N}^{\prime },{S}_{n} \) 与 \( {p}_{1}{p}_{2}\cdots {p}_{k} \) 不互素. (*)

情形一

若存在 \( i\left( {1 \leq  i \leq  k - 1}\right) \) ,使得 \( {p}_{i} \mid  {S}_{n} \) ,因 \( \left( {{a}_{n + 1},{S}_{n}}\right)  = 1 \) ,故 \( {p}_{i} \mid  {a}_{n + 1} \) ,从而 \( {a}_{n + 1} \neq  M \) (因 \( {p}_{i} \mid  M \) ).

情形二

若对每个 \( i\left( {1 \leq  i \leq  k - 1}\right) \) ,均有 \( {p}_{i}/{S}_{n} \) ,则由 (*) 知必有 \( {p}_{k} \mid  {S}_{n} \) . 于是 \( {p}_{k}/{a}_{n + 1} \) ,进而 \( {p}_{k}/\left\{  {{S}_{n} + {a}_{n + 1}\text{,即}{p}_{k}/{S}_{n + 1}\text{. 故由 (*) 知,存在}{i}_{0}\left( {1 \leq  {i}_{0} \leq  k - 1}\right) \text{,使得}{p}_{{i}_{0}} \mid  {S}_{n + 1}}\right\} \) ,再由 \( {S}_{n + 1} = {S}_{n} + {a}_{n + 1} \) 及前面的假设 \( {p}_{i}/{S}_{n}\left( {1 \leq  i \leq  k - 1}\right) \) ,可知 \( {p}_{{i}_{0}}/{a}_{n + 1} \) ,故 \( {a}_{n + 1} \neq  M \) . 因此对 \( n \geq  {N}^{\prime } + 1 \) ,均有 \( {a}_{n} \neq  M \) ,而 \( M > \mathop{\max }\limits_{{1 \leq  i \leq  {N}^{\prime }}}{a}_{n} \) ,故 \( M \) 不在 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 中出现,这与归纳假设矛盾. 因此,若 \( m \) 有 \( k \) 个不同素因子,则 \( m \) 一定在 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 中出现. 由数学归纳法知,所有正整数均在 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 中出现.


## 2018 年全国高中数学联赛一试答案 (B 卷)

## 一、 填空题: 本大题共 8 小题, 每小题 8 分, 满分 64 分.

1. 设集合 \( A = \{ 2,0,1,8\} ,B = \{ {2a} \mid  a \in  A\} \) ,则 \( A\bigcup B \) 的所有元素之和是_____.

解析 31.

易知 \( B = \{ 4,0,2,{16}\} \) ,故 \( A\bigcup B = \{ 0,1,2,4,8,{16}\} .A\bigcup B \) 的所有元素之和是 \( 0 + 1 + \) \( 2 + 4 + 8 + {16} = {31} \)

2. 已知圆锥的顶点为 \( P \) ,底面半径长为 2,高为 1. 在圆锥底面上取一点 \( Q \) ,使得直线 \( {PQ} \) 与底面所成角不大于 \( {45}^{ \circ  } \) ,则满足条件的点 \( Q \) 所构成的区域的面积为_____.

解析 \( {3\pi } \) .

圆锥顶点 \( P \) 在底面上的投影即为底面中心,记之为 \( O \) . 由条件知, \( \frac{OP}{OQ} = \tan \angle {OQP} \leq  1 \) , 即 \( {OQ} \geq  1 \) ,故所求的区域面积为 \( \pi  \cdot  {2}^{2} - \pi  \cdot  {1}^{2} = {3\pi } \) .

3. 将1,2,3,4,5,6随机排成一行,记为 \( a,b,c,d,e,f \) ,则 \( {abc} + {def} \) 是奇数的概率为_____. 解析 \( \frac{1}{10} \) .

当 \( {abc} + {def} \) 为奇数时, \( {abc},{def} \) 必为一奇一偶,若 \( {abc} \) 为奇数,则 \( a,b,c \) 为1,3,5的排列, \( d,e,f \) 为2,4,6的排列,这样有 \( 3! \times  3! = {36} \) 种情况. 由对称性可知,满足条件的情况数为 \( {36} \times  2 = {72} \) 种,从而所求概率为 \( \frac{72}{6!} = \frac{72}{720} = \frac{1}{10} \) .

4. 在平面直角坐标系 \( {xOy} \) 中,直线 \( l \) 通过原点, \( \overrightarrow{n} = \left( {3,1}\right) \) 是 \( l \) 的一个法向量. 已知数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 满足: 对任意正整数 \( n \) ,点 \( \left( {{a}_{n + 1},{a}_{n}}\right) \) 均在 \( l \) 上. 若 \( {a}_{2} = 6 \) ,则 \( {a}_{1}{a}_{2}{a}_{3}{a}_{4}{a}_{5} \) 的值为_____.

解析 -32.

易知直线 \( l \) 的方程是 \( {3x} + y = 0 \) . 因此对任意正整数 \( n \) ,有 \( 3{a}_{n + 1} + {a}_{n} = 0 \) ,即 \( {a}_{n + 1} =  - \frac{1}{3}{a}_{n} \) ,故 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 是以 \( - \frac{1}{3} \) 为公比的等比数列. 于是 \( {a}_{3} =  - \frac{1}{3}{a}_{2} =  - 2 \) . 由等比数列的性质可得, \( {a}_{1}{a}_{2}{a}_{3}{a}_{4}{a}_{5} = {a}_{3}^{5} = {\left( -2\right) }^{5} =  - {32} \) .

5. 设 \( \alpha ,\beta \) 满足 \( \tan \left( {\alpha  + \frac{\pi }{3}}\right)  =  - 3,\tan \left( {\beta  - \frac{\pi }{6}}\right)  = 5 \) ,则 \( \tan \left( {\alpha  - \beta }\right) \) 的值为_____.

解析 \( - \frac{7}{4} \) .

由两角差的正切公式可知 \( \tan \left( {\left( {\alpha  + \frac{\pi }{3}}\right)  - \left( {\beta  - \frac{\pi }{6}}\right) }\right)  = \frac{-3 - 5}{1 + \left( {-3}\right)  \times  5} = \frac{4}{7} \) ,即 \( \tan \left( {\alpha  - \beta  + \frac{\pi }{2}}\right)  = \)

\( \frac{4}{7} \) ,从而 \( \tan \left( {\alpha  - \beta }\right)  =  - \cot \left( {\alpha  - \beta  + \frac{\pi }{2}}\right)  =  - \frac{7}{4} \) .


6. 设抛物线 \( C : {y}^{2} = {2x} \) 的准线与 \( x \) 轴交于点 \( A \) ,过点 \( B\left( {-1,0}\right) \) 作一直线 \( l \) 与抛物线 \( C \) 相切于点 \( K \) ,过点 \( A \) 作 \( l \) 的平行线,与抛物线 \( C \) 交于点 \( M,N \) ,则 \( \bigtriangleup {KMN} \) 的面积为_____.

解析 \( \frac{1}{2} \) .

设直线 \( l \) 与 \( {MN} \) 的斜率为 \( k \) ,则 \( l : x = \frac{1}{k}y - 1,{MN} : x = \frac{1}{k}y - \frac{1}{2} \) .

将 \( l \) 与 \( C \) 联立,得方程 \( {y}^{2} - \frac{2}{k}y + 2 = 0 \) ,由条件知其判别式为零,故 \( k =  \pm  \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2} \) . 将 \( {MN} \) 与 \( C \) 联立,得方程 \( {y}^{2} - \frac{2}{k}y + 1 = 0 \) ,于是 \( \left| {{y}_{M} - {y}_{N}}\right|  = \sqrt{{\left( {y}_{M} + {y}_{N}\right) }^{2} - 4{y}_{M}{y}_{N}} = \) \( \begin{array}{l} \sqrt{\frac{4}{{k}^{2}} - 4} = 2,\text{ 结合 }l\text{ 与 }{MN}\text{ 平行,可知 }{S}_{\bigtriangleup {KMN}} = {S}_{\bigtriangleup {BMN}} = \left| {{S}_{\bigtriangleup {BAM}} - {S}_{\bigtriangleup {BAN}}}\right|  = \\  \frac{1}{2} \cdot  \left| {AB}\right|  \cdot  \left| {{y}_{M} - {y}_{N}}\right|  = \frac{1}{2} \cdot  \frac{1}{2} \cdot  2 = \frac{1}{2}. \end{array} \)

7. 设 \( f\left( x\right) \) 是定义在 \( \mathrm{R} \) 上的以 2 为周期的偶函数,在区间 \( \left\lbrack  {1,2}\right\rbrack \) 上严格递减,且满足 \( f\left( \pi \right)  = \) \( 1,f\left( {2\pi }\right)  = 0 \) ,则不等式组 \( \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} 0 \leq  x \leq  1 & \text{ 的解集为___. } \\  0 \leq  f\left( x\right)  \leq  1 &  \end{array}\right. \)

解析 \( \left\lbrack  {{2\pi } - 6,4 - \pi }\right\rbrack \) .

由 \( f\left( x\right) \) 为偶函数及在 \( \left\lbrack  {1,2}\right\rbrack \) 上严格递减知, \( f\left( x\right) \) 在 \( \left\lbrack  {-2, - 1}\right\rbrack \) 上严格递增,再结合 \( f\left( x\right) \) 以 2 为周期可知, \( \left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack \) 是 \( f\left( x\right) \) 的严格递增区间. 注意到 \( f\left( {4 - \pi }\right)  = f\left( {\pi  - 4}\right)  = f\left( \pi \right)  = \) \( 1,f\left( {{2\pi } - 6}\right)  = f\left( {2\pi }\right)  = 0 \) ,所以 \( 0 \leq  f\left( x\right)  \leq  1 \Leftrightarrow  f\left( {{2\pi } - 6}\right)  \leq  f\left( x\right)  \leq  f\left( {4 - \pi }\right) \) ,而 \( 0 < {2\pi } - 6 < 4 - \pi  < 1 \) ,故原不等式组成立当且仅当 \( x \in  \left\lbrack  {{2\pi } - 6,4 - \pi }\right\rbrack \) .

8. 已知复数 \( {z}_{1},{z}_{2},{z}_{3} \) 满足 \( \left| {z}_{1}\right|  = \left| {z}_{2}\right|  = \left| {z}_{3}\right|  = 1,\left| {{z}_{1} + {z}_{2} + {z}_{3}}\right|  = r \) ,其中 \( r \) 是给定实数, 则 \( \frac{{z}_{1}}{{z}_{2}} + \frac{{z}_{2}}{{z}_{3}} + \frac{{z}_{3}}{{z}_{1}} \) 的实数是_____(用含有 \( r \) 的式子表示).

解析 \( \frac{{r}^{2} - 3}{2} \) .

记 \( w = \frac{{z}_{1}}{{z}_{2}} + \frac{{z}_{2}}{{z}_{3}} + \frac{{z}_{3}}{{z}_{1}} \) . 由复数模的性质可知 \( \overline{{z}_{1}} = \frac{1}{{z}_{1}},\overline{{z}_{2}} = \frac{1}{{z}_{2}},\overline{{z}_{3}} = \frac{1}{{z}_{3}} \) ,因此 \( w = \) \( {z}_{1}\overline{{z}_{2}} + {z}_{2}\overline{{z}_{3}} + {z}_{3}\overline{{z}_{1}} \) . 于是 \( {r}^{2} = \left( {{z}_{1} + {z}_{2} + {z}_{3}}\right) \left( {\overline{{z}_{1}} + \overline{{z}_{2}} + \overline{{z}_{3}}}\right)  = {\left| {z}_{1}\right| }^{2} + {\left| {z}_{2}\right| }^{2} + {\left| {z}_{3}\right| }^{2} + w + \bar{w} = \) \( 3 + 2\operatorname{Re}w \) ,解得 \( \operatorname{Re}w = \frac{{r}^{2} - 3}{2} \) .

## 二、 解答题：本大题共 3 小题,满分 56 分. 解答应写出文字说明、证明过程或演算步骤. 其 中第 9 题满分 16 分, 第 10、11 题满分 20 分.

9. 已知数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\}   : {a}_{1} = 7,\frac{{a}_{n + 1}}{{a}_{n}} = {a}_{n} + 2,n = 1,2,3,\cdots \) . 求满足 \( {a}_{n} > {4}^{2018} \) 的最小正整数 \( n \) .

解析 12.

由 \( \frac{{a}_{n + 1}}{{a}_{n}} = {a}_{n} + 2 \) 可知 \( {a}_{n + 1} + 1 = {\left( {a}_{n} + 1\right) }^{2} \) . 因此 \( {a}_{n} + 1 = {\left( {a}_{1} + 1\right) }^{{2}^{n - 1}} = {8}^{{2}^{n - 1}} = {2}^{3 \times  {2}^{n - 1}} \) ,


故 \( {a}_{n} = {2}^{3 \times  {2}^{n - 1}} - 1 \) . 显然 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 单调递增. 由于 \( {a}_{11} = {2}^{3072} - 1 < {2}^{4036} = {4}^{2018},{a}_{12} = \) \( {2}^{6144} - 1 > {2}^{4036} = {4}^{2018} \) ,故满足题目条件的 \( n \) 的最小值是 12 .

10. 已知定义在 \( {\mathrm{R}}^{ * } \) 上的函数 \( f\left( x\right) \) 为 \( f\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{l} \left| {{\log }_{3}x - 1}\right| ,0 < x \leq  9 \\  4 - \sqrt{x},x > 9 \end{array}\right. \) 设 \( a,b,c \) 是三个互不相同的实数,满足 \( f\left( a\right)  = f\left( b\right)  = f\left( c\right) \) ,求 \( {abc} \) 的取值范围.

解析(81,144).

不妨假设 \( a < b < c \) ,由于 \( f\left( x\right) \) 在 \( (0,3\rbrack \) 上严格递减,在 \( \left\lbrack  {3,9}\right\rbrack \) 上严格递增,在 \( \lbrack 9, + \infty ) \) 上严格递减,且 \( f\left( 3\right)  = 0,f\left( 9\right)  = 1 \) ,故结合图像可知 \( a \in  \left( {0,3}\right) ,b \in  \left( {3,9}\right) ,c \in  \left( {9, + \infty }\right) \) , 并且 \( f\left( a\right)  = f\left( b\right)  = f\left( c\right)  \in  \left( {0,1}\right) \) . 由 \( f\left( a\right)  = f\left( b\right) \) 得 \( 1 - {\log }_{3}a = {\log }_{3}b - 1 \) ,取 \( {\log }_{3}a + {\log }_{3}b = 2 \) ,因此 \( {ab} = {3}^{2} = 9 \) . 于是 \( {abc} = {9c} \) . 又 \( 0 < f\left( c\right)  = 4 - \sqrt{c} < 1 \) ,故 \( c \in  \left( {9,{16}}\right) \) . 进而 \( {abc} = {9c} \in  \left( {{81},{144}}\right) \) .

11. 如图所示,在平面直角坐标系 \( {xOy} \) 中, \( A,B \) 与 \( C,D \) 分别是椭圆 \( \Gamma  : \frac{{x}^{2}}{{a}^{2}} + \frac{{y}^{2}}{{b}^{2}} = 1(a > \) \( b > 0) \) 的左右顶点与上下顶点. 设 \( P,Q \) 是 \( \Gamma \) 上且位于第一象限的两点,满足 \( {OQ}\parallel {AP} \) , \( M \) 是线段 \( {AP} \) 的中点,射线 \( {OM} \) 与椭圆交于点 \( R \) .

证明: 线段 \( {OQ},{OR},{BC} \) 能构成一个直角三角形.

<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( R \) \( B \) \( D \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_122.jpg?x=619&y=1058&w=476&h=410&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

解析

设点 \( P \) 坐标为 \( \left( {{x}_{0},{y}_{0}}\right) \) . 由于 \( \overrightarrow{OQ}\parallel \overrightarrow{AP},\overrightarrow{AP} = \overrightarrow{OP} - \overrightarrow{OA};\overrightarrow{OR}\parallel \overrightarrow{OM},\overrightarrow{OM} = \frac{1}{2}(\overrightarrow{OP} + \) \( \overrightarrow{OA} \) ),故存在实数 \( \lambda ,\mu \) ,使得 \( \overrightarrow{OQ} = \lambda \left( {\overrightarrow{OP} - \overrightarrow{OA}}\right) ,\overrightarrow{OR} = \mu \left( {\overrightarrow{OP} + \overrightarrow{OA}}\right) \) . 此时点 \( Q,R \) 的坐标可分别表示是 \( \left( {\lambda \left( {{x}_{0} + a}\right) ,\lambda {y}_{0}}\right) ,\left( {\mu \left( {{x}_{0} - a}\right) ,\mu {y}_{0}}\right) \) . 由于点 \( Q,R \) 都在椭圆上,所以 \( {\lambda }^{2}\left( {\frac{{\left( {x}_{0} + a\right) }^{2}}{{a}^{2}} + \frac{{y}_{0}^{2}}{{b}^{2}}}\right)  = {\mu }^{2}\left( {\frac{{\left( {x}_{0} - a\right) }^{2}}{{a}^{2}} + \frac{{y}_{0}^{2}}{{b}^{2}}}\right)  = 1. \) 结合 \( \frac{{x}_{0}^{2}}{{a}^{2}} + \frac{{y}_{0}^{2}}{{b}^{2}} = 1 \) 知,上式可化为 \( {\lambda }^{2}\left( {2 + \frac{2{x}_{0}}{a}}\right)  = {\mu }^{2}\left( {2 - \frac{2{x}_{0}}{a}}\right)  = 1 \) ,解得 \( {\lambda }^{2} = \) \( \frac{a}{2\left( {a + {x}_{0}}\right) },{\mu }^{2} = \frac{a}{2\left( {a - {x}_{0}}\right) }. \)


\[\text{因此}{\left| OQ\right| }^{2} + {\left| OR\right| }^{2} = {\lambda }^{2}\left( {{\left( {x}_{0} + a\right) }^{2} + {y}_{0}^{2}}\right)  + {\mu }^{2}\left( {{\left( {x}_{0} - a\right) }^{2} + {y}_{0}^{2}}\right) \]

\[ = \frac{a}{2\left( {a + {x}_{0}}\right) }\left( {{\left( {x}_{0} + a\right) }^{2} + {y}_{0}^{2}}\right)  + \frac{a}{2\left( {a - {x}_{0}}\right) }\left( {{\left( {x}_{0} - a\right) }^{2} + {y}_{0}^{2}}\right) \]

\[ = \frac{a\left( {a + {x}_{0}}\right) }{2} + \frac{a{y}_{0}^{2}}{2\left( {a + {x}_{0}}\right) } + \frac{a\left( {a - {x}_{0}}\right) }{2} + \frac{a{y}_{0}^{2}}{2\left( {a - {x}_{0}}\right) }\]

\[ = {a}^{2} + \frac{a{y}_{0}^{2}}{2}\left( {\frac{1}{a + {x}_{0}} + \frac{1}{a - {x}_{0}}}\right) \]

\[ = {a}^{2} + \frac{a{y}_{0}^{2}}{2} \cdot  \frac{2a}{{a}^{2} - {x}_{0}^{2}} = {a}^{2} + \frac{{a}^{2} \cdot  {b}^{2}\left( {1 - \frac{{x}_{0}^{2}}{{a}^{2}}}\right) }{{a}^{2} - {x}_{0}^{2}} = {a}^{2} + {b}^{2} = {\left| BC\right| }^{2}.\]

从而线段 \( {OQ},{OR},{BC} \) 能构成一个直角三角形.


## 2018 年全国高中数学联赛二试答案 (B 卷)

一、 设 \( a,b \) 是实数,函数 \( f\left( x\right)  = {ax} + b + \frac{9}{x} \) . 证明: 存在 \( {x}_{0} \in  \left\lbrack  {1,9}\right\rbrack \) ,使得 \( \left| {f\left( {x}_{0}\right) }\right|  \geq  2 \) . 解析

证法一

只需证明存在 \( u,v \in  \left\lbrack  {1,9}\right\rbrack \) ,满足 \( \left| {f\left( u\right)  - f\left( v\right) }\right|  \geq  4 \) ,进而由绝对值不等式得 \( \left| {f\left( u\right) }\right|  + \) \( \left| {f\left( v\right) }\right|  \geq  \left| {f\left( u\right)  - f\left( v\right) }\right|  \geq  4 \) ,故 \( \left| {f\left( u\right) }\right|  \geq  2 \) 与 \( \left| {f\left( v\right) }\right|  \geq  2 \) 中至少有一个成立. 当 \( a \in \) \( \left( {-\infty ,\frac{1}{2}\rbrack \bigcup \lbrack \frac{3}{2}, + \infty }\right) \) 时,有 \( \left| {f\left( 1\right)  - f\left( 9\right) }\right|  = \left| {\left( {a + b + 9}\right)  - \left( {{9a} + b + 1}\right) }\right|  = 8\left| {1 - a}\right|  \geq  4 \) . 当 \( \frac{1}{2} < a < \frac{3}{2} \) 时,有 \( \frac{3}{\sqrt{a}} \in  \left\lbrack  {1,9}\right\rbrack \) . 再分两种情况: 若 \( \frac{1}{2} < a \leq  1 \) ,则 \( \left| {f\left( 1\right)  - f\left( \frac{3}{\sqrt{a}}\right) }\right|  = \) \( \left| {\left( {a + b + 9}\right)  - \left( {6\sqrt{a} + b}\right) }\right|  = {\left( 3 - \sqrt{a}\right) }^{2} \geq  4 \) . 若 \( 1 < a < \frac{3}{2} \) ,则 \( \left| {f\left( 9\right)  - f\left( \frac{3}{\sqrt{a}}\right) }\right|  = \) \( \left| {\left( {{9a} + b + 1}\right)  - \left( {6\sqrt{a} + b}\right) }\right|  = {\left( 3\sqrt{a} - 1\right) }^{2} \geq  4 \) .

综上可知,存在 \( u,v \in  \left\lbrack  {1,9}\right\rbrack \) ,满足 \( \left| {f\left( u\right)  - f\left( v\right) }\right|  \geq  4 \) ,从而命题得证.

证法二

用反证法. 假设对任意 \( x \in  \left\lbrack  {1,9}\right\rbrack \) ,均有 \( \left| {f\left( x\right) }\right|  < 2 \) ,则 \( \left| {f\left( 1\right) }\right|  < 2,\left| {f\left( 3\right) }\right|  < 2,\left| {f\left( 9\right) }\right|  < 2 \) . 易知 \( f\left( 1\right)  = a + b + 9 \) ,①

\( f\left( 3\right)  = {3a} + b + 3 \) ,②

\( f\left( 9\right)  = {9a} + b + 1 \) . ③

由 ① ,② 得, \( {2a} - 6 = f\left( 2\right)  - f\left( 1\right) \) ；又由 ② ,③ 得, \( {6a} - 2 = f\left( 3\right)  - f\left( 2\right) \) . 由上述两式消去 \( a \) ,可知 \( f\left( 3\right)  - {4f}\left( 2\right)  + {3f}\left( 1\right)  = \left( {{6a} - 2}\right)  - 3 \cdot  \left( {{2a} - 6}\right)  = {16} \) . 但 \( f\left( 3\right)  - {4f}\left( 2\right)  + {3f}\left( 1\right)  < 2 + 4 \cdot  2 + 3 \cdot  2 = {16} \) ,矛盾! 从而命题得证.

二、如图所示,在等腰 \( \bigtriangleup  {ABC} \) 中, \( {AB} = {AC} \) ,边 \( {AC} \) 上一点 \( D \) 及 \( {BC} \) 延长线上一点 \( E \) 满足 \( \frac{AD}{DC} = \frac{BC}{2CE} \) ,以 \( {AB} \) 为直径的圆 \( w \) 与线段 \( {DE} \) 交于一点 \( F \) . 证明: \( B,C,F,D \) 四点共圆. (答题时请将图画在答卷纸上)


<!-- Media -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_125.jpg?x=507&y=283&w=700&h=394&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

解析

如图,取 \( {BC} \) 中点 \( H \) ,则由 \( {AB} = {AC} \) 知 \( {AH}\bot {BC} \) ,故 \( H \) 在圆 \( w \) 上. 延长 \( {FD} \) 至 \( G \) ,使得 \( {AG}\parallel {BC} \) ,结合已知条件得, \( \frac{AG}{CE} = \frac{AD}{DC} = \frac{BC}{2CE} \) ,故 \( {AG} = \) \( \frac{1}{2}{BC} = {BH} = {HC} \) ,从而 \( {AGBH} \) 为矩形, \( {AGHC} \) 为平行四边形. 由 \( {AGBH} \) 为矩形知, \( G \) 亦在圆 \( w \) 上. 故 \( \angle {HGF} = \angle {HBF} \) . 又 \( {AGHC} \) 为平行四边形,由 \( {AC}\parallel {GH} \) , 得 \( \angle {CDF} = \angle {HGF} \) . 所以 \( \angle {CDF} = \angle {HBF} = \angle {CBF} \) ,故 \( B,C,F,D \) 四点共圆.

<!-- Media -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_125.jpg?x=509&y=1035&w=697&h=400&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

三、设集合 \( A = \{ 1,2,\cdots ,n\} ,X,Y \) 均为 \( A \) 的非空子集(允许 \( X = Y \) ). \( X \) 中的最大元与 \( Y \) 中的最小元分别记为 \( \max X,\min Y \) . 求满足 \( \max X > \min Y \) 的有序集合对(X,Y)的数目.

解析

先计算满足 \( \max X \leq  \min Y \) 的有序集合对(X,Y)的数目. 对给定的 \( m = \max X \) ,集合 \( X \) 是集合 \( \{ 1,2,\cdots ,m - 1\} \) 的任意一个子集与 \( \{ m\} \) 的并,故并有 \( {2}^{m - 1} \) 种取法. 又 \( \min Y \geq  M \) ,故 \( Y \) 是 \( \{ m,m + 1,\cdots ,n\} \) 的任意一个非空子集,共有 \( {2}^{n + 1 - m} - 1 \) 种取法. 因此,满足 \( \max X \leq  \min Y \) 的有序集合对(X,Y)的数目是

\( \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{m = 1}}^{n}{2}^{m - 1}\left( {{2}^{n + 1 - m} - 1}\right)  = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{m = 1}}^{n}{2}^{n} - \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{m = 1}}^{n}{2}^{m - 1} = n \cdot  {2}^{n} - {2}^{n} + 1 \) . 由于有序集合对(X,Y)


有 \( \left( {{2}^{n} - 1}\right)  \cdot  \left( {{2}^{n} - 1}\right)  = {\left( {2}^{n} - 1\right) }^{2} \) 个,于是满足 \( \max X > \min Y \) 的有序集合对(X,Y)的数目是 \( {\left( {2}^{n} - 1\right) }^{2} - n \cdot  {2}^{n} + {2}^{n} - 1 = {2}^{2n} - {2}^{n}\left( {n + 1}\right) \) .

四、给定整数 \( a \geq  2 \) . 证明: 对任意正整数 \( n \) ,存在正整数 \( k \) ,使得连续 \( n \) 个数 \( {a}^{k} + 1,{a}^{k} + \) \( 2,\cdots ,{a}^{k} + n \) 均是合数.

解析

设 \( {i}_{1} < {i}_{2} < \cdots  < {i}_{r} \) 是 \( 1,2,\cdots ,n \) 中与 \( a \) 互素的全体整数,则对 \( 1 \leq  i \leq  n,i \notin \) \( \left\{  {{i}_{1},{i}_{2},\cdots ,{i}_{r}}\right\} \) ,无论正整数 \( k \) 如何取值, \( {a}^{k} + i \) 均与 \( a \) 不互素且大于 \( a \) ,故 \( {a}^{k} + i \) 为合数.

对任意 \( j = 1,2,\cdots ,r \) ,因 \( a + {i}_{j} > 1 \) ,故 \( a + {i}_{j} \) 有素因子 \( {p}_{j} \) .

我们有 \( \left( {{p}_{j},a}\right)  = 1 \) (否则,因 \( {p}_{j} \) 是素数,故 \( {p}_{j} \mid  a \) ,但 \( {p}_{j} \mid  a + {i}_{j} \) ,从而 \( {p}_{j} \mid  {i}_{j} \) ,故 \( a,{i}_{j} \) 不互素,与 \( {i}_{j} \) 的取法矛盾). 因此,由费马小定理知, \( {a}^{{p}_{j} - 1} \equiv  1\left( {\;\operatorname{mod}\;{p}_{j}}\right) \) . 现取 \( k = \) \( \left( {{p}_{1} - 1}\right) \left( {{p}_{2} - 1}\right) \cdots \left( {{p}_{r} - 1}\right)  + 1 \) . 对任意 \( j = 1,2,\cdots ,r \) ,注意到 \( k \equiv  1\left( {\;\operatorname{mod}\;{p}_{j}}\right)  - 1 \) , 故有 \( {a}^{k} + {i}_{j} \equiv  a + {i}_{j} \equiv  0\left( {\;\operatorname{mod}\;{p}_{j}}\right) \) . 又 \( {a}^{k} + {i}_{j} > a + {i}_{j} \geq  {p}_{j} \) ,故 \( {a}^{k} + {i}_{j} \) 为合数.

综上所述,当 \( k = \left( {{p}_{1} - 1}\right) \left( {{p}_{2} - 1}\right) \cdots \left( {{p}_{r} - 1}\right)  + 1 \) 时, \( {a}^{k} + 1,{a}^{k} + 2,\cdots ,{a}^{k} + n \) 均是合数.


## 2017 年全国高中数学联赛一试答案 (A 卷)

## 一、 填空题: 本大题共 8 小题, 每小题 8 分, 满分 64 分.

1. 定义在 \( \mathbb{R} \) 上的函数 \( f\left( x\right) \) 对任意实数 \( x \) 有 \( f\left( {x + 3}\right)  \cdot  f\left( {x - 4}\right)  =  - 1 \) ,又当 \( 0 \leq  x < 7 \) 时,

\( f\left( x\right)  = {\log }_{2}\left( {9 - x}\right) \) ,则 \( f\left( {-{100}}\right) \) 的值为_____.

解析 \( - \frac{1}{2} \) .

根据题意, 有

\[f\left( {x + 7}\right)  =  - \frac{1}{f\left( x\right) },\]

进而可得

\[f\left( {x + {14}}\right)  = f\left( x\right) ,\]

于是

\[f\left( {-{100}}\right)  = f\left( {-2}\right)  =  - \frac{1}{f\left( 5\right) } =  - \frac{1}{{\log }_{2}\left( {9 - 5}\right) } =  - \frac{1}{2}.\]

2. 若实数 \( x,y \) 满足 \( {x}^{2} + 2\cos y = 1 \) ,则 \( x - \cos y \) 的取值范围是_____.

解析 \( \left\lbrack  {-1,\sqrt{3} + 1}\right\rbrack \) .

根据题意, 有

\[\cos y = \frac{1 - {x}^{2}}{2},\]

于是

\[x - \cos y = x - \frac{1 - {x}^{2}}{2} = \frac{1}{2}{x}^{2} + x - \frac{1}{2},\]

其中

\[ - 1 \leq  \frac{1 - {x}^{2}}{2} \leq  1\]

即 \( x \) 的取值范围是 \( \left\lbrack  {-\sqrt{3},\sqrt{3}}\right\rbrack \) . 因此所求的代数式取值范围是 \( \left\lbrack  {-1,\sqrt{3} + 1}\right\rbrack \) .

3. 在平面直角坐标系 \( {xOy} \) 中,椭圆 \( C \) 的方程为 \( \frac{{x}^{2}}{9} + \frac{{y}^{2}}{10} = 1,F \) 为 \( C \) 的上焦点, \( A \) 为 \( C \) 的右顶点, \( P \) 是 \( C \) 上位于第一象限内的动点,则四边形 \( {OAPF} \) 的面积的最大值为_____.


<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( y \) \( P \) \( \overrightarrow{Ax} \) \( F \) 0 -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_128.jpg?x=678&y=278&w=346&h=345&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

解析 \( \frac{3\sqrt{11}}{2} \) .

(1) 设 \( P\left( {3\cos \theta ,\sqrt{10}\sin \theta }\right) ,\theta  \in  \left( {0,\pi }\right) \) ,则四边形 \( {OAPF} \) 的面积

\[S = {S}_{\bigtriangleup {OAP}} + {S}_{\bigtriangleup {OFP}}\]

\[ = \frac{1}{2} \cdot  3 \cdot  \sqrt{10}\sin \theta  + \frac{1}{2} \cdot  1 \cdot  3\cos \theta \]

\[ = \frac{3}{2}\left( {\sqrt{10}\sin \theta  + \cos \theta }\right) \]

\[ \leq  \frac{3\sqrt{11}}{2}\]

等号当 \( \theta  = \arctan \frac{1}{\sqrt{10}} \) 时取得. 因此所求面积的最大值为 \( \frac{3\sqrt{11}}{2} \) .

( 2 )作仿射变换 \( \left( {{x}^{\prime },{y}^{\prime }}\right)  = \left( {x,\frac{3}{\sqrt{10}}y}\right) \) ,则 \( {A}^{\prime }\left( {3,0}\right) \) , \( {F}^{\prime }\left( {0,\frac{3}{\sqrt{10}}}\right) \) , \( O{P}^{\prime } = 3 \) ,且四边形 \( {OAPF} \) 的面积

\[{OAPF} = \frac{\sqrt{10}}{3} \cdot  O{A}^{\prime }{P}^{\prime }{F}^{\prime }\]

\[ \leq  \frac{\sqrt{10}}{3} \cdot  \frac{1}{2} \cdot  O{P}^{\prime } \cdot  {A}^{\prime }{F}^{\prime }\]

\[ = \frac{\sqrt{10}}{3} \cdot  \frac{1}{2} \cdot  3 \cdot  \sqrt{{3}^{2} + {\left( \frac{3}{\sqrt{10}}\right) }^{2}}\]

\[ = \frac{3\sqrt{11}}{2}\]

等号当 \( O{P}^{\prime } \bot  {A}^{\prime }{F}^{\prime } \) 时取得,因此所求面积的最大值为 \( \frac{3\sqrt{11}}{2} \) .

4. 若一个三位数中任意两个相邻数码的差均不超过 1 , 则称其为 “平稳数”. 平稳数的个数是 _____.

解析 75.

设平稳数为 \( \overline{abc} \) .


情形 1: \( b = 0 \) ,此时 \( a = 1,c \in  \{ 0,1\} \) ,有 \( 1 \cdot  2 = 2 \) 个平稳数.

情形 2: \( b = 1 \) ,此时 \( a \in  \{ 1,2\} ,c \in  \{ 0,1,2\} \) ,有 \( 2 \cdot  3 = 6 \) 个平稳数.

情形 3: \( b = k \) ,其中 \( k = 2,3,\cdots ,8 \) ,此时 \( a,c \in  \{ k - 1,k,k + 1\} \) ,有 \( 7 \cdot  3 \cdot  3 = {63} \) 个平稳数.

情形 4: \( b = 9 \) ,此时 \( a,c \in  \{ 8,9\} \) ,有 \( 2 \cdot  2 = 4 \) 个平稳数.

综上所述, 平稳数的个数为

\[2 + 6 + {63} + 4 = {75}.\]

5. 正三棱锥 \( P - {ABC} \) 中, \( {AB} = 1,{AP} = 2 \) ,过 \( {AB} \) 的平面 \( \alpha \) 将其体积平分,则棱 \( {PC} \) 与平面 \( \alpha \) 所成角的余弦值为 _____.

解析 \( \frac{3\sqrt{5}}{10} \) .

根据题意,平面 \( \alpha \) 与棱 \( {PC} \) 交于 \( {PC} \) 的中点 \( M \) ,设 \( N \) 为 \( {AB} \) 的中点,如图.

<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( B \) \( M \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_129.jpg?x=705&y=841&w=309&h=363&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

由平行四边形的性质可得

\[A{M}^{2} = \frac{1}{2}\left( {A{P}^{2} + A{C}^{2}}\right)  - \frac{1}{4}P{C}^{2} = \frac{3}{2},\]

进而

\[{MN} = \sqrt{A{M}^{2} - {\left( \frac{1}{2}AB\right) }^{2}} = \frac{\sqrt{5}}{2}.\]

由于 \( {CN} \) 过底面中心,因此平面 \( {PNC} \) 包含过 \( P \) 的底面垂线,因此 \( {PC} \) 在平面 \( \alpha \) 内的投影为 \( {MN} \) ,于是

\[\cos \langle {PC},{MN}\rangle  = \left| \frac{M{N}^{2} + M{C}^{2} - C{N}^{2}}{2 \cdot  {MN} \cdot  {MC}}\right|  = \frac{3\sqrt{5}}{10}.\]

6. 在平面直角坐标系 \( {xOy} \) 中,点集 \( K = \{ \left( {x,y}\right)  \mid  x,y =  - 1,0,1\} \) . 在 \( K \) 中随机取出三个点,则这三点中存在两点之间距离为 \( \sqrt{5} \) 的概率为_____.

解析 \( \frac{4}{7} \) .

如图,点集 \( K = \left\{  {O,{P}_{1},{P}_{2},{P}_{3},{P}_{4},{P}_{5},{P}_{6},{P}_{7},{P}_{8}}\right\} \) .


<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( \begin{matrix} {P}_{4} & {P}_{3} & {P}_{2} \\  {P}_{5} & {P}_{2} & {P}_{1} \\  {P}_{6} & {P}_{1} & {P}_{2} \end{matrix} \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_130.jpg?x=697&y=278&w=312&h=314&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

记 \( {P}_{k} = {P}_{k - 8},k \geq  9 \) ,则

\[{P}_{i}{P}_{i + 3} = \sqrt{5},i = 1,2,\cdots ,8.\]

选其中的一对点, 然后再从剩下的 7 个点中选一个, 共有 56 种选法. 其中形如

\[\left\{  {{P}_{i},{P}_{i + 3},{P}_{i + 6}}\right\}  ,i = 1,2,\cdots ,8\]

的三点组被计算了 2 次,因此满足条件的三点组共有 \( {56} - 8 = {48} \) 个,所求的概率为

\[\frac{48}{{\mathrm{C}}_{9}^{3}} = \frac{48}{84} = \frac{4}{7}\]

7. 在 \( \bigtriangleup {ABC} \) 中, \( M \) 是边 \( {BC} \) 的中点, \( N \) 是线段 \( {BM} \) 的中点. 若 \( A = \frac{\pi }{3},\bigtriangleup {ABC} \) 的面积为 \( \sqrt{3} \) ,则 \( \overrightarrow{AM} \cdot  \overrightarrow{AN} \) 的最小值为_____.

<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( B \) \( C \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_130.jpg?x=726&y=1222&w=266&h=241&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

解析 \( \sqrt{3} + 1 \) .

记 \( {AB} = c,{AC} = a \) ,则根据题意

\[{S}_{\bigtriangleup {ABC}} = \frac{1}{2} \cdot  \sin A \cdot  {bc} = \frac{\sqrt{3}}{4}{bc} = \sqrt{3},\]


于是 \( {bc} = 4 \) . 因此

\[\overrightarrow{AM} \cdot  \overrightarrow{AN} = \left( {\frac{1}{2}\overrightarrow{AB} + \frac{1}{2}\overrightarrow{AC}}\right)  \cdot  \left( {\frac{3}{4}\overrightarrow{AB} + \frac{1}{4}\overrightarrow{AC}}\right) \]

\[ = \frac{1}{8}\left( {{3A}{B}^{2} + A{C}^{2} + 4\overrightarrow{AB} \cdot  \overrightarrow{AC}}\right) \]

\[ = \frac{1}{8}\left( {3{c}^{2} + {b}^{2} + {2bc}}\right) \]

\[ \geq  \frac{1}{8}\left( {2\sqrt{3} + 2}\right) {bc}\]

\[ = \sqrt{3} + 1\text{,}\]

等号当 \( b = \sqrt{3}c \) 时取得,因此所求的最小值为 \( \sqrt{3} + 1 \) .

8. 设两个严格递增的正整数数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\}  ,\left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 满足: \( {a}_{10} = {b}_{10} < {2017} \) ,对任意正整数 \( n \) ,有 \( {a}_{n + 2} = {a}_{n + 1} + {a}_{n},{b}_{n + 1} = 2{b}_{n} \) ,则 \( {a}_{1} + {b}_{1} \) 的所有可能值为_____.

解析13,20.

考虑到 \( {2}^{10} = {1024} \) ,而

\[{b}_{10} = {2}^{9} \cdot  {b}_{1}\]

于是 \( {b}_{1} = 1,2,3 \) ,对应的 \( {b}_{10} = {512},{1024},{1536} \) . 而

\[{a}_{10} = {a}_{9} + {a}_{8} = 2{a}_{8} + {a}_{7} = \cdots  = {34}{a}_{2} + {21}{a}_{1},\]

因此

\[{21}{a}_{1} \equiv  2{b}_{1}\;\left( {\;\operatorname{mod}\;{34}}\right) ,\]

注意到

<!-- Media -->

<table><tr><td>\( {a}_{1} \)</td><td>2</td><td>4</td><td>6</td><td>8</td><td>10</td><td>12</td><td>14</td><td>16</td><td>18</td><td>20</td><td>22</td><td>24</td><td>26</td><td>28</td><td>30</td><td>32</td><td>34</td></tr><tr><td>\( {21}{a}_{1} \)(mod 34)</td><td>8</td><td>16</td><td>24</td><td>32</td><td>6</td><td>14</td><td>22</td><td>30</td><td>4</td><td>12</td><td>20</td><td>28</td><td>2</td><td>10</td><td>18</td><td>26</td><td>0</td></tr></table>

<!-- Media -->

于是 \( \left( {{a}_{1},{b}_{1},{a}_{2}}\right)  = \left( {{10},3,{39}}\right) ,\left( {{18},2,{19}}\right) \) . 因此所有可能的 \( {a}_{1} + {b}_{1} \) 的值为 13 和 20.

## 二、 解答题：本大题共 3 小题,满分 56 分. 解答应写出文字说明、证明过程或演算步骤. 其 中第 9 题满分 16 分, 第 10、11 题满分 20 分.

9. 设 \( k,m \) 为实数,不等式 \( \left| {{x}^{2} - {kx} - m}\right|  \leq  1 \) 对所有 \( x \in  \left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack \) 成立. 证明: \( b - a \leq  2\sqrt{2} \) . 解析

解法一:

根据题意, 有

\[\forall x \in  \left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack  ,{x}^{2} - 1 \leq  {kx} + m \leq  {x}^{2} + 1.\]

如图,考虑直线 \( y = {kx} + m \) 截图中阴影部分得到的线段在 \( x \) 轴上的投影长度. 不妨设 \( k \geq  0 \) . 分别记

\[{\Delta }_{1} = {k}^{2} + {4m} - 4,{\Delta }_{2} = {k}^{2} + {4m} + 4.\]


<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: 相切 相交 -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_132.jpg?x=715&y=278&w=278&h=345&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

情形 1: 直线 \( y = {kx} + m \) 与抛物线 \( y = {x}^{2} + 1 \) 相交,即 \( {\Delta }_{1} > 0 \) . 且有

\[b - a \leq  \left| {\frac{k + \sqrt{{\Delta }_{2}}}{2} - \frac{k + \sqrt{{\Delta }_{1}}}{2}}\right| \]

\[ = \frac{1}{2}\left| {\sqrt{{k}^{2} + {4m} + 4} - \sqrt{{k}^{2} + {4m} - 4}}\right| \]

\[ = \frac{4}{\sqrt{{k}^{2} + {4m} + 4} + \sqrt{{k}^{2} + {4m} - 4}}\]

\[ < \frac{4}{\sqrt{8} + \sqrt{0}}\]

\[ = \sqrt{2}\text{.}\]

情形 2: 直线 \( y = {kx} + m \) 与抛物线 \( y = {x}^{2} + 1 \) 相离且与抛物线 \( y = {x}^{2} - 1 \) 相交,此时将直线 \( y = {kx} + m \) 向上平移,直至与抛物线 \( y = {x}^{2} + 1 \) 相切可以使得线段投影长度增大, 因此此时无法取得最大值.

情形 3: 直线 \( y = {kx} + m \) 与抛物线 \( y = {x}^{2} + 1 \) 相切,即 \( {\Delta }_{1} = 0 \) . 此时

\[b - a \leq  \frac{2\sqrt{{\Delta }_{2}}}{2} = 2\sqrt{2}.\]

综上所述, 原命题得证. 解法二:

根据题意, 有

\[\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \left| {{b}^{2} - {kb} - m}\right|  \leq  1, \\  \left| {{a}^{2} - {ka} - m}\right|  \leq  1, \\  \left| {{\left( \frac{b + a}{2}\right) }^{2} - k \cdot  \frac{b + a}{2} - m}\right|  \leq  1, \end{array}\right. \]

于是

\[{\left( b - a\right) }^{2} \leq  2\left| {{b}^{2} - {kb} - m}\right|  + 2\left| {{a}^{2} - {ka} - m}\right|  + 4\left| {{\left( \frac{b + a}{2}\right) }^{2} - k \cdot  \frac{b + a}{2} - m}\right|  \leq  8,\]

于是原命题得证.


10. 设 \( {x}_{1},{x}_{2},{x}_{3} \) 是非负实数,满足 \( {x}_{1} + {x}_{2} + {x}_{3} = 1 \) ,求 \( \left( {{x}_{1} + 3{x}_{2} + 5{x}_{3}}\right) \left( {{x}_{1} + \frac{{x}_{2}}{3} + \frac{{x}_{3}}{5}}\right) \) 的最小值和最大值.

解析 最小值为 1,最大值为 \( \frac{9}{5} \) .

解法一:

设题中代数式为 \( M \) ,则

\[M = {x}_{1}^{2} + {x}_{2}^{2} + {x}_{3}^{2} + \frac{10}{3}{x}_{1}{x}_{2} + \frac{34}{15}{x}_{2}{x}_{3} + \frac{26}{5}{x}_{3}{x}_{1}\]

\[ = {\left( {x}_{1} + {x}_{2} + {x}_{3}\right) }^{2} + \frac{4}{15}\left( {5{x}_{1}{x}_{2} + {x}_{2}{x}_{3} + {12}{x}_{3}{x}_{1}}\right) \]

\[ = 1 + \frac{4}{15}\left( {5{x}_{1}{x}_{2} + {x}_{2}{x}_{3} + {12}{x}_{3}{x}_{1}}\right) .\]

一方面, 有

\[5{x}_{1}{x}_{2} + {x}_{2}{x}_{3} + {12}{x}_{3}{x}_{1} \geq  0,\]

等号当 \( \left( {{x}_{1},{x}_{2},{x}_{3}}\right)  = \left( {1,0,0}\right) \) 时取得,因此 \( M \) 的最小值为 1 .

另一方面, 有

\[5{x}_{1}{x}_{2} + {x}_{2}{x}_{3} + {12}{x}_{3}{x}_{1} \leq  6{x}_{1}{x}_{2} + 6{x}_{2}{x}_{3} + 6{x}_{3}{x}_{1} + 3{x}_{3}^{2} + 3{x}_{1}^{2}\]

\[ \leq  3{\left( {x}_{1} + {x}_{2} + {x}_{3}\right) }^{2}\]

\[ = 3\text{,}\]

等号当 \( \left( {{x}_{1},{x}_{2},{x}_{3}}\right)  = \left( {\frac{1}{2},0,\frac{1}{2}}\right) \) 时取得,因此 \( M \) 的最大值为 \( \frac{9}{5} \) .

解法二:

设题中代数式为 \( M \) ,则

\[M = {x}_{1}^{2} + {x}_{2}^{2} + {x}_{3}^{2} + \frac{10}{3}{x}_{1}{x}_{2} + \frac{34}{15}{x}_{2}{x}_{3} + \frac{26}{5}{x}_{3}{x}_{1} \geq  {\left( {x}_{1} + {x}_{2} + {x}_{3}\right) }^{2} = 1,\]

等号当 \( \left( {{x}_{1},{x}_{2},{x}_{3}}\right)  = \left( {1,0,0}\right) \) 时取得,因此 \( M \) 的最小值为 1 .

另一方面, 有

\( {5M} = \left( {{x}_{1} + 3{x}_{2} + 5{x}_{3}}\right) \left( {5{x}_{1} + \frac{5}{3}{x}_{2} + {x}_{3}}\right)  \leq  {\left( 3{x}_{1} + \frac{7}{3}{x}_{2} + 3{x}_{3}\right) }^{2} \leq  {\left( 3{x}_{1} + 3{x}_{2} + 3{x}_{3}\right) }^{2}, \)

等号当 \( \left( {{x}_{1},{x}_{2},{x}_{3}}\right)  = \left( {\frac{1}{2},0,\frac{1}{2}}\right) \) 时取得,因此 \( M \) 的最大值为 \( \frac{9}{5} \) .

11. 设复数 \( {z}_{1},{z}_{2} \) 满足 \( \operatorname{Re}\left( {z}_{1}\right)  > 0,\operatorname{Re}\left( {z}_{2}\right)  > 0 \) ,且 \( \operatorname{Re}\left( {z}_{1}^{2}\right)  = \operatorname{Re}\left( {z}_{2}^{2}\right)  = 2 \) ,其中 \( \operatorname{Re}\left( z\right) \) 表示复数 \( z \) 的实部.

(1)求 \( \operatorname{Re}\left( {{z}_{1}{z}_{2}}\right) \) 的最小值；

( 2 )求 \( \left| {{z}_{1} + 2}\right|  + \left| {\overline{{z}_{2}} + 2}\right|  - \left| {\overline{{z}_{1}} - {z}_{2}}\right| \) 的最小值.


解析 (1)2;

(2) \( 4\sqrt{2} \) .

( 1 )设 \( {z}_{k} = {x}_{k} + \mathrm{i}{y}_{k},k = 1,2 \) . 根据题意,有 \( {x}_{1},{x}_{2} > 0 \) ,且

\[{x}_{1}^{2} - {y}_{1}^{2} = {x}_{2}^{2} - {y}_{2}^{2} = 2.\]

于是 \( {P}_{1}\left( {{x}_{1},{y}_{2}}\right) \) 和 \( {P}_{2}\left( {{x}_{2},{y}_{2}}\right) \) 都是双曲线 \( H : {x}^{2} - {y}^{2} = 2 \) 右支上的点. 而

\[\operatorname{Re}\left( {{z}_{1}{z}_{2}}\right)  = {x}_{1}{x}_{2} - {y}_{1}{y}_{2}\]

\[ = \sqrt{{y}_{1}^{2} + 2} \cdot  \sqrt{{y}_{2}^{2} + 2} - {y}_{1}{y}_{2}\]

\[ = \sqrt{{y}_{1}^{2}{y}_{2}^{2} + 2{y}_{1}^{2} + 2{y}_{2}^{2} + 4} - {y}_{1}{y}_{2}\]

\[ \geq  \sqrt{{y}_{1}^{2}{y}_{2}^{2} + 4{y}_{1}{y}_{2} + 4} - {y}_{1}{y}_{2}\]

\[ = \left| {{y}_{1}{y}_{2} + 2}\right|  - {y}_{1}{y}_{2}\]

\[ \geq  2\text{,}\]

等号当 \( {y}_{1} = {y}_{2} \) 时取得. 因此所求的最小值为 2 .

(2) 由共轭复数的性质, 有
