\[m = \left| {{z}_{1} + 2}\right|  + \left| {\overline{{z}_{2}} + 2}\right|  - \left| {\overline{{z}_{1}} - {z}_{2}}\right|  = \left| {{z}_{1} - \left( {-2}\right) }\right|  + \left| {\overline{{z}_{2}} - \left( {-2}\right) }\right|  - \left| {{z}_{1} - \overline{{z}_{2}}}\right| ,\]

记 \( {F}_{1}\left( {-2,0}\right) ,{F}_{2}\left( {2,0}\right) \) 为双曲线 \( H \) 的左、右焦点, \( {P}_{2}^{\prime } \) 为 \( {P}_{2} \) 关于 \( x \) 轴的对称点 (该点仍然在双曲线 \( H \) 上),于是

\[m = \left| {{P}_{1}{F}_{1}}\right|  + \left| {{P}_{2}^{\prime }{F}_{1}}\right|  - \left| {{P}_{1}{P}_{2}^{\prime }}\right|  = 2\sqrt{2} + \left| {{P}_{1}{F}_{2}}\right|  + 2\sqrt{2} + \left| {{P}_{2}^{\prime }{F}_{2}}\right|  - \left| {{P}_{1}{P}_{2}^{\prime }}\right|  \geq  4\sqrt{2},\]

等号当 \( {F}_{2} \) 在线段 \( {P}_{1}{P}_{2}^{\prime } \) 时取得. 因此所求的最小值为 \( 4\sqrt{2} \) .


## 2017 年全国高中数学联赛二试答案 (A 卷)

一、如图,在 \( \bigtriangleup  {ABC} \) 中, \( {AB} = {AC} \) , \( I \) 为 \( \bigtriangleup  {ABC} \) 的内心. 以 \( A \) 为圆心, \( {AB} \) 为半径作圆 \( {\Gamma }_{1} \) ,以 \( I \) 为圆心, \( {IB} \) 为半径作圆 \( {\Gamma }_{2} \) ,过点 \( B,I \) 的圆 \( {\Gamma }_{3} \) 与 \( {\Gamma }_{1},{\Gamma }_{2} \) 分别交于点 \( P,Q \) (不同于点 \( B \) ). 设 \( {IP} \) 与 \( {BQ} \) 交于点 \( R \) . 证明: \( {BR} \bot  {CR} \) .

<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( B \) \( P \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_135.jpg?x=671&y=650&w=374&h=440&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

解析

如图,连接 \( {IB},{IC},{IQ},{PB},{PC} \) .

<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( B \) \( R \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_135.jpg?x=670&y=1242&w=377&h=443&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

由于点 \( Q \) 在圆 \( {\Gamma }_{2} \) 上,故 \( {IB} = {IQ} \) ,所以

\[\angle {IBQ} = \angle {IQB}\text{.}\]

又 \( B,I,P,Q \) 四点共圆,所以 \( \angle {IQB} = \angle {IPB} \) ,于是 \( \angle {IBQ} = \angle {IPB} \) ,故 \( \bigtriangleup  {IBP} \) 与


\( \bigtriangleup {IRB} \) 相似,从而有 \( \angle {IRB} = \angle {IBP} \) ,且

\[\frac{IB}{IR} = \frac{IP}{IB}\]

注意到 \( {AB} = {AC} \) ,且 \( I \) 为 \( \bigtriangleup {ABC} \) 的内心,故 \( {IB} = {IC} \) ,所以

\[\frac{IC}{IR} = \frac{IP}{IC},\]

于是 \( \bigtriangleup  {ICP} \) 与 \( \bigtriangleup  {IRC} \) 相似,故

\[\angle {IRC} = \angle {ICP}\text{.}\]

又点 \( P \) 在圆 \( {\Gamma }_{1} \) 的弧 \( {BC} \) 上,故

\[\angle {BPC} = {180}^{ \circ  } - \frac{1}{2}\angle A,\]

因此

\[\angle {BRC} = \angle {IRB} + \angle {IRC}\]

\[ = \angle {IBP} + \angle {ICP}\]

\[ = {360}^{ \circ  } - \left( {{90}^{ \circ  } + \frac{1}{2}\angle A}\right)  - \left( {{180}^{ \circ  } - \frac{1}{2}\angle A}\right) \]

\[ = {90}^{ \circ  }\text{,}\]

故 \( {BR} \bot  {CR} \) .

二、设数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 定义为 \( {a}_{1} = 1 \) ,

\[{a}_{n + 1} = \left\{  {\begin{array}{ll} {a}_{n} + n, & {a}_{n} \leq  n, \\  {a}_{n} - n, & {a}_{n} > n, \end{array}n = 1,2,\cdots .}\right. \]

求满足 \( {a}_{r} < r \leq  {3}^{2017} \) 的正整数 \( r \) 的个数.

解析 \( \frac{{3}^{2017} - {2019}}{2} \) .

先计算数列的前几项:

<!-- Media -->

<table><tr><td>\( n \)</td><td>1</td><td>2</td><td>3</td><td>4</td><td>5</td><td>6</td><td>7</td><td>8</td><td>9</td><td>10</td><td>11</td><td>12</td><td>13</td><td>14</td><td>15</td><td>16</td></tr><tr><td>\( {a}_{n} \)</td><td>1</td><td>2</td><td>4</td><td>1</td><td>5</td><td>10</td><td>4</td><td>11</td><td>3</td><td>12</td><td>2</td><td>13</td><td>1</td><td>14</td><td>28</td><td>13</td></tr><tr><td/><td>=</td><td>-</td><td>></td><td><</td><td>-</td><td>></td><td><</td><td>></td><td><</td><td>></td><td><</td><td>></td><td><</td><td>-</td><td>></td><td><</td></tr></table>

<!-- Media -->

归纳出

引理: 若 \( {a}_{r} = r \) ,则对 \( k = 1,2,\cdots ,r - 1 \) ,有

\[{a}_{r + {2k} - 1} = {2r} + k - 1 > r + {2k} - 1,\]

\[{a}_{r + {2k}} = r - k < r + {2k}.\]


对 \( k \) 进行归纳证明.

归纳基础: 当 \( k = 1 \) 时,由于 \( {a}_{r} = r \leq  r \) ,根据定义,有

\[{a}_{r + 1} = {a}_{r} + r = {2r} > r + 1,\]

\[{a}_{r + 2} = {a}_{r + 1} - \left( {r + 1}\right)  = r - 1 < r + 2,\]

命题成立.

推理证明: 假设对某个 \( k\left( {1 \leq  k < r - 1}\right) \) 成立,则由定义

\[{a}_{r + {2k} + 1} = {a}_{r + {2k}} + \left( {r + {2k}}\right)  = {2r} + k > r + {2k} + 1,\]

\[{a}_{r + {2k} + 2} = {a}_{r + {2k} + 1} - \left( {r + {2k} + 1}\right)  = r - k - 1 < r + {2k} + 2,\]

于是命题对 \( k + 1 \) 也成立.

综上所述, 引理得证.

根据引理,将所有满足 \( {a}_{r} = r \) 的正整数 \( r \) 从小到大排列为

\[{r}_{1},{r}_{2},\cdots ,{r}_{n},\cdots ,\]

则有

\[{r}_{n + 1} = 3{r}_{n} - 1,n = 1,2,\cdots .\]

利用不动点法容易求得

\[{r}_{n} = \frac{1}{2} \cdot  {3}^{n - 1} + \frac{1}{2},n \in  {\mathbb{N}}^{ * }.\]

由于

\[{r}_{2018} = \frac{{3}^{2017} + 1}{2} < {3}^{2017} < \frac{{3}^{2018} + 1}{2} = {r}_{2019},\]

于是不超过 \( {3}^{2017} \) 的正整数被如下分段

\[{r}_{1},{r}_{2},\cdots ,{r}_{3},\cdots ,{r}_{4},\cdots ,\cdots ,\cdots ,{r}_{2017},\cdots ,{r}_{2018},\cdots ,{3}^{2017},\]

其中在 \( {r}_{k} \) 和 \( {r}_{k + 1} \) 之间的数恰有一半满足 \( {a}_{r} < r \) ,在 \( {r}_{2018} \) (这是一个偶数) 到 \( {3}^{2017} \) 中所有的偶数 \( r \) 均满足 \( {a}_{r} < r \) ,所有奇数 \( r \) 均满足 \( {a}_{r} > r \) . 因此满足条件的正整数 \( r \) 的

个数为

\[\frac{1}{2}\left( {{3}^{2017} - {2018} - 1}\right)  = \frac{{3}^{2017} - {2019}}{2}.\]

三、 将 \( {33} \times  {33} \) 方格纸中每个小方格染三种颜色之一,使得每种颜色的小方格的个数相等. 若相邻两个小方格的颜色不同, 则称它们的公共边为 “分隔边”. 试求分隔边条数的最小值.

解析 56.

如图,分隔边的条数 \( L = {56} \) . 下面证明 \( L \geq  {56} \) . 将方格纸的行从上至下依次记为 \( {A}_{1},{A}_{2},\cdots ,{A}_{33} \) ,列从左至右依次记为 \( {B}_{1},{B}_{2},\cdots ,{B}_{33} \) . 行 \( {A}_{i} \) 中方格出现的颜色数记为 \( n\left( {A}_{i}\right) \) ,列 \( {B}_{i} \) 中方格出现的颜色数记为 \( n\left( {B}_{i}\right) \) ,三种颜色分别记为 \( {c}_{1},{c}_{2},{c}_{3} \) ,对于一种颜色 \( {c}_{j} \) ,设 \( n\left( {c}_{j}\right) \) 是含有 \( {c}_{j} \) 色方格的行数与列数之和. 若 \( {A}_{i} \) 行中含有 \( {c}_{j} \) 色的方格,则记 \( \delta \left( {{A}_{i},{c}_{j}}\right) \) 为 1,否则记 \( \delta \left( {{A}_{i},{c}_{j}}\right) \) 为 0 . 类似的定义 \( \delta \left( {{B}_{i},{c}_{j}}\right) \) ,于是


\[\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{{33}}\left( {n\left( {A}_{i}\right)  + n\left( {B}_{i}\right) }\right)  = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{{33}}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{j = 1}}^{3}\left( {\delta \left( {{A}_{i},{c}_{j}}\right)  + \delta \left( {{B}_{i},{c}_{j}}\right) }\right) \]

\[ = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{j = 1}}^{3}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{{33}}\left( {\delta \left( {{A}_{i},{c}_{j}}\right)  + \delta \left( {{B}_{j},{c}_{j}}\right) }\right) \]

\[ = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{j = 1}}^{3}n\left( {c}_{j}\right) ,\]

<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: 16 17 11 11 11 11 11 11 33 -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_138.jpg?x=614&y=276&w=492&h=473&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

由于染 \( {c}_{j} \) 色的方格数为

\[\frac{1}{3} \cdot  {33}^{2} = {363}\]

设含有 \( {c}_{j} \) 色方格的行有 \( a \) 个,列有 \( b \) 个,则 \( {c}_{j} \) 色方格一定在这 \( a \) 行和 \( b \) 列的交叉方格中, 因此

\[{ab} \geq  {363},\]

从而

\[n\left( {c}_{j}\right)  = a + b \geq  2\sqrt{ab} > 2\sqrt{363} > {38},\]

故

\[n\left( {c}_{j}\right)  \geq  {39},j = 1,2,3.\]


由于在行 \( {A}_{i} \) 中有 \( n\left( {A}_{i}\right) \) 种颜色的方格,因此至少有 \( n\left( {A}_{i}\right)  - 1 \) 条分割边,同理在列 \( {B}_{i} \) 中,至少有 \( n\left( {B}_{i}\right)  - 1 \) 条分割边,于是

\[L \geq  \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{{33}}\left( {n\left( {A}_{i}\right)  - 1}\right)  + \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{{33}}\left( {n\left( {B}_{i}\right)  - 1}\right) \]

\[ = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{{33}}\left( {n\left( {A}_{i}\right)  + n\left( {B}_{i}\right) }\right)  - {66}\]

\[ = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{j = 1}}^{3}n\left( {c}_{j}\right)  - {66}.\]

下面分两种情形讨论.

情形 1: 有一行或一列全部方格同色. 不妨设有一行全部为 \( {c}_{1} \) 色,从而方格纸的 33 列中均含有 \( {c}_{1} \) 色的方格,由于 \( {c}_{1} \) 色方格有 363 个,故至少有 11 行中含有 \( {c}_{1} \) 色方格,于是

\[n\left( {c}_{1}\right)  \geq  {11} + {33} = {44},\]

于是

\[L \geq  n\left( {c}_{1}\right)  + n\left( {c}_{2}\right)  + n\left( {c}_{3}\right)  - {66} \geq  {44} + {39} + {39} - {66} = {56}.\]

情形 2: 没有一行也没有一列的全部方格同色,则对任意 \( 1 \leq  i \leq  {33} \) ,具有 \( n\left( {A}_{i}\right)  \geq  2 \) , \( n\left( {B}_{i}\right)  \geq  2 \) ,从而可得

\[L \geq  \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{{33}}\left( {n\left( {A}_{i}\right)  + n\left( {B}_{i}\right) }\right)  - {66} \geq  {33} \cdot  4 - {66} = {66}.\]

综上所述, 分隔边条数的最小值为 56 .

四、设 \( m,n \) 均是大于 1 的整数, \( m \geq  n.{a}_{1},{a}_{2},\cdots ,{a}_{n} \) 是 \( n \) 个不超过 \( m \) 的互不相同的正整数,且 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},\cdots ,{a}_{n} \) 互素. 证明: 对任意实数 \( x \) ,均存在一个 \( i\left( {1 \leq  i \leq  n}\right) \) ,使得 \( \begin{Vmatrix}{{a}_{i}x}\end{Vmatrix} \geq  \frac{2}{m\left( {m + 1}\right) }\parallel x\parallel \) ,这里 \( \parallel y\parallel \) 表示实数 \( y \) 到与它最近的整数的距离.

解析

首先证明以下两个结论.

结论一: 存在整数 \( {c}_{1},{c}_{2},\cdots ,{c}_{n} \) ,满足

\[{c}_{1}{a}_{1} + {c}_{2}{a}_{2} + \cdots  + {c}_{n}{a}_{n} = 1,\]

并且 \( \left| {c}_{i}\right|  \leq  m,1 \leq  i \leq  n \) .

证明: 由于 \( \left( {{a}_{1},{a}_{2},\cdots ,{a}_{n}}\right)  = 1 \) ,由裴蜀定理,存在正整数 \( {c}_{1},{c}_{2},\cdots ,{c}_{n} \) 满足

\[{c}_{1}{a}_{1} + {c}_{2}{a}_{2} + \cdots  + {c}_{n}{a}_{n} = 1.\]


下面证明,通过调整,存在一组 \( {c}_{1},{c}_{2},\cdots ,{c}_{n} \) 满足上式,且绝对值均不超过 \( m \) . 记

\[{S}_{1} = {S}_{1}\left( {{c}_{1},{c}_{2},\cdots ,{c}_{n}}\right)  = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{{c}_{i} > m}}{c}_{i} \geq  0,\]

\[{S}_{2} = {S}_{2}\left( {{c}_{1},{c}_{2},\cdots ,{c}_{n}}\right)  = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{{c}_{i} <  - m}}\left| {c}_{i}\right|  \geq  0,\]

如果 \( {S}_{1} > 0 \) ,那么存在 \( {c}_{i} > m > 1 \) ,于是 \( {c}_{i}{a}_{i} > 1 \) ,又因为 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},\cdots ,{a}_{n} \) 均为正数,故由上式可知存在 \( {c}_{j} < 0 \) . 令

\[\left( {{c}_{i}^{\prime },{c}_{j}^{\prime },{c}_{k}^{\prime }}\right)  = \left( {{c}_{i} - {a}_{j},{c}_{j} + {a}_{i},{c}_{k}}\right) ,\]

其中 \( 1 \leq  k \leq  n,k \neq  i,j \) ,则

\[{c}_{1}^{\prime }{a}_{1} + {c}_{2}^{\prime }{a}_{2} + \cdots  + {c}_{n}^{\prime }{a}_{n} = 1,\]

并且

\[0 \leq  m - {a}_{j} < {c}_{i}^{\prime } < {c}_{i},{c}_{j} < {c}_{j}^{\prime } < {a}_{i} \leq  m,\]

因为 \( {c}_{i}^{\prime } < {c}_{i} \) ,且 \( {c}_{j}^{\prime } < m \) ,所以

\[{S}_{1}\left( {{c}_{1}^{\prime },{c}_{2}^{\prime },\cdots ,{c}_{n}^{\prime }}\right)  < {S}_{1}\left( {{c}_{1},{c}_{2},\cdots ,{c}_{n}}\right) .\]

又 \( {c}_{j}^{\prime } > {c}_{j} \) 及 \( {c}_{i}^{\prime } > 0 \) ,故

\[{S}_{2}\left( {{c}_{1}^{\prime },{c}_{2}^{\prime },\cdots ,{c}_{n}^{\prime }}\right)  \leq  {S}_{2}\left( {{c}_{1},{c}_{2},\cdots ,{c}_{n}}\right) .\]

如果 \( {S}_{2} > 0 \) ,那么存在 \( {c}_{j} <  - m \) ,因此有一个 \( {c}_{i} > 0 \) . 令

\[\left( {{c}_{i}^{\prime },{c}_{j}^{\prime },{c}_{k}^{\prime }}\right)  = \left( {{c}_{i} - {a}_{j},{c}_{j} + {a}_{i},{c}_{k}}\right) ,\]

其中 \( 1 \leq  k \leq  n,k \neq  i,j \) ,那么

\[{c}_{1}^{\prime }{a}_{1} + {c}_{2}^{\prime }{a}_{2} + \cdots  + {c}_{n}^{\prime }{a}_{n} = 1\]

成立, 并且

\[ - m < {c}_{i}^{\prime } < {c}_{i},{c}_{j} < {c}_{j}^{\prime } < 0.\]

与上面类似地可知

\[{S}_{1}\left( {{c}_{1}^{\prime },{c}_{2}^{\prime },\cdots ,{c}_{n}^{\prime }}\right)  \leq  {S}_{1}\left( {{c}_{1},{c}_{2},\cdots ,{c}_{n}}\right) ,\]

且

\[{S}_{2}\left( {{c}_{1}^{\prime },{c}_{2}^{\prime },\cdots ,{c}_{n}^{\prime }}\right)  < {S}_{2}\left( {{c}_{1},{c}_{2},\cdots ,{c}_{n}}\right) .\]

因为 \( {S}_{1},{S}_{2} \) 均为非负整数,故通过有限次上述的调整,可得到一组 \( {c}_{1},{c}_{2},\cdots ,{c}_{n} \) 使得

\[{c}_{1}{a}_{1} + {c}_{2}{a}_{2} + \cdots  + {c}_{n}{a}_{n} = 1,\]


并且 \( \left| {c}_{i}\right|  \leq  m,1 \leq  i \leq  n \) . 且 \( {S}_{1} = {S}_{2} = 0 \) ,结论一获证.

结论二: 对任意实数 \( a,b \) ,均有

\[\parallel a + b\parallel  \leq  \parallel a\parallel  + \parallel b\parallel .\]

对任意整数 \( u \) 和实数 \( y \) ,均有

\[\parallel {uy}\parallel  \leq  \left| u\right|  \cdot  \parallel y\parallel .\]

证明: 由于对任意整数 \( u \) 和实数 \( x \) ,有

\[\parallel x + u\parallel  = \parallel x\parallel \]

故不妨设 \( a,b \in  \left\lbrack  {-\frac{1}{2},\frac{1}{2}}\right\rbrack \) ,此时

\[\parallel a\parallel  = \left| a\right| ,\parallel b\parallel  = \left| b\right| .\]

因为 \( \parallel x\parallel  \leq  \left| x\right| \) ,所以

\[\parallel a + b\parallel  \leq  \left| {a + b}\right|  \leq  \left| a\right|  + \left| b\right|  = \parallel a\parallel  + \parallel b\parallel ,\]

多次使用该结论有 \( \parallel {uy}\parallel  \leq  \left| u\right|  \cdot  \parallel y\parallel \) ,于是结论二获证.

回到原题: 由结论一,存在整数 \( {c}_{1},{c}_{2},\cdots ,{c}_{n} \) ,使得

\[{c}_{1}{a}_{1} + {c}_{2}{a}_{2} + \cdots  + {c}_{n}{a}_{n} = 1,\]

并且 \( \left| {c}_{i}\right|  \leq  m,1 \leq  i \leq  n \) ,于是

\[\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}{c}_{i}{a}_{i}x = x.\]

利用结论二得

\[\parallel x\parallel  = \begin{Vmatrix}{\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}{c}_{i}{a}_{i}x}\end{Vmatrix}\]

\[ \leq  \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}\begin{Vmatrix}{{c}_{i}\left| \cdot \right| \begin{Vmatrix}{{a}_{i}x}\end{Vmatrix}}\end{Vmatrix}\]

\[ \leq  m\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}\begin{Vmatrix}{{a}_{i}x}\end{Vmatrix}\]

\[ \leq  {mn} \cdot  \mathop{\max }\limits_{{1 \leq  i \leq  n}}\begin{Vmatrix}{{a}_{i}x}\end{Vmatrix},\]

因此

\[\mathop{\max }\limits_{{1 \leq  i \leq  n}}\begin{Vmatrix}{{a}_{i}x}\end{Vmatrix} \geq  \frac{1}{mn}\parallel x\parallel .\]


若 \( n \leq  \frac{1}{2}\left( {m + 1}\right) \) ,则

\[\mathop{\max }\limits_{{1 \leq  i \leq  n}}\begin{Vmatrix}{{a}_{i}x}\end{Vmatrix} \geq  \frac{\parallel x\parallel }{mn} \geq  \frac{2\parallel x\parallel }{m\left( {m + 1}\right) }.\]

若 \( n > \frac{1}{2}\left( {m + 1}\right) \) ,则在 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},\cdots ,{a}_{n} \) 中存在两个相邻正整数,不妨设 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2} \) 相邻,则

\[\parallel x\parallel  = \begin{Vmatrix}{{a}_{2}x - {a}_{1}x}\end{Vmatrix} \leq  \begin{Vmatrix}{{a}_{2}x}\end{Vmatrix} + \begin{Vmatrix}{{a}_{1}x}\end{Vmatrix},\]

故

\[\max \left\{  {\begin{Vmatrix}{{a}_{1}x}\end{Vmatrix},\begin{Vmatrix}{{a}_{2}x}\end{Vmatrix}}\right\}   \geq  \frac{\parallel x\parallel }{2} \geq  \frac{2\parallel x\parallel }{m\left( {m + 1}\right) }.\]

综上所述,总存在一个 \( i\left( {1 \leq  i \leq  n}\right) \) ,满足

\[\begin{Vmatrix}{{a}_{i}x}\end{Vmatrix} \geq  \frac{2}{m\left( {m + 1}\right) }\parallel x\parallel \]

命题得证.


## 2017 年全国高中数学联赛一试答案 (B 卷)

## 一、 填空题: 本大题共 8 小题, 每小题 8 分, 满分 64 分.

1. 在等比数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 中, \( {a}_{2} = \sqrt{2},{a}_{3} = \sqrt[3]{3} \) ,则 \( \frac{{a}_{1} + {a}_{2011}}{{a}_{7} + {a}_{2017}} \) 的值为_____.

解析 \( \frac{8}{9} \) .

根据题意, 有

\[\frac{{a}_{1} + {a}_{2011}}{{a}_{7} + {a}_{2017}} = \frac{{a}_{1}}{{a}_{7}} = {\left( \frac{{a}_{2}}{{a}_{3}}\right) }^{6} = \frac{8}{9}.\]

2. 设复数 \( z \) 满足 \( z + 9 = {10}\bar{z} + {22}\mathrm{i} \) ,则 \( \left| z\right| \) 的值为_____.

解析 \( \sqrt{5} \) .

根据题意, 有

\[z - {10}\bar{z} =  - 9 + {22}\mathrm{i},\]

于是

\[\bar{z} - {10z} =  - 9 - {22}\mathrm{i},\]

两式相加可得

\[ - 9\left( {z + \bar{z}}\right)  =  - {18}\operatorname{Re}\left( z\right)  =  - {18},\]

两式相减可得

\[{11}\left( {z - \bar{z}}\right)  = {22}\operatorname{Im}\left( z\right) \mathrm{i} = {44}\mathrm{i},\]

因此

\[\left| z\right|  = \sqrt{{\operatorname{Re}}^{2}\left( z\right)  + {\operatorname{Im}}^{2}\left( z\right) } = \sqrt{{1}^{2} + {2}^{2}} = \sqrt{5}.\]

3. 设 \( f\left( x\right) \) 是定义在 \( \mathbb{R} \) 上的函数,若 \( f\left( x\right)  + {x}^{2} \) 是奇函数, \( f\left( x\right)  + {2}^{x} \) 是偶函数,则 \( f\left( 1\right) \) 的值是_____. 解析 \( - \frac{7}{4} \) .

根据题意, 有

\[\left\{  \begin{array}{l} f\left( 1\right)  + 1 =  - \left\lbrack  {f\left( {-1}\right)  + 1}\right\rbrack  , \\  f\left( 1\right)  + 2 = f\left( {-1}\right)  + {2}^{-1}, \end{array}\right. \]

解得

\[f\left( 1\right)  =  - \frac{7}{4},f\left( {-1}\right)  =  - \frac{1}{4}.\]


4. 在 \( \bigtriangleup  {ABC} \) 中,若 \( \sin A = 2\sin C \) ,且三条边 \( a,b,c \) 成等比数列,则 \( \cos A \) 的值是_____. 解析 \( - \frac{\sqrt{2}}{4} \) .

由正弦定理, 可得

\[\frac{a}{c} = \frac{\sin A}{\sin C} = 2\]

又 \( a,b,c \) 成等比数列,于是

\[\left( {a,b,c}\right)  = \left( {{2c},\sqrt{2}c,c}\right) .\]

因此根据余弦定理, 有

\[\cos A = \frac{{b}^{2} + {c}^{2} - {a}^{2}}{2bc} = \frac{{\left( \sqrt{2}c\right) }^{2} + {c}^{2} - {\left( 2c\right) }^{2}}{2 \cdot  \sqrt{2}c \cdot  c} =  - \frac{\sqrt{2}}{4}.\]

5. 在正四面体 \( {ABCD} \) 中, \( E,F \) 分别在棱 \( {AB},{AC} \) 上,满足 \( {BE} = 3,{EF} = 4 \) ,且 \( {EF} \) 与面 \( {BCD} \) 平行,则 \( \bigtriangleup  {DEF} \) 的面积为_____.

解析 \( 2\sqrt{33} \) .

过 \( D \) 作 \( {EF} \) 的垂线,垂足为 \( H \) ,如图.

<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( A \) \( \underline{F} \) \( C \) \( B \) \( E \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_144.jpg?x=704&y=955&w=309&h=321&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

由线面平行的性质定理, \( {EF}\parallel {BC} \) ,因此

\[{AE} = {EF} = {FA} = 4,\]

于是

\[D{E}^{2} = A{D}^{2} + A{E}^{2} - 2 \cdot  {AD} \cdot  {AE} \cdot  \cos {60}^{ \circ  }\]

\[ = {7}^{2} + {4}^{2} - 2 \cdot  7 \cdot  4 \cdot  \frac{1}{2}\]

\[ = {37}\text{.}\]

于是 \( \bigtriangleup {DEF} \) 的面积

\[S = \frac{1}{2} \cdot  {EF} \cdot  {DH}\]

\[ = \frac{1}{2} \cdot  {EF} \cdot  \sqrt{D{E}^{2} - {\left( \frac{1}{2}EF\right) }^{2}}\]

\[ = 2\sqrt{33},\]


因此所求的面积为 \( 2\sqrt{33} \) .

6. 在平面直角坐标系 \( {xOy} \) ,点集 \( K = \{ \left( {x,y}\right)  \mid  x,y \in   - 1,0,1\} \) . 在 \( K \) 中随机取出三个点, 则这三个点两两之间的距离均不超过 2 的概率是_____.

解析 \( \frac{5}{14} \) .

如图,点集 \( K = \left\{  {O,{P}_{1},{P}_{2},{P}_{3},{P}_{4},{P}_{5},{P}_{6},{P}_{7},{P}_{8}}\right\} \) .

<!-- Media -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_145.jpg?x=695&y=564&w=314&h=313&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

三个点两两之间的距离可能为 \( 1,\sqrt{2},2,\sqrt{5},2\sqrt{2} \) . 因此有如下情形.

情形 1: 两两之间的距离为 \( 1,1,\sqrt{2} \) ,共有 16 个.

情形 2: 两两之间的距离为1,1,2,共有 6 个.

情形 3: 两两之间的距离为 \( \sqrt{2},\sqrt{2},2 \) ,共有 8 个.

综上所述. 所求的概率为

\[\frac{{16} + 6 + 8}{{\mathrm{C}}_{9}^{3}} = \frac{30}{84} = \frac{5}{14}.\]

7. 设 \( a \) 为非零实数,在平面直角坐标系中 \( {xOy} \) 中,二次曲线 \( {x}^{2} + a{y}^{2} + {a}^{2} = 0 \) 的焦距为 4 ,则 \( a \) 的值为_____.

解析 \( \frac{1 - \sqrt{17}}{2} \) .

题中方程即

\[\frac{{y}^{2}}{-a} - \frac{{x}^{2}}{{a}^{2}} = 1\]

因此 \( - a > 0 \) 且该方程表示焦点在 \( y \) 轴上的双曲线,且焦距

\[2\sqrt{-a + {a}^{2}} = 4,\]

解得

\[a = \frac{1 - \sqrt{17}}{2}\]

8. 若正整数 \( a,b,c \) 满足 \( {2017} \geq  {10a} \geq  {100b} \geq  {1000c} \) ,则数组(a,b,c)的个数为_____.

解析 574.

根据题意,有 \( c = 1,2 \) .


情形 1: 当 \( c = 1 \) 时,有 \( {10} \leq  b \leq  {20} \) ,且 \( {10b} \leq  a \leq  {201} \) ,于是对应的数组(a,b,c)的个数为

\[\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{b = {10}}}^{{20}}\left( {{202} - {10b}}\right)  = \frac{\left( {{102} + 2}\right)  \times  {11}}{2} = {572}.\]

情形 2: 当 \( c = 2 \) 时,有 \( b = {20} \) ,于是

\[{200} \leq  a \leq  \left\lbrack  \frac{2017}{10}\right\rbrack   = {201},\]

因此对应的数组(a,b,c)的个数为 2 .

综上所述,满足题意的数组(a,b,c)的个数为 574.

## 二、 解答题：本大题共 3 小题,满分 56 分. 解答应写出文字说明、证明过程或演算步骤. 其 中第 9 题满分 16 分, 第 10、11 题满分 20 分.

9. 设不等式 \( \left| {{2}^{x} - a}\right|  < \left| {5 - {2}^{x}}\right| \) 对所有 \( x \in  \left\lbrack  {1,2}\right\rbrack \) 成立,求实数 \( a \) 的取值范围.

解析(3,5).

根据题意, 有

\[\forall x \in  \left\lbrack  {1,2}\right\rbrack  ,\left| {{2}^{x} - a}\right|  < 5 - {2}^{x},\]

即

\[\forall x \in  \left\lbrack  {1,2}\right\rbrack  ,{2}^{x} - 5 < {2}^{x} - a < 5 - {2}^{x},\]

也即

\[\forall x \in  \left\lbrack  {1,2}\right\rbrack  ,2 \cdot  {2}^{x} - 5 < a < 5,\]

也即

\[3 < a < 5\text{.}\]

10. 设数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 是等差数列,数列 \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 满足 \( {b}_{n} = {a}_{n + 1}{a}_{n + 2} - {a}_{n}^{2},n = 1,2,\cdots \) .

(1)证明：数列 \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 也是等差数列；

(2)设数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\}  ,\left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 的公差均是 \( d \neq  0 \) ,并且存在正整数 \( s,t \) ,使得 \( {a}_{s} + {b}_{t} \) 是整数,

求 \( \left| {a}_{1}\right| \) 的最小值.

解析(1)见解析

(2) \( \frac{1}{18} \) .

(1) 不妨设 \( {a}_{n} = a + {nd},n \in  {\mathbb{N}}^{ * } \) ,则

\[{b}_{n} = \left\lbrack  {a + \left( {n + 1}\right) d}\right\rbrack   \cdot  \left\lbrack  {a + \left( {n + 2}\right) d}\right\rbrack   - {\left( a + nd\right) }^{2}\]

\[ = \left\lbrack  {{dn} + \left( {a + d}\right) }\right\rbrack   \cdot  \left\lbrack  {{dn} + \left( {a + {2d}}\right) }\right\rbrack   - {\left( dn + a\right) }^{2}\]

\[ = \left\lbrack  {{d}^{2}{n}^{2} + \left( {{2ad} + 3{d}^{2}}\right) n + \left( {{a}^{2} + {3ad} + 2{d}^{2}}\right) }\right\rbrack   - \left( {{d}^{2}{n}^{2} + {2adn} + {a}^{2}}\right) \]

\[ = 3{d}^{2}n + \left( {{3ad} + 2{d}^{2}}\right) ,\]


因此数列 \( \left\{  {b}_{n}\right\} \) 也是等差数列.

(2)根据题意,有 \( 3{d}^{2} = d \) ,因此 \( d = \frac{1}{3} \) ,于是

\[{b}_{n} = \frac{1}{3}n + a + \frac{2}{9} = {a}_{n} + \frac{2}{9},\]

进而

\[{a}_{s} + {b}_{t} = {a}_{s} + {a}_{t} + \frac{2}{9}\]

\[ = 2{a}_{1} + \frac{s + t - 2}{3} + \frac{2}{9},\]

于是

\[{18}{a}_{1} = 3\left\lbrack  {3\left( {{a}_{s} + {b}_{t}}\right)  - s - t + 1}\right\rbrack   + 1,\]

因此

\[\left| {{18}{a}_{1}}\right|  \geq  1\]

又当 \( \left( {{a}_{1},s,t}\right)  = \left( {\frac{1}{18},1,3}\right) \) 时, \( {a}_{s} + {b}_{t} = 1 \) 符合题意,因此所求 \( \left| {a}_{1}\right| \) 的最小值为 \( \frac{1}{18} \) .

11. 在平面直角坐标系 \( {xOy} \) 中,曲线 \( {C}_{1} : {y}^{2} = {4x} \) ,曲线 \( {C}_{2} : {\left( x - 4\right) }^{2} + {y}^{2} = 8 \) . 经过 \( {C}_{1} \) 上一点 \( P \) 作一条倾斜角为 \( {45}^{ \circ  } \) 的直线 \( l \) ,与 \( {C}_{2} \) 交于两个不同的点 \( Q,R \) ,求 \( \left| {PQ}\right|  \cdot  \left| {PR}\right| \) 的取值范围.

<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( y \) \( M \) \( x \) Og -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_147.jpg?x=722&y=1213&w=266&h=314&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

解析 \( \lbrack 4,8) \cup  \left( {8,{200}}\right) \) .

设 \( P\left( {4{t}^{2},{4t}}\right) \) ,则直线

\[l : x - y - 4{t}^{2} + {4t} = 0.\]

该直线与圆相交, 因此

\[\frac{\left| 4 - 4{t}^{2} + 4t\right| }{\sqrt{2}} < 2\sqrt{2}\]

即

\[ - 1 < {t}^{2} - t - 1 < 1\]


解得 \( t \) 的取值范围是 \( \left( {-1,0}\right)  \cup  \left( {1,2}\right) \) .

联立曲线 \( {C}_{1},{C}_{2} \) 的方程可得

\[{x}^{2} - {4x} + 8 = 0,\]

于是 \( {C}_{1} \) 与 \( {C}_{2} \) 没有公共点. 因此有

\[\left| {PQ}\right|  \cdot  \left| {PR}\right|  = \overrightarrow{PQ} \cdot  \overrightarrow{PR},\]

根据圆幂定理, 有

\[\overrightarrow{PQ} \cdot  \overrightarrow{PR} = P{M}^{2} - 8\]

\[ = {\left( 4{t}^{2} - 4\right) }^{2} + {\left( 4t\right) }^{2} - 8\]

\[ = {16}{t}^{4} - {16}{t}^{2} + 8\]

\[ = {16}{\left( {t}^{2} - \frac{1}{2}\right) }^{2} + 4\]

因此所求的取值范围是 \( \lbrack 4,8) \cup  \left( {8,{200}}\right) \) .


## 2017 年全国高中数学联赛二试答案 (B 卷)

一、设实数 \( a,b,c \) 满足 \( a + b + c = 0 \) ,令 \( d = \max \{ \left| a\right| ,\left| b\right| ,\left| c\right| \} \) . 证明:

\[\left| {\left( {1 + a}\right) \left( {1 + b}\right) \left( {1 + c}\right) }\right|  \geq  1 - {d}^{2}.\]

解析

不妨设 \( a \leq  b \leq  c \) ,则 \( a \leq  0 \) 且 \( c \geq  0 \) . 若 \( d \geq  1 \) ,则不等式显然成立. 下面考虑 \( 0 \leq  d < 1 \) 的情形,此时 \( a,b,c \in  \left( {-1,1}\right) \) ,于是

\[m = \left| {\left( {1 + a}\right) \left( {1 + b}\right) \left( {1 + c}\right) }\right|  = \left( {1 + a}\right) \left( {1 + b}\right) \left( {1 + c}\right) .\]

当 \( b \geq  0 \) 时,有

\[m \geq  \left( {1 + a}\right) \left( {1 + b + c}\right)  = 1 - {a}^{2} \geq  1 - {d}^{2},\]

类似的,当 \( b < 0 \) 时,有

\[m \geq  \left( {1 + a + b}\right) \left( {1 + c}\right)  = 1 - {c}^{2} \geq  1 - {d}^{2},\]

因此原不等式得证.

二、给定正整数 \( m \) ,证明: 存在正整数 \( k \) ,使得可将正整数集 \( {\mathbb{N}}^{ * } \) 分拆为 \( k \) 个互不相交的子集 \( {A}_{1},{A}_{2},\cdots ,{A}_{k} \) ,每个子集 \( {A}_{i} \) 中均不存在 4 个数 \( a,b,c,d \) (可以相同),满足 \( {ab} - {cd} = m \) . 解析

取 \( k = m + 1 \) ,令

\[{A}_{i} = \left\{  {x \mid  x \equiv  i\;\left( {{\;\operatorname{mod}\;m} + 1}\right) ,x \in  {\mathbb{N}}^{ * }}\right\}  ,\]

其中 \( i = 1,2,\cdots ,m + 1 \) . 设 \( a,b,c,d \in  {A}_{i} \) ,则

\[{ab} - {cd} \equiv  i \cdot  i - i \cdot  i = 0 \equiv  0\;\left( {{\;\operatorname{mod}\;m} + 1}\right) ,\]

故 \( m + 1 \mid  {ab} - {cd} \) ,而 \( m + 1 \nmid  m \) ,所以 \( {A}_{i} \) 中不存在 4 个数 \( a,b,c,d \) 满足 \( {ab} - {cd} = m \) .

三、如图,点 \( D \) 是锐角 \( \bigtriangleup  {ABC} \) 的外接圆 \( \omega \) 上弧 \( {BC} \) 的中点,直线 \( {DA} \) 与圆 \( \omega \) 过点 \( B,C \) 的切线分别相交于点 \( P,Q,{BQ} \) 与 \( {AC} \) 的交点为 \( X,{CP} \) 与 \( {AB} \) 的交点为 \( Y,{BQ} \) 与 \( {CP} \) 的交点为 \( T \) . 求证: \( {AT} \) 平分线段 \( {XY} \) .


<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( P \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_150.jpg?x=608&y=277&w=499&h=306&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

解析

首先证明 \( {YX}\parallel {BC} \) ,即证 \( \frac{AX}{XC} = \frac{AY}{YB} \) . 连接 \( {BD},{CD} \) ,如图.

<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( C \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_150.jpg?x=610&y=752&w=497&h=305&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

为了方便我们直接用三角形代表该三角形的面积, 因为

\[\frac{\bigtriangleup {ACQ}}{\bigtriangleup {ABC}} \cdot  \frac{\bigtriangleup {ABC}}{\bigtriangleup {ABP}} = \frac{\bigtriangleup {ACQ}}{\bigtriangleup {ABP}},\]

于是

\[\frac{{AC} \cdot  {CQ} \cdot  \sin \angle {ACQ}}{{AB} \cdot  {BC} \cdot  \sin \angle {ABC}} \cdot  \frac{{AC} \cdot  {BC} \cdot  \sin \angle {ACB}}{{AB} \cdot  {BP} \cdot  \sin \angle {ABP}} = \frac{{AC} \cdot  {AQ} \cdot  \angle {CAQ}}{{AB} \cdot  {AP} \cdot  \sin \angle {BAP}}.\]

根据弦切角定理, 有

\[\angle {ACQ} = \angle {ABC},\angle {ACB} = \angle {ABP},\]

又 \( D \) 是弧 \( {BC} \) 的中点,于是

\[\angle {CAQ} = \angle {DBC} = \angle {DCB} = \angle {BAP},\]

于是可得

\[\frac{{AB} \cdot  {AQ}}{{AC} \cdot  {AP}} = \frac{CQ}{BP}.\]

因为 \( \angle {CAQ} = \angle {BAP} \) ,所以 \( \angle {BAQ} = \angle {CAP} \) ,于是

\[\frac{\bigtriangleup {ABQ}}{\bigtriangleup {ACP}} = \frac{{AB} \cdot  {AQ} \cdot  \sin \angle {BAQ}}{{AC} \cdot  {AP} \cdot  \sin \angle {CAP}} = \frac{{AB} \cdot  {AQ}}{{AC} \cdot  {AP}},\]


而

\[\frac{\bigtriangleup {BCQ}}{\bigtriangleup {BCP}} = \frac{{BC} \cdot  {CQ} \cdot  \sin \angle {BCQ}}{{BC} \cdot  {BP} \cdot  \sin \angle {CBP}} = \frac{CQ}{BP},\]

因此可得

\[\frac{\bigtriangleup {ABQ}}{\bigtriangleup {ACP}} = \frac{\bigtriangleup {CBQ}}{\bigtriangleup {BCP}},\]

即

\[\frac{\bigtriangleup {ABQ}}{\bigtriangleup {CBQ}} = \frac{\bigtriangleup {ACP}}{\bigtriangleup {BCP}},\]

又

\[\frac{\bigtriangleup {ABQ}}{\bigtriangleup {CBQ}} = \frac{AX}{XC},\frac{\bigtriangleup {ACP}}{\bigtriangleup {BCP}} = \frac{AY}{YB},\]

故 \( \frac{AX}{XC} = \frac{AY}{YB} \) .

设 \( \overset{⏜}{BC} \) 边的中点为 \( M \) ,因为

\[\frac{AX}{XC} \cdot  \frac{CM}{MB} \cdot  \frac{BY}{YA} = 1\]

所以由塞瓦定理的逆定理可知 \( {AM},{BX},{CY} \) 三线共点于 \( T \) ,故由 \( {YX}\parallel {BC} \) 可知 \( {AT} \) 平分线段 \( {XY} \) .

四、设 \( m,n \) 均是大于 1 的整数, \( m \geq  n.{a}_{1},{a}_{2},\cdots ,{a}_{n} \) 是 \( n \) 个不超过 \( m \) 的互不相同的正整数,且 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},\cdots ,{a}_{n} \) 互素. 证明: 对任意实数 \( x \) ,均存在一个 \( i\left( {1 \leq  i \leq  n}\right) \) ,使得 \( \begin{Vmatrix}{{a}_{i}x}\end{Vmatrix} \geq  \frac{2}{m\left( {m + 1}\right) }\parallel x\parallel \) ,这里 \( \parallel y\parallel \) 表示实数 \( y \) 到与它最近的整数的距离.

解析

首先证明以下两个结论.

结论一: 存在整数 \( {c}_{1},{c}_{2},\cdots ,{c}_{n} \) ,满足

\[{c}_{1}{a}_{1} + {c}_{2}{a}_{2} + \cdots  + {c}_{n}{a}_{n} = 1,\]

并且 \( \left| {c}_{i}\right|  \leq  m,1 \leq  i \leq  n \) .

证明: 由于 \( \left( {{a}_{1},{a}_{2},\cdots ,{a}_{n}}\right)  = 1 \) ,由裴蜀定理,存在正整数 \( {c}_{1},{c}_{2},\cdots ,{c}_{n} \) 满足

\[{c}_{1}{a}_{1} + {c}_{2}{a}_{2} + \cdots  + {c}_{n}{a}_{n} = 1.\]

下面证明,通过调整,存在一组 \( {c}_{1},{c}_{2},\cdots ,{c}_{n} \) 满足上式,且绝对值均不超过 \( m \) . 记

\[{S}_{1} = {S}_{1}\left( {{c}_{1},{c}_{2},\cdots ,{c}_{n}}\right)  = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{{c}_{i} > m}}{c}_{i} \geq  0,\]

\[{S}_{2} = {S}_{2}\left( {{c}_{1},{c}_{2},\cdots ,{c}_{n}}\right)  = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{{c}_{i} <  - m}}\left| {c}_{i}\right|  \geq  0,\]


如果 \( {S}_{1} > 0 \) ,那么存在 \( {c}_{i} > m > 1 \) ,于是 \( {c}_{i}{a}_{i} > 1 \) ,又因为 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},\cdots ,{a}_{n} \) 均为正数,故由上式可知存在 \( {c}_{j} < 0 \) . 令

\[\left( {{c}_{i}^{\prime },{c}_{j}^{\prime },{c}_{k}^{\prime }}\right)  = \left( {{c}_{i} - {a}_{j},{c}_{j} + {a}_{i},{c}_{k}}\right) ,\]

其中 \( 1 \leq  k \leq  n,k \neq  i,j \) ,则

\[{c}_{1}^{\prime }{a}_{1} + {c}_{2}^{\prime }{a}_{2} + \cdots  + {c}_{n}^{\prime }{a}_{n} = 1,\]

并且

\[0 \leq  m - {a}_{j} < {c}_{i}^{\prime } < {c}_{i},{c}_{j} < {c}_{j}^{\prime } < {a}_{i} \leq  m,\]

因为 \( {c}_{i}^{\prime } < {c}_{i} \) ,且 \( {c}_{j}^{\prime } < m \) ,所以

\[{S}_{1}\left( {{c}_{1}^{\prime },{c}_{2}^{\prime },\cdots ,{c}_{n}^{\prime }}\right)  < {S}_{1}\left( {{c}_{1},{c}_{2},\cdots ,{c}_{n}}\right) .\]

又 \( {c}_{j}^{\prime } > {c}_{j} \) 及 \( {c}_{i}^{\prime } > 0 \) ,故

\[{S}_{2}\left( {{c}_{1}^{\prime },{c}_{2}^{\prime },\cdots ,{c}_{n}^{\prime }}\right)  \leq  {S}_{2}\left( {{c}_{1},{c}_{2},\cdots ,{c}_{n}}\right) .\]

如果 \( {S}_{2} > 0 \) ,那么存在 \( {c}_{j} <  - m \) ,因此有一个 \( {c}_{i} > 0 \) . 令

\[\left( {{c}_{i}^{\prime },{c}_{j}^{\prime },{c}_{k}^{\prime }}\right)  = \left( {{c}_{i} - {a}_{j},{c}_{j} + {a}_{i},{c}_{k}}\right) ,\]

其中 \( 1 \leq  k \leq  n,k \neq  i,j \) ,那么

\[{c}_{1}^{\prime }{a}_{1} + {c}_{2}^{\prime }{a}_{2} + \cdots  + {c}_{n}^{\prime }{a}_{n} = 1\]

成立, 并且

\[ - m < {c}_{i}^{\prime } < {c}_{i},{c}_{j} < {c}_{j}^{\prime } < 0.\]

与上面类似地可知

\[{S}_{1}\left( {{c}_{1}^{\prime },{c}_{2}^{\prime },\cdots ,{c}_{n}^{\prime }}\right)  \leq  {S}_{1}\left( {{c}_{1},{c}_{2},\cdots ,{c}_{n}}\right) ,\]

且.

\[{S}_{2}\left( {{c}_{1}^{\prime },{c}_{2}^{\prime },\cdots ,{c}_{n}^{\prime }}\right)  < {S}_{2}\left( {{c}_{1},{c}_{2},\cdots ,{c}_{n}}\right) .\]

因为 \( {S}_{1},{S}_{2} \) 均为非负整数,故通过有限次上述的调整,可得到一组 \( {c}_{1},{c}_{2},\cdots ,{c}_{n} \) 使得

\[{c}_{1}{a}_{1} + {c}_{2}{a}_{2} + \cdots  + {c}_{n}{a}_{n} = 1,\]

并且 \( \left| {c}_{i}\right|  \leq  m,1 \leq  i \leq  n \) . 且 \( {S}_{1} = {S}_{2} = 0 \) ,结论一获证.

结论二: 对任意实数 \( a,b \) ,均有

\[\parallel a + b\parallel  \leq  \parallel a\parallel  + \parallel b\parallel .\]


对任意整数 \( u \) 和实数 \( y \) ,均有

\[\parallel {uy}\parallel  \leq  \left| u\right|  \cdot  \parallel y\parallel .\]

证明: 由于对任意整数 \( u \) 和实数 \( x \) ,有

\[\parallel x + u\parallel  = \parallel x\parallel \]

故不妨设 \( a,b \in  \left\lbrack  {-\frac{1}{2},\frac{1}{2}}\right\rbrack \) ,此时

\[\parallel a\parallel  = \left| a\right| ,\parallel b\parallel  = \left| b\right| .\]

因为 \( \parallel x\parallel  \leq  \left| x\right| \) ,所以

\[\parallel a + b\parallel  \leq  \left| {a + b}\right|  \leq  \left| a\right|  + \left| b\right|  = \parallel a\parallel  + \parallel b\parallel ,\]

多次使用该结论有 \( \parallel {uy}\parallel  \leq  \left| u\right|  \cdot  \parallel y\parallel \) ,于是结论二获证.

回到原题: 由结论一,存在整数 \( {c}_{1},{c}_{2},\cdots ,{c}_{n} \) ,使得

\[{c}_{1}{a}_{1} + {c}_{2}{a}_{2} + \cdots  + {c}_{n}{a}_{n} = 1,\]

并且 \( \left| {c}_{i}\right|  \leq  m,1 \leq  i \leq  n \) ,于是

\[\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}{c}_{i}{a}_{i}x = x.\]

利用结论二得

\[\parallel x\parallel  = \begin{Vmatrix}{\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}{c}_{i}{a}_{i}x}\end{Vmatrix}\]

\[ \leq  \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}\begin{Vmatrix}{{c}_{i}\left| \cdot \right| \begin{Vmatrix}{{a}_{i}x}\end{Vmatrix}}\end{Vmatrix}\]

\[ \leq  m\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}\begin{Vmatrix}{{a}_{i}x}\end{Vmatrix}\]

\[ \leq  {mn} \cdot  \mathop{\max }\limits_{{1 \leq  i \leq  n}}\begin{Vmatrix}{{a}_{i}x}\end{Vmatrix},\]

因此

\[\mathop{\max }\limits_{{1 \leq  i \leq  n}}\begin{Vmatrix}{{a}_{i}x}\end{Vmatrix} \geq  \frac{1}{mn}\parallel x\parallel .\]

若 \( n \leq  \frac{1}{2}\left( {m + 1}\right) \) ,则

\[\mathop{\max }\limits_{{1 \leq  i \leq  n}}\begin{Vmatrix}{{a}_{i}x}\end{Vmatrix} \geq  \frac{\parallel x\parallel }{mn} \geq  \frac{2\parallel x\parallel }{m\left( {m + 1}\right) }.\]


若 \( n > \frac{1}{2}\left( {m + 1}\right) \) ,则在 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},\cdots ,{a}_{n} \) 中存在两个相邻正整数,不妨设 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2} \) 相邻,则

\[\parallel x\parallel  = \begin{Vmatrix}{{a}_{2}x - {a}_{1}x}\end{Vmatrix} \leq  \begin{Vmatrix}{{a}_{2}x}\end{Vmatrix} + \begin{Vmatrix}{{a}_{1}x}\end{Vmatrix},\]

故

\[\max \left\{  {\begin{Vmatrix}{{a}_{1}x}\end{Vmatrix},\begin{Vmatrix}{{a}_{2}x}\end{Vmatrix}}\right\}   \geq  \frac{\parallel x\parallel }{2} \geq  \frac{2\parallel x\parallel }{m\left( {m + 1}\right) }.\]

综上所述,总存在一个 \( i\left( {1 \leq  i \leq  n}\right) \) ,满足

\[\begin{Vmatrix}{{a}_{i}x}\end{Vmatrix} \geq  \frac{2}{m\left( {m + 1}\right) }\parallel x\parallel \]

命题得证.

1. 设 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},\cdots ,{a}_{20} \in  \{ 1,2,\cdots ,5\} ,{b}_{1},{b}_{2},\cdots ,{b}_{20} \in  \{ 1,2,\cdots ,{10}\} \) ,集合 \( X = \{ \left( {i,j}\right)  \mid \) \( \left. {1 \leq  i < j \leq  {20},\left( {{a}_{i} - {a}_{j}}\right) \left( {{b}_{i} - {b}_{j}}\right)  < 0}\right\} \) ,求 \( X \) 的元素个数的最大值.

解析 160.

考虑一组满足条件的正整数

\[\left\{  {{a}_{1},{a}_{2},\cdots ,{a}_{20},{b}_{1},{b}_{2},\cdots ,{b}_{20}}\right\}  .\]

对 \( k = 1,2,\cdots ,5 \) ,设 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},\cdots ,{a}_{20} \) 中取值为 \( k \) 的数有 \( {t}_{k} \) 个. 根据 \( X \) 的定义,当 \( {a}_{i} = {a}_{j} \) 时, \( \left( {i,j}\right)  \notin  X \) ,因此至少有 \( \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{k = 1}}^{5}{\mathrm{C}}_{{t}_{k}}^{2} \) 个(i,j)不在 \( X \) 中. 注意到

\[\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{k = 1}}^{5}{t}_{k} = {20}\]

由柯西不等式, 有

\[\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{k = 1}}^{5}{\mathrm{C}}_{{t}_{k}}^{2} = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{k = 1}}^{5}{t}_{k}^{2} - \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{k = 1}}^{5}{t}_{k}}\right)  \geq  \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{1}{5}{\left( \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{k = 1}}^{5}{t}_{k}\right) }^{2} - \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{k = 1}}^{5}{t}_{k}}\right)  = {30},\]

从而 \( X \) 的元素个数不超过

\[{\mathrm{C}}_{20}^{2} - {30} = {160}\]

另一方面, 取

\[{a}_{{4k} - 3} = {a}_{{4k} - 2} = {a}_{{4k} - 1} = {a}_{4k} = k,\]

其中 \( k = 1,2,\cdots ,5 \) ,且

\[{b}_{i} = 6 - {a}_{i},\]

其中 \( i = 1,2,\cdots ,{20} \) ,则对任意 \( i,j\left( {1 \leq  i < j \leq  {20}}\right) \) ,有

\[\left( {{a}_{i} - {a}_{j}}\right) \left( {{b}_{i} - {b}_{j}}\right)  = \left( {{a}_{i} - {a}_{j}}\right) \left\lbrack  {\left( {6 - {a}_{i}}\right)  - \left( {6 - {a}_{j}}\right) }\right\rbrack   =  - {\left( {a}_{i} - {a}_{j}\right) }^{2} \leq  0,\]

等号成立当且仅当 \( {a}_{i} = {a}_{j} \) ,这恰好发生 \( 5{\mathrm{C}}_{4}^{2} = {30} \) 次. 此时 \( X \) 的元素个数取得 160 . 综上所述, \( X \) 的元素个数的最大值为 160 .


## 2016 年全国高中数学联赛一试答案

## 一、 填空题: 本大题共 8 小题, 每小题 8 分, 满分 64 分.

1. 设实数 \( a \) 满足 \( a < 9{a}^{3} - {11a} < \left| a\right| \) ,则 \( a \) 的取值范围是_____.

解析 \( \left( {-\frac{2\sqrt{3}}{3}, - \frac{\sqrt{10}}{3}}\right) \) .

由 \( a < \left| a\right| \) ,可得 \( a < 0 \) ,于是原不等式即

\[\left\{  \begin{array}{l} a < 0, \\   - 1 < \frac{9{a}^{3} - {11a}}{-a} < 1, \end{array}\right. \]

解得 \( a \) 的取值范围是 \( \left( {-\frac{2\sqrt{3}}{3}, - \frac{\sqrt{10}}{3}}\right) \) .

2. 设复数 \( z,w \) 满足 \( \left| z\right|  = 3,\left( {z + \bar{w}}\right) \left( {\bar{z} - w}\right)  = 7 + 4\mathrm{i} \) ,其中 \( \mathrm{i} \) 是虚数单位, \( \bar{z},\bar{w} \) 分别表示 \( z,w \) 的共轭复数,则 \( \left( {z + 2\bar{w}}\right) \left( {\bar{z} - {2w}}\right) \) 的模为_____.

解析 \( \sqrt{65} \) .

根据已知, 有

\[z \cdot  \bar{z} - w \cdot  \bar{w} - z \cdot  w + \bar{z} \cdot  \bar{w} = 7 + 4\mathrm{i},\]

于是

\[\left\{  \begin{array}{l} z \cdot  \bar{z} - w \cdot  \bar{w} = 7, \\   - z \cdot  w + \bar{z} \cdot  \bar{w} = 4\mathrm{i}. \end{array}\right. \]

于是

\[\left( {z + 2\bar{w}}\right) \left( {\bar{z} - {2w}}\right)  = z \cdot  \bar{z} - {4w} \cdot  \bar{w} - {2z} \cdot  w + 2\bar{z} \cdot  \bar{w}\]

\[ = 4\left( {z \cdot  \bar{z} - w \cdot  \bar{w}}\right)  - {3z} \cdot  \bar{z} + 2\left( {-z \cdot  w + \bar{z} \cdot  \bar{w}}\right) \]

\[ = 1 + 8\mathrm{i},\]

于是所求复数的模为 \( \sqrt{65} \) .

3. 正实数 \( u,v,w \) 均不等于 1,若 \( {\log }_{u}\left( {vw}\right)  + {\log }_{v}w = 5,{\log }_{v}u + {\log }_{w}v = 3 \) ,则 \( {\log }_{w}u \) 的值为_____.


解析 \( \frac{4}{5} \) .

令 \( {\log }_{v}u = x,{\log }_{w}v = y \) ,则 \( {\log }_{w}u = {xy} \) ,条件变为

\[\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \frac{1}{x} + \frac{1}{y} + \frac{1}{xy} = 5 \\  x + y = 3 \end{array}\right. \]

从而解得 \( {xy} = \frac{4}{5} \) .

4. 袋子 \( A \) 中装有 2 张 10 元纸币和 3 张 1 元纸币,袋子 \( B \) 中装有 4 张 5 元纸币和 3 张 1 元纸币. 现随机从两个袋子中各取出两张纸币,则 \( A \) 中剩下的纸币面值之和大于 \( B \) 中剩下的纸币面值之和的概率为_____.

解析 \( \frac{9}{35} \) .

符合题意的情形只有 \( A \) 取走 2 张 1 元纸币, \( B \) 取走 2 张 5 元纸币或取走 1 张 5 元纸币和 1 张 1 元纸币, 因此所求的概率为

\[\frac{{\mathrm{C}}_{3}^{2} \cdot  \left( {{\mathrm{C}}_{4}^{2} + {\mathrm{C}}_{4}^{1}{\mathrm{C}}_{3}^{1}}\right) }{{\mathrm{C}}_{5}^{2}{\mathrm{C}}_{7}^{2}} = \frac{9}{35}.\]

5. 设 \( P \) 为圆锥的顶点, \( A,B,C \) 是其底面圆周上的三点,满足 \( \angle {ABC} = {90}^{ \circ  },M \) 为 \( {AP} \) 的中点. 若 \( {AB} = 1,{AC} = 2,{AP} = \sqrt{2} \) ,则二面角 \( M - {BC} - A \) 的大小为_____. 解析 arctan \( \frac{2}{3} \) .

如图,设 \( M \) 在底面 \( {ABC} \) 上的投影为 \( H \) ,过 \( H \) 作 \( {HN} \bot  {BC} \) 于点 \( N \) ,则 \( \angle {MNH} \) 为所求二面角的平面角.

<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( M \) \( C \) \( N \) \( A \) \( B \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_156.jpg?x=674&y=1298&w=368&h=312&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

于是

\[\tan \angle {MNH} = \frac{MH}{HN} = \frac{\frac{1}{2}{PO}}{\frac{3}{4}{AB}} = \frac{2}{3},\]

从而所求二面角的大小为 \( \arctan \frac{2}{3} \) .


6. 设函数 \( f\left( x\right)  = {\sin }^{4}\frac{kx}{10} + {\cos }^{4}\frac{kx}{10} \) ,其中 \( k \) 是一个正整数. 若对任意实数 \( a \) ,均有 \( \{ f\left( x\right)  \mid  a < x < a + 1\}  = \{ f\left( x\right)  \mid  x \in  \mathbb{R}\} \) ,则 \( k \) 的最小值为_____.

解析 16.

根据已知, 有

\[f\left( x\right)  = {\left( {\sin }^{2}\frac{kx}{10} + {\cos }^{2}\frac{kx}{10}\right) }^{2} - \frac{1}{2}{\left( 2\sin \frac{kx}{10} \cdot  \cos \frac{kx}{10}\right) }^{2}\]

\[ = 1 - \frac{1}{2}{\sin }^{2}\frac{kx}{5}\]

\[ = \frac{1}{4}\cos \frac{2kx}{5} + \frac{3}{4}\text{.}\]

题意为任取函数 \( f\left( x\right) \) 图象上在 \( x \) 轴上投影长度为 1 的一段 (不包含端点) 都能同时覆盖函数 \( f\left( x\right) \) 的最大值点和最小值点,于是其最小正周期小于 1,从而 \( k \) 的最小值为 \( \left\lbrack  {5\pi }\right\rbrack   + 1 = {16} \)

7. 双曲线 \( C \) 的方程为 \( {x}^{2} - \frac{{y}^{2}}{3} = 1 \) ,左、右焦点分别为 \( {F}_{1},{F}_{2} \) ,过点 \( {F}_{2} \) 作一直线与双曲线 \( C \) 的右半支交于点 \( P,Q \) ,使得 \( \angle {F}_{1}{PQ} = {90}^{ \circ  } \) ,则 \( \bigtriangleup  {F}_{1}{PQ} \) 的内切圆半径是_____.

解析 \( \sqrt{7} - 1 \) .

如图, \( {F}_{1}{F}_{2} = 4,P{F}_{1} - P{F}_{2} = Q{F}_{1} - Q{F}_{2} = 2 \) .

<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( y \) Og \( x \) Q \( {F}_{1} \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_157.jpg?x=671&y=1089&w=360&h=360&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

于是 \( \bigtriangleup {F}_{1}{PQ} \) 的内切圆的半径

\[r = \frac{1}{2}\left( {P{F}_{1} + {PQ} - {F}_{1}Q}\right) \]

\[ = \frac{1}{2}\left( {P{F}_{1} + P{F}_{2} + Q{F}_{2} - {F}_{1}Q}\right) \]

\[ = \frac{1}{2}\left\lbrack  {\sqrt{2\left( {P{F}_{1}^{2} + P{F}_{2}^{2}}\right)  - {\left( P{F}_{1} - P{F}_{2}\right) }^{2}} - \left( {Q{F}_{1} - Q{F}_{2}}\right) }\right\rbrack  \]

\[ = \sqrt{7} - 1\text{. }\]

8. 设 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},{a}_{3},{a}_{4} \) 是 \( 1,2,\cdots ,{100} \) 中的 4 个互不相同的数,满足

\[\left( {{a}_{1}^{2} + {a}_{2}^{2} + {a}_{3}^{2}}\right) \left( {{a}_{2}^{2} + {a}_{3}^{2} + {a}_{4}^{2}}\right)  = {\left( {a}_{1}{a}_{2} + {a}_{2}{a}_{3} + {a}_{3}{a}_{4}\right) }^{2},\]


则这样的序列数组 \( \left( {{a}_{1},{a}_{2},{a}_{3},{a}_{4}}\right) \) 的个数为_____.

解析 40.

由柯西不等式的取等条件可知 \( \frac{{a}_{1}}{{a}_{2}} = \frac{{a}_{2}}{{a}_{3}} = \frac{{a}_{3}}{{a}_{4}} \) ,于是问题即从 \( 1,2,\cdots ,{100} \) 中选出 4 个不同的数组成的等比数列的个数. 不难推知 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},{a}_{3},{a}_{4} \) 必然形如 \( a{m}^{3},a{m}^{2}n,a{mn}^{2},a{n}^{3} \) , 其中 \( a,m,n \) 均为正整数,且 \( m \neq  n,\left( {m,n}\right)  = 1 \) . 考虑 \( m < n \) 的情形,此时所有的(m,n) 有

\[\left( {1,2}\right) ,\left( {1,3}\right) ,\left( {1,4}\right) ,\left( {2,3}\right) ,\left( {3,4}\right) \text{,}\]

对应的等比数列个数之和为

\[\left\lbrack  \frac{100}{{2}^{3}}\right\rbrack   + 2 \cdot  \left\lbrack  \frac{100}{{3}^{3}}\right\rbrack   + 2 \cdot  \left\lbrack  \frac{100}{{4}^{3}}\right\rbrack   = {20},\]

因此所求的有序数组 \( \left( {{a}_{1},{a}_{2},{a}_{3},{a}_{4}}\right) \) 共有 40 个.

## 二、 解答题：本大题共 3 小题,满分 56 分. 解答应写出文字说明、证明过程或演算步骤. 其 中第 9 题满分 16 分, 第 10、11 题满分 20 分.

9. 在 \( \bigtriangleup {ABC} \) 中,已知 \( \overrightarrow{AB} \cdot  \overrightarrow{AC} + 2\overrightarrow{BA} \cdot  \overrightarrow{BC} = 3\overrightarrow{CA} \cdot  \overrightarrow{CB} \) . 求 \( \sin C \) 的最大值.

解析 \( \frac{\sqrt{7}}{3} \) .

统一起点, 有

\[\left( {\overrightarrow{CA} - \overrightarrow{CB}}\right)  \cdot  \overrightarrow{CA} + 2\left( {\overrightarrow{CB} - \overrightarrow{CA}}\right)  \cdot  \overrightarrow{CB} = 3\overrightarrow{CA} \cdot  \overrightarrow{CB},\]

即

\[6\overrightarrow{CA} \cdot  \overrightarrow{CB} = C{A}^{2} + {2C}{B}^{2},\]

也即

\[\cos C = \frac{C{A}^{2} + {2C}{B}^{2}}{{6CA} \cdot  {CB}} \geq  \frac{\sqrt{2}}{3},\]

等号当 \( {CA} = \sqrt{2} \cdot  {CB} \) 时取得. 因此 \( \cos C \) 的最小值为 \( \frac{\sqrt{2}}{3} \) ,对应 \( \sin C \) 的最大值为 \( \frac{\sqrt{7}}{3} \) . 10. 已知 \( f\left( x\right) \) 是 \( \mathbb{R} \) 上的奇函数, \( f\left( 1\right)  = 1 \) ,且对任意 \( x < 0 \) ,均有 \( f\left( \frac{x}{x - 1}\right)  = {xf}\left( x\right) \) . 求

\[f\left( 1\right) f\left( \frac{1}{100}\right)  + f\left( \frac{1}{2}\right) f\left( \frac{1}{99}\right)  + f\left( \frac{1}{3}\right) f\left( \frac{1}{98}\right)  + \cdots  + f\left( \frac{1}{50}\right) f\left( \frac{1}{51}\right) \]

的值.

解析 \( \frac{{2}^{98}}{{99}!} \) .

令 \( x =  - \frac{1}{n},n \in  {\mathbb{N}}^{ * } \) ,则

\[\frac{x}{x - 1} = \frac{-\frac{1}{n}}{-\frac{1}{n} - 1} = \frac{1}{n + 1}\]


于是有

\[f\left( \frac{1}{n + 1}\right)  =  - \frac{1}{n}f\left( {-\frac{1}{n}}\right)  = \frac{1}{n}f\left( \frac{1}{n}\right) ,\]

记 \( {a}_{n} = f\left( \frac{1}{n}\right) ,n \in  {\mathbb{N}}^{ * } \) ,则有 \( \frac{{a}_{n + 1}}{{a}_{n}} = \frac{1}{n} \) ,从而

\[{a}_{n} = \frac{1}{\left( {n - 1}\right) !}\]

于是所求代数式即

\[\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{{50}}{a}_{i}{a}_{{101} - i} = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{{50}}\frac{1}{\left( {i - 1}\right) ! \cdot  \left( {{100} - i}\right) !} = \frac{1}{{99}!}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 0}}^{{49}}{\mathrm{C}}_{99}^{i} = \frac{1}{{99}!} \cdot  \frac{1}{2}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 0}}^{{99}}{\mathrm{C}}_{99}^{i} = \frac{{2}^{98}}{{99}!}.\]

11. 如图所示,在平面直角坐标系 \( {xOy} \) 中, \( F \) 是 \( x \) 轴正半轴上的一个动点,以 \( F \) 为焦点、 \( O \) 为顶点作抛物线 \( C \) ,设 \( P \) 是第一象限内 \( C \) 上的一点, \( Q \) 是 \( x \) 轴负半轴上一点,使得 \( {PQ} \) 为 \( C \) 的切线,且 \( \left| {PQ}\right|  = 2 \) ,圆 \( {C}_{1},{C}_{2} \) 均与直线 \( {OP} \) 相切于点 \( P \) ,且均与 \( x \) 轴相切,求点 \( F \) 的坐标,使圆 \( {C}_{1} \) 与 \( {C}_{2} \) 的面积之和取到最小值.

<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( {\dot{C}}_{1} \) \( {y}_{4} \) \( {C}_{2} \) 0 \( x \) \( Q \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_159.jpg?x=604&y=983&w=499&h=445&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

解析 \( F\left( {\frac{1}{\sqrt{3 - \sqrt{3}}},0}\right) \) .

如图,设抛物线方程为 \( C : {y}^{2} = {2px} \) ,焦点 \( F\left( {\frac{p}{2},0}\right) \) ,连接 \( {C}_{1}{C}_{2},{PF} \) .


<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( Q \) \( {y}_{4} \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_160.jpg?x=603&y=278&w=500&h=444&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

设 \( P\left( {{2p}{a}^{2},{2pa}}\right) \) ,则根据抛物线的光学性质, \( \left| {FQ}\right|  = \left| {PF}\right| \) ,于是 \( Q\left( {-{2p}{a}^{2},0}\right) \) ,进而由 \( \left| {PQ}\right|  = 2 \) ,可得

\[4{p}^{2}{a}^{4} + {p}^{2}{a}^{2} = 1\]

即

\[{p}^{2}{a}^{2} = \frac{1}{4{a}^{2} + 1}.\]

圆心 \( {C}_{1},{C}_{2} \) 都在过点 \( P \) 且与 \( {OP} \) 垂直的直线 \( l \) 上,设直线 \( l \) 的参数方程为

\[\left\{  \begin{array}{l} x = {2p}{a}^{2} + t \\  y = {2pa} - {at} \end{array}\right. \]

根据题意, \( {C}_{1},{C}_{2} \) 对应的参数满足

\[\sqrt{1 + {a}^{2}} \cdot  \left| t\right|  = {2pa} - {at}\]

即

\[{t}^{2} + {4p}{a}^{2}t - 4{p}^{2}{a}^{2} = 0,\]

因此圆 \( {C}_{1} \) 的面积 \( {S}_{1} \) 与圆 \( {C}_{2} \) 的面积 \( {S}_{2} \) 之和

\[{S}_{1} + {S}_{2} = \pi \left\lbrack  {\left( {1 + {a}^{2}}\right) {t}_{1}^{2} + \left( {1 + {a}^{2}}\right) {t}_{2}^{2}}\right\rbrack  \]

\[ = \pi \left( {1 + {a}^{2}}\right) \left\lbrack  {{\left( -4p{a}^{2}\right) }^{2} + 2 \cdot  4{p}^{2}{a}^{2}}\right\rbrack  \]

\[ = \pi \left( {1 + {a}^{2}}\right) \left( {{16}{a}^{2} + 8}\right)  \cdot  {p}^{2}{a}^{2}\]

\[ = \frac{\pi \left( {{16}{a}^{4} + {24}{a}^{2} + 8}\right) }{4{a}^{2} + 1}\]

\[ = \pi \left( {4{a}^{2} + 1 + \frac{3}{4{a}^{2} + 1} + 4}\right) \]

\[ \geq  \pi \left( {4 + 2\sqrt{3}}\right) ,\]


等号当 \( 4{a}^{2} + 1 = \sqrt{3} \) ,即 \( {a}^{2} = \frac{\sqrt{3} - 1}{4} \) 时取得. 此时

\[{p}^{2} = \frac{1}{{a}^{2}\left( {4{a}^{2} + 1}\right) } = \frac{4}{\left( {\sqrt{3} - 1}\right)  \cdot  \sqrt{3}},\]

于是 \( F \) 点的坐标为 \( \left( {\frac{1}{\sqrt{3 - \sqrt{3}}},0}\right) \) .


## 2016 年全国高中数学联赛二试答案

一、设实数 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},\cdots ,{a}_{2016} \) 满足 \( 9{a}_{i} > {11}{a}_{i + 1}^{2}\left( {i = 1,2,\cdots ,{2015}}\right) \) . 求

\[\left( {{a}_{1} - {a}_{2}^{2}}\right)  \cdot  \left( {{a}_{2} - {a}_{3}^{2}}\right) \cdots \left( {{a}_{2015} - {a}_{2016}^{2}}\right)  \cdot  \left( {{a}_{2016} - {a}_{1}^{2}}\right) \]

的最大值.

解析 \( \frac{1}{{4}^{2016}} \) .

令原式为 \( P \) . 由于 \( {a}_{i} - {a}_{i + 1}^{2} > 0,i = 1,2,\cdots ,{2015} \) ,因此只需要考虑当 \( {a}_{2016} - {a}_{1}^{2} > 0 \)

的情况,记 \( {a}_{2017} = {a}_{1} \) ,则

\[{P}^{\frac{1}{2016}} \leq  \frac{1}{2016}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{k = 1}}^{{2016}}\left( {{a}_{k} - {a}_{k + 1}^{2}}\right) \]

\[ = \frac{1}{2016}\left( {\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{k = 1}}^{{2016}}{a}_{k} - \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{k = 1}}^{{2016}}{a}_{k}^{2}}\right) \]

\[ = \frac{1}{2016}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{k = 1}}^{{2016}}\left\lbrack  {{a}_{k}\left( {1 - {a}_{k}}\right) }\right\rbrack   \leq  \frac{1}{4},\]

等号当 \( {a}_{1} = {a}_{2} = \cdots  = {a}_{2016} = \frac{1}{2} \) 时取得. 因此 \( P \) 的最大值为 \( \frac{1}{{4}^{2016}} \) .

二、如图所示,在 \( \bigtriangleup {ABC} \) 中, \( X,Y \) 是直线 \( {BC} \) 上两点 ( \( X,B,C,Y \) 顺次排列),使得

\[{BX} \cdot  {AC} = {CY} \cdot  {AB}.\]

设 \( \bigtriangleup {ACX},\bigtriangleup {ABY} \) 的外心分别为 \( {O}_{1},{O}_{2} \) ,直线 \( {O}_{1}{O}_{2} \) 与 \( {AB},{AC} \) 分别交于点 \( U,V \) . 证明: \( \bigtriangleup {AUV} \) 是等腰三角形.

<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( X \) \( B \) \( A \) \( {O}_{2} \) \( V \) \( C \) Y -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_162.jpg?x=640&y=1501&w=436&h=253&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

解析

解法一:

如图,设圆 \( {O}_{1} \) 与圆 \( {O}_{2} \) 的公共弦为 \( {AD},{AD} \) 交 \( {XY} \) 于 \( E \) .


<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( X \) \( B \) / \( E \) \( C \) \( D \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_163.jpg?x=645&y=271&w=430&h=354&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

由于 \( {AD} \) 为两圆的根轴,于是 \( E \) 点对圆 \( {O}_{1} \) 和圆 \( {O}_{2} \) 的幂相等,从而

\[{XE} \cdot  {CE} = {BE} \cdot  {YE},\]

进而结合合分比定理有

\[\frac{BE}{CE} = \frac{XE}{YE} = \frac{XB}{YC},\]

又由已知,有 \( \frac{XB}{YC} = \frac{AB}{AC} \) ,于是有 \( \frac{BE}{CE} = \frac{AB}{AC} \) ,从而 \( {AE} \) 是 \( \angle {BAC} \) 的角平分线. 又 \( {AD} \bot  {O}_{1}{O}_{2} \) ,于是 \( U,V \) 关于直线 \( {AD} \) 对称,因此 \( \bigtriangleup {AUV} \) 是等腰三角形.

解法二:

如图,设 \( \bigtriangleup {ABC} \) 的外心为 \( O \) ,连结 \( O{O}_{1},O{O}_{2} \) ,过点 \( O,{O}_{1},{O}_{2} \) 分别作直线 \( {BC} \) 的垂线,垂足分别为 \( D,{D}_{1},{D}_{2} \) . 作 \( {O}_{1}K \bot  {OD} \) 于点 \( K \) .

<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( X \) \( V \) \( Y \) \( B{D}_{1}D{D}_{2}C \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_163.jpg?x=658&y=1151&w=401&h=222&r=0"/>

图 2

<!-- Media -->

我们证明 \( O{O}_{1} = O{O}_{2} \) . 在直角三角形 \( {OK}{O}_{1} \) 中,

\[O{O}_{1} = \frac{{O}_{1}K}{\sin \angle {O}_{1}{OK}}.\]

由外心的性质, \( O{O}_{1} \bot  {AC} \) ,又 \( {OD} \bot  {BC} \) ,故 \( \angle {O}_{1}{OK} = \angle {ACB} \) . 而 \( D,{D}_{1} \) 分别是 \( {BC},{CX} \) 的中点,所以

\[D{D}_{1} = C{D}_{1} - {CD} = \frac{1}{2}{CX} - \frac{1}{2}{BC} = \frac{1}{2}{BX}.\]

因此

\[O{O}_{1} = \frac{{O}_{1}K}{\sin \angle {O}_{1}{OK}} = \frac{D{D}_{1}}{\sin \angle {ACB}} = \frac{\frac{1}{2}{BX}}{\frac{AB}{2R}} = R \cdot  \frac{BX}{AB},\]


这里 \( R \) 是 \( \bigtriangleup {ABC} \) 的外接圆半径. 同理 \( O{O}_{2} = R \cdot  \frac{CY}{AC} \) . 由已知条件可得 \( \frac{BX}{AB} = \frac{CY}{AC} \) , 故 \( O{O}_{1} = O{O}_{2} \) . 由于 \( O{O}_{1} = O{O}_{2} \) ,故 \( \angle O{O}_{1}{O}_{2} = \angle O{O}_{2}{O}_{1} \) ,从而 \( \angle {AUV} = \angle {AVU} \) . 这样 \( {AU} = {AV} \) ,即 \( \bigtriangleup  {AUV} \) 是等腰三角形.

三、 给定空间中 10 个点, 其中任意四点不在一个平面上, 将某些点之间用线段相连, 若得到的图形中没有三角形也没有空间四边形, 试确定所连线段数目的最大值.

解析 15.

记这 10 个点分别为 \( {P}_{i} \) 且从 \( {P}_{i} \) 点引出了 \( {a}_{i} \) 条线段,其中 \( i = 1,2,\cdots ,{10} \) . 这样图形中总共包含 \( \frac{1}{2}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{{10}}{a}_{i} \) 条线段和 \( \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{{10}}{\mathrm{C}}_{{a}_{i}}^{2} \) 个角. 根据题意,图形中没有空间四边形,因此任何一个角都与一个点对 \( \left( {{P}_{m},{P}_{n}}\right) \) 一一对应,且不存在线段 \( {P}_{m}{P}_{n} \) . 这样就有

\[\frac{1}{2}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{{10}}{a}_{i} + \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{{10}}{\mathrm{C}}_{{a}_{i}}^{2} = \frac{1}{2}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{{10}}{a}_{i}^{2} \leq  {\mathrm{C}}_{10}^{2},\]

于是所连线段数目

\[\frac{1}{2}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{{10}}{a}_{i} \leq  \frac{1}{2}\sqrt{{10} \cdot  \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{{10}}{a}_{i}^{2}} = {15}.\]

接下来构造包含 15 条线段的图形, 此时从每个顶点出发的线段数均为 3 , 如图.

<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( {P}_{6} \) \( {P}_{1} \) \( {P}_{10} \) \( {P}_{5} \) \( {P}_{4} \) \( {P}_{9} \) \( {P}_{7} \) \( {P}_{2} \) \( {P}_{3} \) \( {P}_{8} \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_164.jpg?x=690&y=1124&w=337&h=315&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

设 \( p \) 与 \( p + 2 \) 均是素数, \( p > 3 \) . 数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 定义为

\[{a}_{1} = 2,{a}_{n} = {a}_{n - 1} + \left\lceil  \frac{p{a}_{n - 1}}{n}\right\rceil  ,n = 2,3,\cdots .\]

这里 \( \lceil x\rceil \) 表示不小于实数 \( x \) 的最小整数. 证明: 对 \( n = 3,4,\cdots ,p - 1 \) 均有 \( n \mid  p{a}_{n - 1} + 1 \) 成立.

解析

首先注意, \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 是整数数列.

对 \( n \) 用数学归纳法. 当 \( n = 3 \) 时,由条件知 \( {a}_{2} = 2 + p \) ,故 \( p{a}_{2} + 1 = {\left( p + 1\right) }^{2} \) . 因 \( p \) 与 \( p + 2 \) 均是素数,且 \( p > 3 \) ,故必须 \( 3 \mid  p + 1 \) . 因此 \( 3 \mid  p{a}_{2} + 1 \) ,即 \( n = 3 \) 时结论成立.


对 \( 3 < n \leq  p - 1 \) ,设对 \( k = 3,\cdots ,n - 1 \) 成立,此时 \( \left\lceil  \frac{p{a}_{k - 1}}{k}\right\rceil   = \frac{p{a}_{k - 1} + 1}{k} \) ,故

\[p{a}_{k - 1} + 1 = p\left( {{a}_{k - 2} + \left\lceil  \frac{p{a}_{k - 2}}{k - 1}\right\rceil  }\right)  + 1\]

\[ = p\left( {{a}_{k - 2} + \frac{p{a}_{k - 2} + 1}{k - 1}}\right)  + 1\]

\[ = \frac{\left( {p{a}_{k - 2} + 1}\right) \left( {p + k - 1}\right) }{k - 1}.\]

故对 \( 3 < n \leq  p - 1 \) ,有

\[p{a}_{n - 1} + 1 = \frac{p + n - 1}{n - 1}\left( {p{a}_{n - 2} + 1}\right) \]

\[ = \frac{p + n - 1}{n - 1} \cdot  \frac{p + n - 2}{n - 2}\left( {p{a}_{n - 3} + 1}\right) \]

\[ = \cdots \]

\[ = \frac{p + n - 1}{n - 1} \cdot  \frac{p + n - 2}{n - 2}\cdots \frac{p + 3}{3}\left( {p{a}_{2} + 1}\right) ,\]

因此

\[p{a}_{n - 1} + 1 = \frac{{2n}\left( {p + 1}\right) }{\left( {p + n}\right) \left( {p + 2}\right) }{\mathrm{C}}_{p + n}^{n}.\]

由此知 (注意 \( {\mathrm{C}}_{p + n}^{n} \) 是整数)

\[n \mid  \left( {p + n}\right) \left( {p + 2}\right) \left( {p{a}_{n - 1} + 1}\right) .\]

因 \( n < p,p \) 为素数,故 \( \left( {n,n + p}\right)  = \left( {n,p}\right)  = 1 \) ,又 \( p + 2 \) 是大于 \( n \) 的素数,故 \( \left( {n,p + 2}\right)  = 1 \) , 从而 \( n \) 与 \( \left( {p + n}\right) \left( {p + 2}\right) \) 互素,故 \( n \mid  p{a}_{n - 1} + 1 \) . 由数学归纳法知,本题得证.


## 2015 年全国高中数学联赛一试答案

## 一、 填空题: 本大题共 8 小题, 每小题 8 分, 满分 64 分.

1. 设 \( a,b \) 是不相等的实数,若二次函数 \( f\left( x\right)  = {x}^{2} + {ax} + b \) 满足 \( f\left( a\right)  = f\left( b\right) \) ,则 \( f\left( 2\right) \) 的值为 _____.

解析 4.

\( x = \frac{a + b}{2} \) 是 \( f\left( x\right) \) 的对称轴,于是可得 \( {2a} + b = 0 \) .

2. 若实数 \( \alpha \) 满足 \( \cos \alpha  = \tan \alpha \) ,则 \( \frac{1}{\sin \alpha } + {\cos }^{4}\alpha \) 的值为 _____.

解析 2.

\( {\sin }^{2}\alpha  + \sin \alpha  = 1 \) ,于是

\[\frac{1}{\sin \alpha } + {\cos }^{4}\alpha  = \sin \alpha  + 1 + {\sin }^{2}\alpha  = 2.\]

3. 已知复数数列 \( \left\{  {z}_{n}\right\} \) 满足 \( {z}_{1} = 1,{z}_{n + 1} = \overline{{z}_{n}} + 1 + n\mathrm{i} \) ,其中 \( n = 1,2,\cdots \) ,其中 \( \mathrm{i} \) 是虚数单位, \( \overline{{z}_{n}} \) 表示 \( {z}_{n} \) 的共轭复数,则 \( {z}_{2015} \) 的值为 _____.

解析 \( {2015} + {1007}\mathrm{i} \) .

\( {z}_{n + 2} = {z}_{n} + 2 + \mathrm{i}. \)

4. 在矩形 \( {ABCD} \) 中, \( {AB} = 2,{AD} = 1 \) ,在 \( {DC} \) 边上(包含点 \( D \) 、 \( C \) )的动点 \( P \) 与 \( {CB} \) 延长线上 (包含 \( B \) ) 的动点 \( Q \) 满足 \( \left| \overrightarrow{DP}\right|  = \left| \overrightarrow{BQ}\right| \) ,则向量 \( \overrightarrow{PA} \) 与向量 \( \overrightarrow{PQ} \) 的数量积 \( \overrightarrow{PA} \cdot  \overrightarrow{PQ} \) 的最小值为 _____.

解析 \( \frac{3}{4} \) .

如图建系即可,设 \( {DP} = {BQ} = x \) ,则有

\[\overrightarrow{PA} \cdot  \overrightarrow{PQ} = \left( {x,1}\right)  \cdot  \left( {x - 2,1 + x}\right)  = {\left( x - \frac{1}{2}\right) }^{2} + \frac{3}{4}.\]

5. 在正方体中随机取 3 条棱,它们两两异面的概率为 _____.

解析 \( \frac{2}{55} \) .

将正方体的 12 条棱按方向分为 3 组,从第一组中任取一条棱,有四种取法；再从第二组中任取一条棱, 有两种取法; 最后一组中只剩下一条棱与它们异面, 所以所求概率

\[P = \frac{4 \times  2}{{\mathrm{C}}_{12}^{3}} = \frac{8}{220} = \frac{2}{55}.\]

6. 在平面直角坐标系 \( {xOy} \) 中,点集

\[K = \{ \left( {x,y}\right)  \mid  \left( {\left| x\right|  + \left| {3y}\right|  - 6}\right) \left( {\left| {3x}\right|  + \left| y\right|  - 6}\right)  \leq  0\} \]

所对应的平面区域的面积为_____.

解析 24.

考虑到对称性, 先处理第一象限的情形.

7. 设 \( \omega \) 为正实数,若存在 \( a,b \) ( \( \pi  \leq  a < b \leq  {2\pi } \) ),使得 \( \sin {\omega a} + \sin {\omega b} = 2 \) ,则 \( \omega \) 的取值范围是_____.

解析 \( \left\lbrack  {\frac{9}{4},\frac{5}{2}}\right\rbrack   \cup  \left\lbrack  {\frac{13}{4}, + \infty }\right) \) .

由 \( \sin x \in  \left\lbrack  {-1,1}\right\rbrack \) 知,本题条件可以转化成存在 \( a,b \in  \left\lbrack  {\pi ,{2\pi }}\right\rbrack  ,a \neq  b \) ,使得

\[\sin {\omega a} = \sin {\omega b} = 1.\]


也即 \( y = \sin {\omega x} \) 在 \( \left\lbrack  {\pi ,{2\pi }}\right\rbrack \) 上存在两个不同的最大值点.

\( y = \sin {\omega x} \) 的曲线由正弦曲线 \( y = \sin x \) 在横方向上进行伸缩得到的,且必有 \( \omega  > 1 \) ,即图象一定会进行压缩, 如图:

<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( y \) \( A \) \( B \) 13π \( x \) O \( {5\pi } \) \( x = {\pi x} = {2\pi } \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_168.jpg?x=528&y=436&w=661&h=225&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

当最大值点 \( A,B,C,\cdots \) 中至少存在两个点经过压缩进入阴影区域时,满足题意.

考虑最大值点 \( A,B,C,\cdots \) 恰好压缩到边界 \( \pi \) 与 \( {2\pi } \) 时 \( \omega \) 的值,如下:

<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: O 9π \( B \) \( B \) \( B \) \( B \) C \( B \) \( \omega  = \frac{9}{4} \) 1A \( \omega  = \frac{5}{2} \) I \( \omega  = \frac{13}{4} \) \( A \) \( A \) \( \omega  = 4 \) \( A \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_168.jpg?x=472&y=823&w=780&h=442&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

易知当 \( \omega \) 从 1 逐渐增大时, \( A \) 点先到达右边界 \( {2\pi } \) ,此时不满足条件,当 \( B \) 点到达右边界时开始满足,直到 \( A \) 点到达左边界 \( \pi \) ,故 \( \omega  \in  \left\lbrack  {\frac{9}{4},\frac{5}{2}}\right\rbrack \) 时,满足题意;

之后, \( \omega \) 继续增加时, \( A \) 出左边界,只有 \( B \) 点在区域内,此时不满足,直到 \( \omega  = \frac{13}{4} \) 时, \( C \) 点压缩到右边界,此时 \( B,C \) 两个最值点都在区域内,重新满足条件,直到 \( B \) 出左边界,此时需要考虑 \( C \) 右边下一个最大值点.

但因为此时 \( \omega  = \frac{9}{2} > 4 \) ,边界内已经存在至少两个周期,故此时区域内至少含有两个最大值点,一定满足条件,故 \( \omega  \geq  \frac{13}{4} \) 时一定满足.

8. 对四位数 \( \overline{abcd}\left( {1 \leq  a \leq  9,0 \leq  b,c,d \leq  9}\right) \) ,若 \( a > b,b < c,c > d \) ,则称 \( \overline{abcd} \) 为 \( P \) 类数,若 \( a < b,b > c,c < d \) ,则称 \( \overline{abcd} \) 为 \( Q \) 类数. 用 \( N\left( P\right) \) 与 \( N\left( Q\right) \) 分别表示 \( P \) 类数与 \( Q \) 类数的个数,则 \( N\left( P\right)  - N\left( Q\right) \) 的值为_____.

解析 285.

一个 \( Q \) 类数 \( \overline{abcd} \) 与一个 \( P \) 类数 \( \overline{dcba} \) 对应; 因为 \( a \neq  0 \) ,所以所有以 0 结尾的 \( P \) 类数


即为所求.

当 \( a = c \) 时,以 0 结尾的 \( P \) 类数有 \( {\mathrm{C}}_{10}^{2} = {45} \) 个;

当 \( a \neq  c \) 时,以 0 结尾的 \( P \) 类数有 \( {\mathrm{C}}_{10}^{3}{\mathrm{\;A}}_{2}^{2} = {240} \) 个;

所以 \( N\left( P\right)  - N\left( Q\right)  = {285} \) .

## 二、 解答题：本大题共 3 小题,满分 56 分. 解答应写出文字说明、证明过程或演算步骤. 其 中第 9 题满分 16 分, 第 10、11 题满分 20 分.

9. 若实数 \( a,b,c \) 满足 \( {2}^{a} + {4}^{b} = {2}^{c},{4}^{a} + {2}^{b} = {4}^{c} \) ,求 \( c \) 的最小值.

解析 \( {\log }_{2}3 - \frac{5}{3} \) .

记 \( x = {2}^{a},y = {2}^{b},z = {2}^{c} \) ,则

\[\left\{  \begin{array}{l} x + {y}^{2} = z \\  {x}^{2} + y = {z}^{2} \end{array}\right. \]

消元得

\[{\left( z - {y}^{2}\right) }^{2} + y = {z}^{2},\]

整理得

\[z = \frac{{y}^{2}}{2} + \frac{1}{2y} = \frac{{y}^{2}}{2} + \frac{1}{4y} + \frac{1}{4y} \geq  3\sqrt[3]{\frac{{y}^{2}}{2} \cdot  \frac{1}{4y} \cdot  \frac{1}{4y}} = \frac{3}{4}\sqrt[3]{2},\]

等号当 \( y = \frac{1}{\sqrt[3]{2}},x = \frac{\sqrt[3]{2}}{4} \) 时取得. 于是 \( z \) 的最小值为 \( \frac{3}{4}\sqrt[3]{2} \) ,进而 \( c \) 的最小值为

\[{\log }_{2}\left( {\frac{3}{4}\sqrt[3]{2}}\right)  = {\log }_{2}3 - \frac{5}{3}.\]

10. 设 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},{a}_{3},{a}_{4} \) 是 4 个有理数,使得

\[\left\{  {{a}_{i}{a}_{j} \mid  1 \leq  i < j \leq  4}\right\}   = \left\{  {-{24}, - 2, - \frac{3}{2}, - \frac{1}{8},1,3}\right\}  ,\]

求 \( {a}_{1} + {a}_{2} + {a}_{3} + {a}_{4} \) 的值.

解析 \( {a}_{1} + {a}_{2} + {a}_{3} + {a}_{4} =  \pm  \frac{9}{4} \) .

设 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},{a}_{3},{a}_{4} \) 的绝对值从小到大排列,则

\[\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {a}_{1}{a}_{2} =  - \frac{1}{8}, \\  {a}_{1}{a}_{3} = 1, \\  {a}_{2}{a}_{4} = 3, \\  {a}_{3}{a}_{4} =  - {24}, \\  \left\{  {{a}_{2}{a}_{3},{a}_{1}{a}_{4}}\right\}   = \left\{  {-2, - \frac{3}{2}}\right\}  , \end{array}\right. \]


解得

\[\left( {{a}_{1},{a}_{2},{a}_{3},{a}_{4}}\right)  = \left( {\frac{1}{4}, - \frac{1}{2},4, - 6}\right)  \vee  \left( {-\frac{1}{4},\frac{1}{2}, - 4,6}\right) ,\]

于是 \( {a}_{1} + {a}_{2} + {a}_{3} + {a}_{4} =  \pm  \frac{9}{4} \) .

11. 在平面直角坐标系 \( {xOy} \) 中, \( {F}_{1},{F}_{2} \) 分别是椭圆 \( \frac{{x}^{2}}{2} + {y}^{2} = 1 \) 的左、右焦点,设不经过焦点 \( {F}_{1} \) 的直线 \( l \) 与椭圆交于两个不同的点 \( A,B \) ,焦点 \( {F}_{2} \) 到直线 \( l \) 的距离为 \( d \) . 如果直线 \( A{F}_{1},l,B{F}_{1} \) 的斜率依次成等差数列,求 \( d \) 的取值范围. 解析 \( \left( {\sqrt{3},2}\right) \) .

根据已知,有 \( {F}_{1}\left( {-1,0}\right) ,{F}_{2}\left( {1,0}\right) \) .

设 \( l : y = {kx} + m,A\left( {{x}_{1},{y}_{1}}\right) ,B\left( {{x}_{2},{y}_{2}}\right) \) ,则联立直线与椭圆方程得

\[\left( {2{k}^{2} + 1}\right) {x}^{2} + {4kmx} + 2{m}^{2} - 2 = 0,\]

判别式

\[\Delta  = 8\left( {2{k}^{2} + 1 - {m}^{2}}\right)  > 0,\]

即

\[2{k}^{2} + 1 > {m}^{2}\text{.}\]

由题意直线 \( A{F}_{1}\text{、}l\text{、}B{F}_{1} \) 的斜率成等差数列,得

\[\frac{{y}_{1}}{{x}_{1} + 1} + \frac{{y}_{2}}{{x}_{2} + 1} = {2k}\]

将 \( {y}_{1} = k{x}_{1} + m,{y}_{2} = k{x}_{2} + m \) 代入并整理得

\[\left( {m - k}\right) \left( {{x}_{1} + {x}_{2} + 2}\right)  = 0,\]

由直线 \( l \) 不经过 \( {F}_{1} \) 点,舍去 \( m - k = 0 \) ,于是

\[{x}_{1} + {x}_{2} =  - 2,\]

结合韦达定理有

\[ - \frac{4km}{2{k}^{2} + 1} =  - 2,\]

即

\[m = k + \frac{1}{2k}\]

由此可得 \( {k}^{2} \) 的取值范围由

\[2{k}^{2} + 1 > {m}^{2} = {\left( k + \frac{1}{2k}\right) }^{2}\]


确定, 即

\[{k}^{2} > \frac{1}{2}\]

点 \( {F}_{2}\left( {1,0}\right) \) 到直线 \( l \) 的距离为

\[d = \frac{\left| k + m\right| }{\sqrt{1 + {k}^{2}}} = \sqrt{\frac{{k}^{2}}{1 + {k}^{2}}} \cdot  \left( {2 + \frac{1}{2{k}^{2}}}\right) ,\]

结合 \( {k}^{2} \) 的取值范围可得 \( d \) 的取值范围为 \( \left( {\sqrt{3},2}\right) \) .


## 2015 年全国高中数学联赛二试答案

一、 设 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},\cdots ,{a}_{n}\left( {n \geq  2}\right) \) 是实数,证明: 可以选取 \( {\varepsilon }_{1},{\varepsilon }_{2},\cdots ,{\varepsilon }_{n} \in  \{  - 1,1\} \) ,使得

\[{\left( \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}{a}_{i}\right) }^{2} + {\left( \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}{\varepsilon }_{i}{a}_{i}\right) }^{2} \leq  \left( {n + 1}\right) \left( {\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}{a}_{i}^{2}}\right) .\]

解析

解法一:

我们证明

\[{\left( \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}{a}_{i}\right) }^{2} + {\left( \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{m}{a}_{i} - \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = m + 1}}^{n}{a}_{i}\right) }^{2} \leq  \left( {n + 1}\right) \left( {\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}{a}_{i}^{2}}\right) ,\]

其中 \( m = \left\lbrack  \frac{n}{2}\right\rbrack \) ,即

\[{\varepsilon }_{i} = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} 1, & i = 1,2,\cdots ,m, \\   - 1, & i = m + 1,m + 2,\cdots ,n. \end{array}\right. \]

事实上, 上述不等式的左边为

\[{\left( \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{m}{a}_{i} + \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{j = m + 1}}^{n}{a}_{j}\right) }^{2} + {\left( \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{m}{a}_{i} - \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{j = m + 1}}^{n}{a}_{j}\right) }^{2}\]

\[ = 2{\left( \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{m}{a}_{i}\right) }^{2} + 2{\left( \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{j = m + 1}}^{n}{a}_{j}\right) }^{2}\]

\[ \leq  {2m}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{m}{a}_{i}^{2} + 2\left( {n - m}\right) \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{j = m + 1}}^{n}{a}_{j}^{2}\]

\[ = 2\left\lbrack  \frac{n}{2}\right\rbrack  \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{m}{a}_{i}^{2} + 2\left\lbrack  \frac{n + 1}{2}\right\rbrack  \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{j = m + 1}}^{n}{a}_{j}^{2}\]

\[ \leq  n\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{m}{a}_{i}^{2} + \left( {n + 1}\right) \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{j = m + 1}}^{n}{a}_{j}^{2}\]

\[ \leq  \left( {n + 1}\right) \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}{a}_{i}^{2}\]

其中第三行用到了柯西不等式. 从而不等式得证, 原题得证.

解法二:

首先,由于问题中 \( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},\cdots ,{a}_{n} \) 的对称性,可设 \( {a}_{1} \geq  {a}_{2} \geq  \cdots  \geq  {a}_{n} \) ,此外,若将


\( {a}_{1},{a}_{2},\cdots ,{a}_{n} \) 中的负数均改变符号,则问题中的不等式左边的 \( {\left( \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}{a}_{i}\right) }^{2} \) 不减,而右边的 \( \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}{a}_{i}^{2} \) 不变,并且此变化不影响 \( \varepsilon \) 的选取,因此我们可以进一步设 \( {a}_{1} \geq  {a}_{2} \geq  \cdots {a}_{n} \geq \) 0.

引理: 设 \( {a}_{1} \geq  {a}_{2} \geq  \cdots {a}_{n} \geq  n \) ,则

\[0 \leq  \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}{\left( -1\right) }^{i - 1}{a}_{i} \leq  {a}_{1}.\]

引理的证明从略.

于是回到原题, 由柯西不等式及上述引理可得

\[{\left( \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}{a}_{i}\right) }^{2} + {\left( \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}{\left( -1\right) }^{i - 1}{a}_{i}\right) }^{2} \leq  n\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}{a}_{i}^{2} + {a}_{1}^{2} \leq  \left( {n + 1}\right) \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}{a}_{i}^{2},\]

这就证明了结论.

二、设 \( S = \left\{  {{A}_{1},{A}_{2},\cdots ,{A}_{n}}\right\} \) ,其中 \( {A}_{1},{A}_{2},\cdots ,{A}_{n} \) 是 \( n \) 个互不相同的有限集合 \( \left( {n \geq  2}\right) \) , 满足对任意 \( {A}_{i},{A}_{j} \in  S \) ,均有 \( {A}_{i} \cup  {A}_{j} \in  S \) . 若 \( k = \mathop{\min }\limits_{{1 \leq  i \leq  n}}\left| {A}_{i}\right|  \geq  2 \) . 证明: 存在 \( x \in  \mathop{\bigcup }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}{A}_{i} \) , 使得 \( x \) 属于 \( {A}_{1},{A}_{2},\cdots ,{A}_{n} \) 中的至少 \( \frac{n}{k} \) 个集合(这里 \( \left| X\right| \) 表示有限集合 \( X \) 的元素个数).

解析

不妨设 \( \left| {A}_{1}\right|  = k \) . 设在 \( {A}_{1},{A}_{2},\cdots ,{A}_{n} \) 中与 \( {A}_{1} \) 不相交的集合有 \( s \) 个,重新记为 \( {B}_{1},{B}_{2},\cdots ,{B}_{s} \) , 设包含 \( {A}_{1} \) 的集合有 \( t \) 个,重新记为 \( {C}_{1},{C}_{2},\cdots ,{C}_{t} \) . 由已知条件 \( \left( {{B}_{i} \cup  {A}_{1}}\right)  \in  S \) ,即

\[\left( {{B}_{i} \cup  {A}_{1}}\right)  \in  \left\{  {{C}_{1},{C}_{2},\cdots ,{C}_{t}}\right\}  \]

这样我们得到一个映射

\[f : \left\{  {{B}_{1},{B}_{2},\cdots ,{B}_{s}}\right\}   \rightarrow  \left\{  {{C}_{1},{C}_{2},\cdots ,{C}_{t}}\right\}  ,f\left( {B}_{i}\right)  = {B}_{i} \cup  {A}_{1},\]

显然 \( f \) 是单射,于是 \( s \leq  t \) . 设 \( {A}_{1} = \left\{  {{a}_{1},{a}_{2},\cdots ,{a}_{k}}\right\} \) . 在 \( {A}_{1},{A}_{2},\cdots ,{A}_{n} \) 中除去 \( {B}_{1},{B}_{2},\cdots ,{B}_{s},{C}_{1},{C}_{2},\cdots ,{C}_{t} \) 后在剩下的 \( n - s - t \) 个集合中,设包含 \( {a}_{i} \) 的集合有 \( {x}_{i} \) 个 \( \left( {1 \leq  i \leq  k}\right) \) ,由于剩下的 \( n - s - t \) 个集合中每个集合与 \( {A}_{1} \) 的交集非空,即包含某个 \( {a}_{i} \) ,从而

\[{x}_{1} + {x}_{2} + \cdots  + {x}_{k} \geq  n - s - t.\]

不妨设 \( {x}_{1} = \max \left\{  {{x}_{1},{x}_{2},\cdots ,{x}_{k}}\right\} \) ,则由上式知

\[{x}_{1} \geq  \frac{n - s - t}{k}\]


即在剩下的 \( n - s - t \) 个集合中,包含 \( {a}_{1} \) 的集合至少有 \( \frac{n - s - t}{k} \) 个.

又由于 \( {A}_{1} \subseteq  {C}_{i}\left( {i = 1,2,\cdots ,t}\right) \) ,故 \( {C}_{1},{C}_{2},\cdots ,{C}_{t} \) 都包含 \( {a}_{1} \) ,因此包含 \( {a}_{1} \) 的集合个

数至少为

\[\frac{n - s - t}{k} + t = \frac{n - s + t\left( {k - 1}\right) }{k} \geq  \frac{n - s + t}{k} \geq  \frac{n}{k}.\]

三、如图, \( \bigtriangleup {ABC} \) 内接于圆 \( O,P \) 为弧 \( {BC} \) 上一点,点 \( K \) 在线段 \( {AP} \) 上,使得 \( {BK} \) 平分 \( \angle {ABC} \) . 过 \( K\text{、}P\text{、}C \) 三点的圆 \( \Omega \) 与边 \( {AC} \) 交于点 \( D \) ,连接 \( {BD} \) 交圆 \( \Omega \) 于点 \( E \) ,连接 \( {PE} \) 并延长与边 \( {AB} \) 交于点 \( F \) ,证明: \( \angle {ABC} = 2\angle {FCB} \) .

<!-- Media -->

解析

解法一:

设 \( {CF} \) 与圆 \( \Omega \) 交于点 \( L \) (异于 \( C \) ). 连接 \( {PB}\text{、}{PC}\text{、}{BL}\text{、}{KL} \) .

<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( F \) \( A \) Og I \( K \) \( D \) . E \( P \) \( B \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_174.jpg?x=698&y=1179&w=323&h=344&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

注意此时 \( C\text{、}D\text{、}L\text{、}K\text{、}E\text{、}P \) 六点均在圆 \( \Omega \) 上,结合 \( A\text{、}B\text{、}P\text{、}C \) 四点共圆,可知

\[\angle {FEB} = \angle {DEP} = {180}^{ \circ  } - \angle {DCP} = \angle {ABP} = \angle {FBP},\]

因此 \( \bigtriangleup {FBE} \sim  \bigtriangleup {FPB} \) ,因此

\[F{B}^{2} = {FE} \cdot  {FP}.\]

又由圆幂定理可知, \( {FE} \cdot  {FP} = {FL} \cdot  {FC} \) ,所以

\[F{B}^{2} = {FL} \cdot  {FC},\]


因此 \( \bigtriangleup {FBL} \sim  \bigtriangleup {FCB} \) . 因此

\[\angle {FLB} = \angle {FBC} = \angle {APC} = \angle {KPC} = \angle {KLC},\]

即 \( B\text{、}K\text{、}L \) 三点共线. 再根据 \( \bigtriangleup {FBL} \sim  \bigtriangleup {FCB} \) 得

\[\angle {FCB} = \angle {FBL} = \angle {FBK} = \frac{1}{2}\angle {ABC},\]

即 \( \angle {ABC} = 2\angle {FCB} \) . 解法二:

设 \( {CF} \) 与圆 \( \Omega \) 交于点 \( L \) (异于 \( C \) ).

<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( F \) Og IX \( D \) I \( B\left( {B}^{\prime }\right. \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_175.jpg?x=675&y=684&w=368&h=346&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

对圆内接广义六边形 \( {DCPELK} \) 应用帕斯卡定理可知, \( {DC} \) 与 \( {KP} \) 的交点 \( A\text{、}{CL} \) 与 \( {PE} \) 的交点 \( F\text{、}{LK} \) 与 \( {ED} \) 的交点 \( {B}^{\prime } \) 共线,因此 \( {B}^{\prime } \) 是 \( {AF} \) 与 \( {ED} \) 的交点,即 \( {B}^{\prime } = B \) , 所以 \( B\text{、}K\text{、}L \) 共线. 根据 \( A\text{、}B\text{、}P\text{、}C \) 四点共圆及 \( L\text{、}K\text{、}P\text{、}C \) 四点共圆,得

\[\angle {ABC} = \angle {APC} = \angle {KLC} = \angle {FCB} + \angle {LBC},\]

又由 \( {BK} \) 平分 \( \angle {ABC} \) 知

\[\angle {ABC} = 2\angle {LBC},\]

从而 \( \angle {ABC} = 2\angle {FCB} \) .

四、求具有下列性质的所有正整数 \( k \) : 对任意正整数 \( n,{2}^{\left( {k - 1}\right) n + 1} \) 不整除 \( \frac{\left( {kn}\right) !}{n!} \) .

解析 \( k \) 为 \( {2}^{a} \) ,其中 \( a = 0,1,2,\cdots \) .

对正整数 \( m \) ,设 \( {v}_{2}\left( m\right) \) 表示正整数 \( m \) 的标准分解中素因子 2 的方幂,则熟知

\[{v}_{2}\left( {m!}\right)  = m - S\left( m\right) ,\]

这里 \( S\left( m\right) \) 表示正整数 \( m \) 在二进制表示下的数码之和. 由于 \( {2}^{\left( {k - 1}\right) n + 1} \) 不整除 \( \frac{\left( {kn}\right) !}{n!} \) 等

价于

\[{v}_{2}\left( \frac{\left( {kn}\right) !}{n!}\right)  \leq  \left( {k - 1}\right) n\]


即

\[{kn} - {v}_{2}\left( {\left( {kn}\right) !}\right)  \geq  n - {v}_{2}\left( {n!}\right) ,\]

进而本题等价于求所有正整数 \( k \) ,使得 \( S\left( {kn}\right)  \geq  S\left( n\right) \) 对任意正整数 \( n \) 成立. 我们证明, 所有符合条件的 \( k \) 为 \( {2}^{a} \) ,其中 \( a = 0,1,2,\cdots \) . 一方面,由于 \( S\left( {{2}^{a}n}\right)  = S\left( n\right) \) 对任意正整数 \( n \) 成立,故 \( k = {2}^{a} \) 符合条件. 另一方面,若 \( k \) 不是 2 的方幂,设 \( k = {2}^{a} \cdot  q,a \geq  0 \) , \( q \) 是大于 1 的奇数. 下面构造一个正整数 \( n \) ,使得 \( S\left( {kn}\right)  < S\left( n\right) \) . 因为

\[S\left( {kn}\right)  = S\left( {{2}^{a}{qn}}\right)  = S\left( {qn}\right) ,\]

因此问题等价于我们选取的 \( q \) 的一个倍数 \( m \) ,使得

\[S\left( m\right)  < S\left( \frac{m}{q}\right) .\]

由 \( \left( {2,q}\right)  = 1 \) ,熟知存在正整数 \( u \) ,使得 \( {2}^{u} \equiv  1\left( {\;\operatorname{mod}\;q}\right) \) . (事实上,由欧拉定理知, \( u \) 可以取 \( \varphi \left( q\right) \) .) 设奇数 \( q \) 的二进制表示为

\[{2}^{{\alpha }_{1}} + {2}^{{\alpha }_{2}} + \cdots  + {2}^{{\alpha }_{t}}\]

其中 \( 0 = {\alpha }_{1} < {\alpha }_{2} < \cdots  < {\alpha }_{t},t \geq  2 \) . 取 \( m = {2}^{{\alpha }_{1}} + {2}^{{\alpha }_{2}} + \cdots  + {2}^{{\alpha }_{t} + {tu}} \) ,则 \( S\left( m\right)  = t \) ,且

\[m = q + {2}^{{\alpha }_{t}}\left( {{2}^{tu} - 1}\right)  \equiv  0\;\left( {\;\operatorname{mod}\;q}\right) .\]

我们有

\[\frac{m}{q} = 1 + {2}^{{\alpha }_{t}} \cdot  \frac{{2}^{tu} - 1}{q}\]

\[ = 1 + {2}^{{\alpha }_{t}} \cdot  \frac{{2}^{u} - 1}{q}\left( {1 + {2}^{u} + \cdots  + {2}^{\left( {t - 1}\right) u}}\right) \]

\[ = 1 + \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 0}}^{{t - 1}}\frac{{2}^{u} - 1}{q} \cdot  {2}^{{iu} + {\alpha }_{t}}.\]

由于 \( 0 < \frac{{2}^{u} - 1}{q} < {2}^{u} \) ,故正整数 \( \frac{{2}^{u} - 1}{q} \) 的二进制表示中的最高次幂小于 \( u \) ,由此可得,对任意整数 \( i,j\left( {0 \leq  i < j \leq  t - 1}\right) \) ,数 \( \frac{{2}^{u} - 1}{q} \cdot  {2}^{{iu} + {\alpha }_{t}} \) 与 \( \frac{{2}^{u} - 1}{q} \cdot  {2}^{{ju} + {\alpha }_{t}} \) 的二进制表示中没有相同的项. 又因为 \( {\alpha }_{t} > 0 \) ,故 \( \frac{{2}^{u} - 1}{q} \cdot  {2}^{{iu} + {\alpha }_{t}}\left( {i = 0,1,2,\cdots ,t - 1}\right) \) 的二进制表示中均不包含 1 , 故

\[S\left( \frac{m}{q}\right)  = 1 + S\left( \frac{{2}^{u} - 1}{q}\right)  \cdot  t > t = S\left( m\right) ,\]

因此上述选取的 \( m \) 满足要求.

综合上述的两个方面可知,所求 \( k \) 为 \( {2}^{a} \) ,其中 \( a = 0,1,2,\cdots \) .


## 2014 年全国高中数学联赛一试答案

## 一、 填空题: 本大题共 8 小题, 每小题 8 分, 满分 64 分.

1. 若正数 \( a,b \) 满足 \( 2 + {\log }_{2}a = 3 + {\log }_{3}b = {\log }_{6}\left( {a + b}\right) \) ,则 \( \frac{1}{a} + \frac{1}{b} \) 的值为_____.

解析 108.

设

\[2 + {\log }_{2}a = 3 + {\log }_{3}b = {\log }_{6}\left( {a + b}\right)  = k,\]

则

\[a = {2}^{k - 2},b = {3}^{k - 3},a + b = {6}^{k},\]

从而

\[\frac{1}{a} + \frac{1}{b} = \frac{a + b}{ab} = \frac{{6}^{k}}{{2}^{k - 2} \times  {3}^{k - 3}} = {108}.\]

2. 设集合 \( \left\{  {\left. {\frac{3}{a} + b}\right| \;1 \leq  a \leq  b \leq  2}\right\} \) 中的最大元素与最小元素分别为 \( M,m \) ,则 \( M - m \) 的

值为 _____.

解析 \( 5 - 2\sqrt{3} \) .

由 \( 1 \leq  a \leq  b \leq  2 \) 知,

\[\frac{3}{a} + b \leq  \frac{3}{1} + 2 = 5\]

当 \( a = 1,b = 2 \) 时,得最大元素 \( M = 5 \) .

又

\[\frac{3}{a} + b \geq  \frac{3}{a} + a \geq  2\sqrt{\frac{3}{a} \cdot  a} = 2\sqrt{3},\]

当 \( a = b = \sqrt{3} \) 时,得最小元素 \( m = 2\sqrt{3} \) .

因此, \( M - m = 5 - 2\sqrt{3} \) .

3. 若函数 \( f\left( x\right)  = {x}^{2} + a\left| {x - 1}\right| \) 在 \( \lbrack 0, + \infty ) \) 上单调递增,则实数 \( a \) 的取值范围是 _____.

解析 \( \left\lbrack  {-2,0}\right\rbrack \) .

情形 1: 在 \( \lbrack 1, + \infty ) \) 上, \( f\left( x\right)  = {x}^{2} + {ax} - a \) 单调递增,等价于

\[ - \frac{a}{2} \leq  1\]

即 \( a \geq   - 2 \) .

情形 2: 在 \( \left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack \) 上, \( f\left( x\right)  = {x}^{2} - {ax} + a \) 单调递增,等价于

\[\frac{a}{2} \leq  0\]


即 \( a \leq  0 \) . 因此实数 \( a \) 的取值范围是 \( \left\lbrack  {-2,0}\right\rbrack \) .

4. 数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 满足 \( {a}_{1} = 2,{a}_{n + 1} = \frac{2\left( {n + 2}\right) }{n + 1}{a}_{n}\left( {n \in  {\mathbb{N}}^{ * }}\right) \) ,则 \( \frac{{a}_{2014}}{{a}_{1} + {a}_{2} + \cdots  + {a}_{2013}} = \)

_____.

解析 \( \frac{2015}{2013} \) .

由题设

\[{a}_{n} = \frac{2\left( {n + 1}\right) }{n}{a}_{n - 1}\]

\[ = \frac{2\left( {n + 1}\right) }{n} \cdot  \frac{2n}{n - 1}{a}_{n - 2} = \cdots \]

\[ = \frac{2\left( {n + 1}\right) }{n} \cdot  \frac{2n}{n - 1}\cdots  \cdot  \frac{2 \cdot  3}{2}{a}_{1}\]

\[ = {2}^{n - 1}\left( {n + 1}\right) \text{.}\]

记数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 的前 \( n \) 项和为 \( {S}_{n} \) ,则

\[{S}_{n} = 2 + 2 \times  3 + {2}^{2} \times  4 + \cdots  + {2}^{n - 1}\left( {n + 1}\right) ,\]

所以

\[2{S}_{n} = 2 \times  2 + {2}^{2} \times  3 + {2}^{3} \times  4 + \cdots  + {2}^{n}\left( {n + 1}\right) ,\]

将上面两式相减, 得

\[{S}_{n} = {2}^{n}\left( {n + 1}\right)  - \left( {{2}^{n - 1} + {2}^{n - 2} + \cdots  + 2 + 2}\right) \]

\[ = {2}^{n}\left( {n + 1}\right)  - {2}^{n}\]

\[ = {2}^{n}n\]

故

\[\frac{{a}_{2014}}{{a}_{1} + {a}_{2} + \cdots  + {a}_{2013}} = \frac{{2}^{2013} \times  {2015}}{{2}^{2013} \times  {2013}} = \frac{2015}{2013}.\]

5. 正四棱锥 \( P - {ABCD} \) 中,侧面是边长为 1 的正三角形, \( M,N \) 分别是边 \( {AB},{BC} \) 的中点,则异面直线 \( {MN} \) 与 \( {PC} \) 之间的距离是 _____.

解析 \( \frac{\sqrt{2}}{4} \) .

设底面对角线 \( {AC},{BD} \) 交于点 \( O \) ,过点 \( C \) 作直线 \( {MN} \) 的垂线,交 \( {MN} \) 于点 \( H \) .

由于 \( {PO} \) 是底面的垂线,故

\[{PO} \bot  {CH},\]

又 \( {AC} \bot  {CH} \) ,所以

<!-- Meanless: \( {CH} \bot \) 平面 \( {POC} \) ,-->




故

\[{CH} \bot  {PC}\text{.}\]

因此 \( {CH} \) 是直线 \( {MN} \) 与 \( {PC} \) 的公垂线.

又因为

\[{CH} = \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}{CN} = \frac{\sqrt{2}}{4},\]

故异面直线 \( {MN} \) 与 \( {PC} \) 之间的距离是 \( \frac{\sqrt{2}}{4} \) .

6. 设椭圆 \( \Gamma \) 的两个焦点是 \( {F}_{1},{F}_{2} \) ,过点 \( {F}_{1} \) 的直线与 \( \Gamma \) 交于点 \( P,Q \) . 若 \( \left| {P{F}_{2}}\right|  = \left| {{F}_{1}{F}_{2}}\right| \) , 且 \( 3\left| {P{F}_{1}}\right|  = 4\left| {Q{F}_{1}}\right| \) ,则椭圆 \( \Gamma \) 的短轴与长轴的比值为 _____.

解析 \( \frac{2\sqrt{6}}{7} \) .

不妨设 \( \left| {P{F}_{1}}\right|  = 4,\left| {Q{F}_{1}}\right|  = 3 \) .

记椭圆 \( \Gamma \) 的长轴、短轴的长度分别为 \( {2a},{2b} \) ,焦距为 \( {2c} \) ,则

\[\left| {P{F}_{2}}\right|  = \left| {{F}_{1}{F}_{2}}\right|  = {2c}.\]

由椭圆的定义知

\[{2a} = \left| {Q{F}_{1}}\right|  + \left| {Q{F}_{2}}\right|  = \left| {P{F}_{1}}\right|  + \left| {P{F}_{2}}\right|  = {2c} + 4,\]

于是

\[\left| {Q{F}_{2}}\right|  = \left| {P{F}_{1}}\right|  + \left| {P{F}_{2}}\right|  - \left| {Q{F}_{1}}\right|  = {2c} + 1.\]

设 \( H \) 为线段 \( P{F}_{1} \) 的中点,则

\[\left| {{F}_{1}H}\right|  = 2,\left| {QH}\right|  = 5,\]

且有 \( {F}_{2}H \bot  P{F}_{1} \) ,由勾股定理知

\[{\left| Q{F}_{2}\right| }^{2} - {\left| QH\right| }^{2} = {\left| {F}_{2}H\right| }^{2} = {\left| {F}_{1}{F}_{2}\right| }^{2} - {\left| {F}_{1}H\right| }^{2},\]

即

\[{\left( 2c + 1\right) }^{2} - {5}^{2} = {\left( 2c\right) }^{2} - {2}^{2},\]

解得 \( c = 5 \) ,进而 \( a = 7,b = 2\sqrt{6} \) .

因此椭圆 \( \Gamma \) 的短轴与长轴的比值为 \( \frac{b}{a} = \frac{2\sqrt{6}}{7} \) .


<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( P \) \( {F}_{2} \) \( H \) \( {F}_{1} \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_180.jpg?x=570&y=273&w=575&h=404&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

设等边三角形 \( {ABC} \) 的内切圆半径为 2,圆心为 \( I \) . 若点 \( P \) 满足 \( {PI} = 1 \) ,则 \( \bigtriangleup  {APB} \) 与 \( \bigtriangleup  {APC} \) 的面积之比的最大值为 _____.

解析 \( \frac{3 + \sqrt{5}}{2} \) .

由 \( {PI} = 1 \) 知点 \( P \) 在以 \( I \) 为圆心的单位圆 \( K \) 上.

设 \( \angle {BAP} = \alpha \) . 在圆 \( K \) 上取一点 \( {P}_{0} \) ,使得 \( \alpha \) 取到最大值 \( {\alpha }_{0} \) ,此时 \( {P}_{0} \) 应落在 \( \angle {IAC} \) 内,且是 \( A{P}_{0} \) 与圆 \( K \) 的切点.

<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: . \( B \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_180.jpg?x=548&y=1012&w=573&h=451&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->


由于 \( 0 < \alpha  \leq  {\alpha }_{0} < \frac{\pi }{3} \) ,故

\[\frac{{S}_{\bigtriangleup {APB}}}{{S}_{\bigtriangleup {APC}}} = \frac{\frac{1}{2}{AP} \cdot  {AB} \cdot  \sin \alpha }{\frac{1}{2}{AP} \cdot  {AC} \cdot  \sin \left( {\frac{\pi }{3} - \alpha }\right) }\]

\[ = \frac{\sin \alpha }{\sin \left( {\frac{\pi }{3} - \alpha }\right) }\]

\[ \leq  \frac{\sin {\alpha }_{0}}{\sin \left( {\frac{\pi }{3} - {\alpha }_{0}}\right) }\]

\[ = \frac{\sin \left( {\frac{\pi }{6} + \theta }\right) }{\sin \left( {\frac{\pi }{6} - \theta }\right) }.\]

①

其中, \( \theta  = {\alpha }_{0} - \frac{\pi }{6} = \angle {IA}{P}_{0} \) .

由 \( \angle A{P}_{0}I = \frac{\pi }{2} \) 知,

\[\sin \theta  = \frac{I{P}_{0}}{AI} = \frac{1}{2r} = \frac{1}{4},\]

于是 \( \cot \theta  = \sqrt{15} \) ,所以

\[\frac{\sin \left( {\frac{\pi }{6} + \theta }\right) }{\sin \left( {\frac{\pi }{6} - \theta }\right) } = \frac{\frac{1}{2}\cos \theta  + \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\sin \theta }{\frac{1}{2}\cos \theta  - \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\sin \theta }\]

\[ = \frac{\cot \theta  + \sqrt{3}}{\cot \theta  - \sqrt{3}}\]

\[ = \frac{3 + \sqrt{5}}{2}\text{. }\]

②

根据 ①② 可知,当 \( P = {P}_{0} \) 时, \( \bigtriangleup {APB} \) 与 \( \bigtriangleup {APC} \) 的面积之比的最大值为 \( \frac{3 + \sqrt{5}}{2} \) .

8. 设 \( A,B,C,D \) 是空间四个不共面的点,以 \( \frac{1}{2} \) 的概率在每对点之前连一条边,任意两对点之间是否连边是相互独立的,则 \( A,B \) 可用空间折线 (一条或若干条边组成的) 连接的概率为_____.

解析 \( \frac{3}{4} \) .

考虑反面:


<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( D \) \( B \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_182.jpg?x=746&y=279&w=225&h=235&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

解法一: 以 \( B,C \) 与 \( B,D \) 是否连边分情况讨论.

① 若 \( B,C \) 与 \( B,D \) 都不连边,则一定满足情况,所求概率为

\[\frac{1}{2} \times  \frac{1}{2} \times  \frac{1}{2} = \frac{1}{8}\]

② 若 \( B,C \) 与 \( B,D \) 都连边,那么 \( A,C \) 与 \( A,D \) 都不连边,所求概率为

\[{\left( \frac{1}{2}\right) }^{5} = \frac{1}{32}\]

③ 若 \( B,C \) 与 \( B,D \) 恰有一组连边,不妨考虑 \( B,C \) 连边, \( B,D \) 不连边,则 \( A,C \) 不连边, 且 \( C,D \) 与 \( A,D \) 不同时连边即可,所求概率为

\[\frac{1}{2} \times  \frac{1}{2} \times  \frac{1}{2} \times  \frac{1}{2} \times  \left( {1 - \frac{1}{4}}\right)  = \frac{3}{64}.\]

所以 \( A,B \) 不能用空间折线连接的概率为

\[\frac{1}{8} + \frac{1}{32} + 2 \times  \frac{3}{64} = \frac{1}{4}.\]

从而所求概率为 \( 1 - \frac{1}{4} = \frac{3}{4} \) .

解法二: 按 \( C,D \) 是否连边分两种情况讨论:

① 若 \( C,D \) 不连边,则满足条件的有三种情况： \( A,D,B,D,A,C \) 与 \( B,C \) 都不连边； 仅有一组连边; 或有两组连边,但 \( A,D \) 与 \( B,D \) 不同时连边, \( A,C \) 与 \( B,C \) 不同时连边均可.

故所求概率为

\[\frac{1}{2} \times  \frac{1}{2} \times  \left\lbrack  {{\left( \frac{1}{2}\right) }^{4} + {\mathrm{C}}_{4}^{1} \times  {\left( \frac{1}{2}\right) }^{4} + {\mathrm{C}}_{2}^{1} \times  {\mathrm{C}}_{2}^{1} \times  {\left( \frac{1}{2}\right) }^{4}}\right\rbrack   = \frac{9}{64}.\]

② 若 \( C,D \) 连边,也有三种情况： \( A,D,B,D,A,C,B,C \) 全不连边；或只有一组连边,或有两组连边,但两组连边为 \( {AD},{AC} \) 或 \( {BC},{BD} \) . 所求概率为

\[\frac{1}{2} \times  \frac{1}{2} \times  \left\lbrack  {\frac{1}{16} + {\mathrm{C}}_{4}^{3} \times  {\left( \frac{1}{2}\right) }^{4} + 2 \times  {\left( \frac{1}{2}\right) }^{4}}\right\rbrack   = \frac{7}{64}.\]


从而 \( A,B \) 不能用折线连接的概率为

\[\frac{9}{64} + \frac{7}{64} = \frac{1}{4}\]

所求概率为 \( 1 - \frac{1}{4} = \frac{3}{4} \) .

## 二、 解答题：本大题共 3 小题,满分 56 分. 解答应写出文字说明、证明过程或演算步骤. 其 中第 9 题满分 16 分, 第 10、11 题满分 20 分.

9. 平面直角坐标系中 \( {xOy} \) 中, \( P \) 是不在 \( x \) 轴上的一个动点,过 \( P \) 作抛物线 \( {y}^{2} = {4x} \) 的两条切线,切点设为 \( A,B \) ,且直线 \( {PO} \bot  {AB} \) 于 \( Q,R \) 为直线 \( {AB} \) 与 \( x \) 轴的交点.

<!-- Media -->

<!-- figureText: \( y \) \( B \) \( x \) \( P \) 0 \( A \) -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/0198302e-eed8-722e-b9b7-e1386afb6727_183.jpg?x=719&y=713&w=276&h=325&r=0"/>

<!-- Media -->

(1)求证： \( R \) 是定点；

(2)求 \( \frac{PQ}{QR} \) 的最小值.

解析 (1)定点 \( R\left( {2,0}\right) \) ；

(2) \( 2\sqrt{2} \) .

(1)设 \( P\left( {m,n}\right) \) ,则 \( {AB} : {ny} = 2\left( {x + m}\right) \) ,根据题意,直线 \( {PO} \) 与直线 \( {AB} \) 垂直,于是

\[\frac{n}{m} \cdot  \frac{2}{n} =  - 1\]

因此 \( m =  - 2 \) . 进而 \( R\left( {2,0}\right) \) 为定点.

(2) 设直线 \( {AB} \) 的倾斜角为 \( \theta \) ,根据对称性,不妨设 \( \theta \) 为锐角. 过 \( P \) 作 \( x \) 轴的垂线,设垂足为 \( H \) ,则 \( \bigtriangleup {OPH} \) 与 \( \bigtriangleup {ORQ} \) 相似,于是

\[\frac{PQ}{QR} = \frac{{PO} + {OQ}}{QR} = \frac{\frac{2}{\sin \theta } + 2\sin \theta }{2\cos \theta } = \frac{3 - \cos {2\theta }}{\sin {2\theta }},\]

令右侧代数式为 \( t \) ,则

\[t\sin {2\theta } + \cos {2\theta } = 3,\]

于是

\[\sqrt{1 + {t}^{2}} \geq  3\]

解得 \( t \geq  2\sqrt{2} \) ,等号当 \( \theta  = \frac{1}{2}\arctan 2\sqrt{2} \) 时取得. 因此所求的最小值为 \( 2\sqrt{2} \) .


10. 数列 \( \left\{  {a}_{n}\right\} \) 满足 \( {a}_{1} = \frac{\pi }{6},{a}_{n + 1} = \arctan \left( {\sec {a}_{n}}\right) \left( {n \in  {\mathbb{N}}^{ * }}\right) \) . 求正整数 \( m \) ,使得

\[\sin {a}_{1} \cdot  \sin {a}_{2}\cdots \sin {a}_{m} = \frac{1}{100}.\]

解析 \( m = {3333} \) .

由已知条件可知,对任意正整数 \( n \) ,

\[{a}_{n + 1} \in  \left( {-\frac{\pi }{2},\frac{\pi }{2}}\right) \]

且

\[\tan {a}_{n + 1} = \sec {a}_{n},\]

①

由于 \( \sec {a}_{n} > 0 \) ,故

\[{a}_{n + 1} \in  \left( {0,\frac{\pi }{2}}\right) .\]

由 ① 得,

\[{\tan }^{2}{a}_{n + 1} = {\sec }^{2}{a}_{n} = 1 + {\tan }^{2}{a}_{n}\]

故

\[{\tan }^{2}{a}_{n} = n - 1 + {\tan }^{2}{a}_{1} = n - 1 + \frac{1}{3} = \frac{{3n} - 2}{3},\]

即

\[\tan {a}_{n} = \sqrt{\frac{{3n} - 2}{3}},\]

因此

\[\sin {a}_{1} \cdot  \sin {a}_{2}\cdots \sin {a}_{m} = \frac{\tan {a}_{1}}{\sec {a}_{1}} \cdot  \frac{\tan {a}_{2}}{\sec {a}_{2}}\cdots \frac{\tan {a}_{m}}{\sec {a}_{m}}\]

\[ = \frac{\tan {a}_{1}}{\tan {a}_{2}} \cdot  \frac{\tan {a}_{2}}{\tan {a}_{3}}\cdots \frac{\tan {a}_{m}}{\tan {a}_{m + 1}}\]

\[ = \frac{\tan {a}_{1}}{\tan {a}_{m + 1}} = \sqrt{\frac{1}{{3m} + 1}},\]

由

\[\sqrt{\frac{1}{{3m} + 1}} = \frac{1}{100}\]

得 \( m = {3333} \) .

11. 确定所有的复数 \( \alpha \) ,使得对任意复数 \( {z}_{1},{z}_{2},\left( {\left| {z}_{1}\right| ,\left| {z}_{2}\right|  < 1,{z}_{1} \neq  {z}_{2}}\right) \) ,均有

\[{\left( {z}_{1} + \alpha \right) }^{2} + \alpha \overline{{z}_{1}} \neq  {\left( {z}_{2} + \alpha \right) }^{2} + \alpha \overline{{z}_{2}}.\]

解析 \( \{ \alpha \left| {\alpha  \in  \mathbb{C},}\right| \alpha  \mid   \geq  2\} \) .

记 \( {f}_{\alpha }\left( z\right)  = {\left( z + \alpha \right) }^{2} + \alpha \bar{z} \) ,则

\[{f}_{\alpha }\left( {z}_{1}\right)  - {f}_{\alpha }\left( {z}_{2}\right)  = \left( {{z}_{1} + {z}_{2} + {2\alpha }}\right) \left( {{z}_{1} - {z}_{2}}\right)  + \alpha \left( {\overline{{z}_{1}} - \overline{{z}_{2}}}\right) .\]
